 nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam
 devīṃ sarasvatīṃ caiva tato jayam udīrayet
 janamejaya uvāca
a evaṃ nipātite karṇe samare savyasācinā
c alpāvaśiṣṭāḥ kuravaḥ kim akurvata vai dvija
a udīryamāṇaṃ ca balaṃ dṛṣṭvā rājā suyodhanaḥ
c pāṇḍavaiḥ prāptakālaṃ ca kiṃ prāpadyata kauravaḥ
a etad icchāmy ahaṃ śrotuṃ tad ācakṣva dvijottama
c na hi tṛpyāmi pūrveṣāṃ śṛṇvānaś caritaṃ mahat
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tataḥ karṇe hate rājan dhārtarāṣṭraḥ suyodhanaḥ
c bhṛśaṃ śokārṇave magno nirāśaḥ sarvato 'bhavat
a hā karṇa hā karṇa iti śocamānaḥ punaḥ punaḥ
c kṛcchrāt svaśibiraṃ prāyād dhataśeṣair nṛpaiḥ saha
a sa samāśvāsyamāno 'pi hetubhiḥ śāstraniścitaiḥ
c rājabhir nālabhac charma sūtaputravadhaṃ smaran
a sa daivaṃ balavan matvā bhavitavyaṃ ca pārthivaḥ
c saṃgrāme niścayaṃ kṛtvā punar yuddhāya niryayau
a śalyaṃ senāpatiṃ kṛtvā vidhivad rājapuṃgavaḥ
b madrarājaṃ puraskṛtya yuddhāyopajagāma ha
c raṇāya niryayau rājā hataśeṣair nṛpaiḥ saha
a tataḥ sutumulaṃ yuddhaṃ kurupāṇḍavasenayoḥ
c babhūva bharataśreṣṭha devāsuraraṇopamam
a tataḥ śalyo mahārāja kṛtvā kadanam āhave
c pāṇḍusainyasya madhyāhne dharmarājena pātitaḥ
a tato duryodhano rājā hatabandhū raṇājirāt
c apasṛtya hradaṃ ghoraṃ viveśa ripujād bhayāt
a athāparāhṇe tasyāhnaḥ parivārya mahārathaiḥ
b tathāparāhṇe tatrasthaṃ parivārya suyodhanam
c hradād āhūya yogena bhīmasenena pātitaḥ
a tasmin hate maheṣvāse hataśiṣṭās trayo rathāḥ
a   sānubandhe suyodhane
a kṛtavarmā kṛpo drauṇir
b suptaṃ śibiram āviśya dhṛṣṭadyumnapurogamān
c saṃrabhān niśi rājendra jaghnuḥ pāñcālasainikān
a tataḥ pūrvāhṇasamaye śibirād etya saṃjayaḥ
c praviveśa purīṃ dīno duḥkhaśokasamanvitaḥ
a praviśya ca puraṃ tūrṇaṃ bhujāv ucchritya duḥkhitaḥ
c vepamānas tato rājñaḥ praviveśa niveśanam
a ruroda ca naravyāghra hā rājann iti duḥkhitaḥ
c aho bata vivignāḥ sma nidhanena mahātmanaḥ
a aho subalavān kālo gatiś ca paramā tathā
b vidhis tu balavān atra pauruṣaṃ tu nirarthakam
c śakratulyabalāḥ sarve yatrāvadhyanta pārthivāḥ
a dṛṣṭvaiva ca puro rājañ janaḥ sarvaḥ sa saṃjayam
b kleśena mahatā yuktaḥ sarvato rājasattama
c praruroda bhṛśodvigno hā rājann iti sasvaram
a ākumāraṃ naravyāghra tat puraṃ vai samantataḥ
c ārtanādaṃ mahac cakre śrutvā vinihataṃ nṛpam
a dhāvataś cāpy apaśyac ca tatra trīn puruṣarṣabhān
c naṣṭacittān ivonmattāñ śokena bhṛśapīḍitān
d dṛṣṭvaiva ca narāñ śīghraṃ vyājahārātiduḥkhitaḥ
a tathā sa vihvalaḥ sūtaḥ praviśya nṛpatikṣayam
c dadarśa nṛpatiśreṣṭhaṃ prajñācakṣuṣam īśvaram
a dṛṣṭvā cāsīnam anaghaṃ samantāt parivāritam
c snuṣābhir bharataśreṣṭha gāndhāryā vidureṇa ca
a tathānyaiś ca suhṛdbhiś ca jñātibhiś ca hitaiṣibhiḥ
c tam eva cārthaṃ dhyāyantaṃ karṇasya nidhanaṃ prati
a rudann evābravīd vākyaṃ rājānaṃ janamejaya
c nātihṛṣṭamanāḥ sūto bāṣpasaṃdigdhayā girā
d uvāca bharataśreṣṭhaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ janādhipam
a saṃjayo 'haṃ naravyāghra namas te bharatarṣabha
c madrādhipo hataḥ śalyaḥ śakuniḥ saubalas tathā
e ulūkaḥ puruṣavyāghra kaitavyo dṛḍhavikramaḥ
a saṃśaptakā hatāḥ sarve kāmbojāś ca śakaiḥ saha
c mlecchāś ca pārvatīyāś ca yavanāś ca nipātitāḥ
a prācyā hatā mahārāja dākṣiṇātyāś ca sarvaśaḥ
c udīcyā nihatāḥ sarve pratīcyāś ca narādhipa
e rājāno rājaputrāś ca sarvato nihatā nṛpa
a duryodhano hato rājan yathoktaṃ pāṇḍavena ca
c bhagnasaktho mahārāja śete pāṃsuṣu rūṣitaḥ
d duryodhanasya bhīmena bhagnāv ūrū sutasya te
d sa bhūmau patitaḥ śete pāṃśubhiḥ pariguṇṭhitaḥ
a dhṛṣṭadyumno hato rājañ śikhaṇḍī cāparājitaḥ
c uttamaujā yudhāmanyus tathā rājan prabhadrakāḥ
a pāñcālāś ca naravyāghrāś cedayaś ca niṣūditāḥ
c tava putrā hatāḥ sarve draupadeyāś ca bhārata
e karṇaputro hataḥ śūro vṛṣaseno mahābalaḥ
a narā vinihatāḥ sarve gajāś ca vinipātitāḥ
c rathinaś ca naravyāghra hayāś ca nihatā yudhi
a kiṃciccheṣaṃ ca śibiraṃ tāvakānāṃ kṛtaṃ vibho
c pāṇḍavānāṃ ca śūrāṇāṃ samāsādya parasparam
a prāyaḥ strīśeṣam abhavaj jagat kālena mohitam
c sapta pāṇḍavataḥ śeṣā dhārtarāṣṭrās tathā trayaḥ
a te caiva bhrātaraḥ pañca vāsudevo 'tha sātyakiḥ
c kṛpaś ca kṛtavarmā ca drauṇiś ca jayatāṃ varaḥ
a tavāpy ete mahārāja rathino nṛpasattama
c akṣauhiṇīnāṃ sarvāsāṃ sametānāṃ janeśvara
e ete śeṣā mahārāja sarve 'nye nidhanaṃ gatāḥ
a kālena nihataṃ sarvaṃ jagad vai bharatarṣabha
c duryodhanaṃ vai purataḥ kṛtvā vairasya bhārata
a etac chrutvā vacaḥ krūraṃ dhṛtarāṣṭro janeśvaraḥ
c nipapāta mahārāja gatasattvo mahītale
a tasmin nipatite bhūmau viduro 'pi mahāyaśāḥ
c nipapāta mahārāja rājavyasanakarśitaḥ
a gāndhārī ca nṛpaśreṣṭha sarvāś ca kuruyoṣitaḥ
c patitāḥ sahasā bhūmau śrutvā krūraṃ vacaś ca tāḥ
a niḥsaṃjñaṃ patitaṃ bhūmau tadāsīd rājamaṇḍalam
c pralāpayuktā mahatī kathā nyastā paṭe yathā
a kṛcchreṇa tu tato rājā dhṛtarāṣṭro mahīpatiḥ
c śanair alabhata prāṇān putravyasanakarśitaḥ
a labdhvā tu sa nṛpaḥ saṃjñāṃ vepamānaḥ suduḥkhitaḥ
c udīkṣya ca diśaḥ sarvāḥ kṣattāraṃ vākyam abravīt
a vidvan kṣattar mahāprājña tvaṃ gatir bharatarṣabha
c mamānāthasya subhṛśaṃ putrair hīnasya sarvaśaḥ
e evam uktvā tato bhūyo visaṃjño nipapāta ha
a taṃ tathā patitaṃ dṛṣṭvā bāndhavā ye 'sya ke cana
c śītais tu siṣicus toyair vivyajur vyajanair api
a sa tu dīrgheṇa kālena pratyāśvasto mahīpatiḥ
c tūṣṇīṃ dadhyau mahīpālaḥ putravyasanakarśitaḥ
e niḥśvasañ jihmaga iva kumbhakṣipto viśāṃ pate
a saṃjayo 'py arudat tatra dṛṣṭvā rājānam āturam
c tathā sarvāḥ striyaś caiva gāndhārī ca yaśasvinī
a tato dīrgheṇa kālena viduraṃ vākyam abravīt
c dhṛtarāṣṭro naravyāghro muhyamāno muhur muhuḥ
a gacchantu yoṣitaḥ sarvā gāndhārī ca yaśasvinī
c tatheme suhṛdaḥ sarve bhraśyate me mano bhṛśam
a evam uktas tataḥ kṣattā tāḥ striyo bharatarṣabha
c visarjayām āsa śanair vepamānaḥ punaḥ punaḥ
a niścakramus tataḥ sarvās tāḥ striyo bharatarṣabha
c suhṛdaś ca tataḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā rājānam āturam
a tato narapatiṃ tatra labdhasaṃjñaṃ paraṃtapa
b gatir me ko bhaved adya iti cintāsamākulaḥ
c avekṣya saṃjayo dīno rodamānaṃ bhṛśāturam
a prāñjalir niḥśvasantaṃ ca taṃ narendraṃ muhur muhuḥ
b jñātīn striyo 'tha niryāpya praviśya viduraḥ punaḥ
b rājānaṃ śocamānas tu taṃ śocantaṃ muhur muhuḥ
c samāśvāsayata kṣattā vacasā madhureṇa ha
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a visṛṣṭāsv atha nārīṣu dhṛtarāṣṭro 'mbikāsutaḥ
c vilalāpa mahārāja duḥkhād duḥkhataraṃ gataḥ
a sadhūmam iva niḥśvasya karau dhunvan punaḥ punaḥ
c vicintya ca mahārāja tato vacanam abravīt
d yac chrutvā suhṛdāṃ cātikaruṇā samajāyata
a aho bata mahad duḥkhaṃ yad ahaṃ pāṇḍavān raṇe
c kṣemiṇaś cāvyayāṃś caiva tvattaḥ sūta śṛṇomi vai
a vajrasāramayaṃ nūnaṃ hṛdayaṃ sudṛḍhaṃ mama
c yac chrutvā nihatān putrān dīryate na sahasradhā
a cintayitvā vacas teṣāṃ bālakrīḍāṃ ca saṃjaya
c adya śrutvā hatān putrān bhṛśaṃ me dīryate manaḥ
a andhatvād yadi teṣāṃ tu na me rūpanidarśanam
c putrasnehakṛtā prītir nityam eteṣu dhāritā
a bālabhāvam atikrāntān yauvanasthāṃś ca tān aham
c madhyaprāptāṃs tathā śrutvā hṛṣṭa āsaṃ tathānagha
a tān adya nihatāñ śrutvā hṛtaiśvaryān hṛtaujasaḥ
c na labhe vai kva cic chāntiṃ putrādhibhir abhiplutaḥ
a ehy ehi putra rājendra mamānāthasya sāṃpratam
c tvayā hīno mahābāho kāṃ nu yāsyāmy ahaṃ gatim
a gatir bhūtvā mahārāja jñātīnāṃ suhṛdāṃ tathā
c andhaṃ vṛddhaṃ ca māṃ vīra vihāya kva nu gacchasi
a sā kṛpā sā ca te prītiḥ sā ca rājan sumānitā
c kathaṃ vinihataḥ pārthaiḥ saṃyugeṣv aparājitaḥ
a kathaṃ tvaṃ pṛthivīpālān bhuktvā tāta samāgatān
c śeṣe vinihato bhūmau prākṛtaḥ kunṛpo yathā
a ko nu mām utthitaṃ kālye tāta tāteti vakṣyati
c mahārājeti satataṃ lokanātheti cāsakṛt
a pariṣvajya ca māṃ kaṇṭhe snehenāklinnalocanaḥ
c anuśādhīti kauravya tat sādhu vada me vacaḥ
a nanu nāmāham aśrauṣaṃ vacanaṃ tava putraka
c bhūyasī mama pṛthvīyaṃ yathā pārthasya no tathā
a bhagadattaḥ kṛpaḥ śalya āvantyo 'tha jayadrathaḥ
c bhūriśravāḥ somadatto mahārājo 'tha bāhlikaḥ
a aśvatthāmā ca bhojaś ca māgadhaś ca mahābalaḥ
c bṛhadbalaś ca kāśīśaḥ śakuniś cāpi saubalaḥ
a mlecchāś ca bahusāhasrāḥ śakāś ca yavanaiḥ saha
c sudakṣiṇaś ca kāmbojas trigartādhipatis tathā
a bhīṣmaḥ pitāmahaś caiva bhāradvājo 'tha gautamaḥ
c śrutāyuś cācyutāyuś ca śatāyuś cāpi vīryavān
a jalasaṃdho 'thārśyaśṛṅgī rākṣasaś cāpy alāyudhaḥ
c alaṃbuso mahābāhuḥ subāhuś ca mahārathaḥ
a ete cānye ca bahavo rājāno rājasattama
c madartham udyatāḥ sarve prāṇāṃs tyaktvā raṇe prabho
a yeṣāṃ madhye sthito yuddhe bhrātṛbhiḥ parivāritaḥ
c yodhayiṣyāmy ahaṃ pārthān pāñcālāṃś caiva sarvaśaḥ
a cedīṃś ca nṛpaśārdūla draupadeyāṃś ca saṃyuge
c sātyakiṃ kuntibhojaṃ ca rākṣasaṃ ca ghaṭotkacam
a eko 'py eṣāṃ mahārāja samarthaḥ saṃnivāraṇe
c samare pāṇḍaveyānāṃ saṃkruddho hy abhidhāvatām
e kiṃ punaḥ sahitā vīrāḥ kṛtavairāś ca pāṇḍavaiḥ
a atha vā sarva evaite pāṇḍavasyānuyāyibhiḥ
c yotsyanti saha rājendra haniṣyanti ca tān mṛdhe
a karṇas tv eko mayā sārdhaṃ nihaniṣyati pāṇḍavān
c tato nṛpatayo vīrāḥ sthāsyanti mama śāsane
a yaś ca teṣāṃ praṇetā vai vāsudevo mahābalaḥ
c na sa saṃnahyate rājann iti mām abravīd vacaḥ
a tasyāhaṃ vadataḥ sūta bahuśo mama saṃnidhau
c yuktito hy anupaśyāmi nihatān pāṇḍavān mṛdhe
a teṣāṃ madhye sthitā yatra hanyante mama putrakāḥ
c vyāyacchamānāḥ samare kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥ
a bhīṣmaś ca nihato yatra lokanāthaḥ pratāpavān
c śikhaṇḍinaṃ samāsādya mṛgendra iva jambukam
a droṇaś ca brāhmaṇo yatra sarvaśastrāstrapāragaḥ
c nihataḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saṃkhye kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥ
d karṇaś ca nihataḥ saṃkhye divyāstrajño mahābalaḥ
a bhūriśravā hato yatra somadattaś ca saṃyuge
c bāhlīkaś ca mahārāja kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥ
d bhagadatto hato yatra gajayuddhaviśāradaḥ
d jayadrathaś ca nihataḥ kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥ
a sudakṣiṇo hato yatra jalasaṃdhaś ca kauravaḥ
c śrutāyuś cācyutāyuś ca kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥ
d mahābalas tathā pāṇḍyaḥ sarvaśastrāstrapāragaḥ
d nihataḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saṃkhye kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥ
a bṛhadbalo hato yatra māgadhaś ca mahābalaḥ
b ugrāyudhaś ca vikrāntaḥ pratimānaṃ dhanuṣmatām
b śatāyuś caiva vikrāntaḥ kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥ
c āvantyo nihato yatra trigartaś ca janādhipaḥ
e saṃśaptakāś ca bahavaḥ kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥ
f   śakuniś cāpi saubalaḥ
f trigartaś ca mahābāhuḥ saṃśaptāś ca mahābalāḥ
f yatra śūrā maheṣvāsā madarthe tyaktajīvitāḥ
f nihatā bhīmasenena kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥ
a alaṃbusas tathā rājan rākṣasaś cāpy alāyudhaḥ
c ārśyaśṛṅgaś ca nihataḥ kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥ
a nārāyaṇā hatā yatra gopālā yuddhadurmadāḥ
c mlecchāś ca bahusāhasrāḥ kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥ
a śakuniḥ saubalo yatra kaitavyaś ca mahābalaḥ
c nihataḥ sabalo vīraḥ kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥ
d ete cānye ca bahavaḥ kṛtāstrā yuddhadurmadāḥ
a rājāno rājaputrāś ca śūrāḥ parighabāhavaḥ
c nihatā bahavo yatra kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥ
d yatra śūrā maheṣvāsāḥ kṛtāstrā yuddhadurmadāḥ
d yatra śūrā mahātmānaḥ sarvaśāstrāstrapāragāḥ
d bahavo nihatāḥ sūta mahendrasamavikramāḥ
a nānādeśasamāvṛttāḥ kṣatriyā yatra saṃjaya
c nihatāḥ samare sarve kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥ
a putrāś ca me vinihatāḥ pautrāś caiva mahābalāḥ
b duryodhano hato yatra putraś cāsya mahātmanaḥ
c vayasyā bhrātaraś caiva kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥ
d pārthena saṃyuge ghore kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥ
a bhāgadheyasamāyukto dhruvam utpadyate naraḥ
c yaś ca bhāgyasamāyuktaḥ sa śubhaṃ prāpnuyān naraḥ
a ahaṃ viyuktaḥ svair bhāgyaiḥ putraiś caiveha saṃjaya
c katham adya bhaviṣyāmi vṛddhaḥ śatruvaśaṃ gataḥ
a nānyad atra paraṃ manye vanavāsād ṛte prabho
c so 'haṃ vanaṃ gamiṣyāmi nirbandhur jñātisaṃkṣaye
a na hi me 'nyad bhavec chreyo vanābhyupagamād ṛte
c imām avasthāṃ prāptasya lūnapakṣasya saṃjaya
a duryodhano hato yatra śalyaś ca nihato yudhi
c duḥśāsano viśastaś ca vikarṇaś ca mahābalaḥ
a kathaṃ hi bhīmasenasya śroṣye 'haṃ śabdam uttamam
c ekena samare yena hataṃ putraśataṃ mama
a asakṛd vadatas tasya duryodhanavadhena ca
c duḥkhaśokābhisaṃtapto na śroṣye paruṣā giraḥ
a evaṃ sa śokasaṃtaptaḥ pārthivo hatabāndhavaḥ
c muhur muhur muhyamānaḥ putrādhibhir abhiplutaḥ
a vilapya suciraṃ kālaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭro 'mbikāsutaḥ
c dīrgham uṣṇaṃ ca niḥśvasya cintayitvā parābhavam
a duḥkhena mahatā rājā saṃtapto bharatarṣabha
c punar gāvalgaṇiṃ sūtaṃ paryapṛcchad yathātatham
a bhīṣmadroṇau hatau śrutvā sūtaputraṃ ca pātitam
c senāpatiṃ praṇetāraṃ kim akurvata māmakāḥ
d tathā śalyaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ madrāṇām īśvaraṃ vibhum
a yaṃ yaṃ senāpraṇetāraṃ yudhi kurvanti māmakāḥ
c acireṇaiva kālena taṃ taṃ nighnanti pāṇḍavāḥ
a raṇamūrdhni hato bhīṣmaḥ paśyatāṃ vaḥ kirīṭinā
c evam eva hato droṇaḥ sarveṣām eva paśyatām
a evam eva hataḥ karṇaḥ sūtaputraḥ pratāpavān
c sa rājakānāṃ sarveṣāṃ paśyatāṃ vaḥ kirīṭinā
a pūrvam evāham ukto vai vidureṇa mahātmanā
c duryodhanāparādhena prajeyaṃ vinaśiṣyati
a ke cin na samyak paśyanti mūḍhāḥ samyak tathāpare
c tad idaṃ mama mūḍhasya tathābhūtaṃ vacaḥ sma ha
a yad abravīn me dharmātmā viduro dīrghadarśivān
c tat tathā samanuprāptaṃ vacanaṃ satyavādinaḥ
a daivopahatacittena yan mayāpakṛtaṃ purā
c anayasya phalaṃ tasya brūhi gāvalgaṇe punaḥ
a ko vā mukham anīkānām āsīt karṇe nipātite
c arjunaṃ vāsudevaṃ ca ko vā pratyudyayau rathī
a ke 'rakṣan dakṣiṇaṃ cakraṃ madrarājasya saṃyuge
c vāmaṃ ca yoddhukāmasya ke vā vīrasya pṛṣṭhataḥ
a kathaṃ ca vaḥ sametānāṃ madrarājo mahābalaḥ
c nihataḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saṃkhye putro vā mama saṃjaya
a brūhi sarvaṃ yathātattvaṃ bharatānāṃ mahākṣayam
c yathā ca nihataḥ saṃkhye putro duryodhano mama
a pāñcālāś ca yathā sarve nihatāḥ sapadānugāḥ
c dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca draupadyāḥ pañca cātmajāḥ
a pāṇḍavāś ca yathā muktās tathobhau sātvatau yudhi
c kṛpaś ca kṛtavarmā ca bhāradvājasya cātmajaḥ
a yad yathā yādṛśaṃ caiva yuddhaṃ vṛttaṃ ca sāṃpratam
c akhilaṃ śrotum icchāmi kuśalo hy asi saṃjaya
 saṃjaya uvāca
a śṛṇu rājann avahito yathā vṛtto mahān kṣayaḥ
c kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca samāsādya parasparam
a nihate sūtaputre tu pāṇḍavena mahātmanā
c vidruteṣu ca sainyeṣu samānīteṣu cāsakṛt
d ghore manuṣyadehānām ājau gajavarakṣaye
d yat tat karṇe hate pārthaḥ siṃhanādam athākarot
d tadā tava sutān rājan prāviśat sumahad bhayam
d na saṃdhātum anīkāni na caivātha parākrame
d āsīd buddhir hate karṇe tava yodhasya kasya cit
d vaṇijo nāvi bhinnāyām agādhe viplavā iva
d apāre pāram icchanto hate dvīpe kirīṭinā
d sūtaputre hate rājan vitrastāḥ śaravikṣatāḥ
d anāthā nātham icchanto mṛgāḥ siṃhārditā iva
d bhagnaśṛṅgā iva vṛṣāḥ śīrṇadaṃṣṭrā ivoragāḥ
d pratyupāyāma sāyāhne nirjitāḥ savyasācinā
d hatapravīrā vidhvastā nikṛttā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
d sūtaputre hate rājan putrās te prādravan bhayāt
d viśastrakavacāḥ sarve kāṃdiśīkā vicetasaḥ
d anyonyam abhinighnanto vīkṣamāṇā bhayārditāḥ
d mām eva nūnaṃ bībhatsur mām eva ca vṛkodaraḥ
d abhiyātīti manvānāḥ petur mamluś ca bhārata
d hayān anye gajān anye rathān anye mahārathāḥ
d āruhya javasaṃpannān pādātān prajahur bhayāt
d kuñjaraiḥ syandanā bhagnāḥ sādinaś ca mahārathaiḥ
d padātisaṃghāś cāśvaughaiḥ palāyadbhir bhṛśaṃ hatāḥ
d vyālataskarasaṃkīrṇe sārthahīnā yathā vane
d tathā tvadīyā nihate sūtaputre tadābhavan
d hatārohās tathā nāgāś chinnahastās tathāpare
d sarvaṃ pārthamayaṃ lokam apaśyan vai bhayārditāḥ
d tān prekṣya dravataḥ sarvān bhīmasenabhayārditān
d duryodhano 'tha svaṃ sūtaṃ hāhākṛtvedam abravīt
d nātikramiṣyate pārtho dhanuṣpāṇim avasthitam
d jaghane yudhyamānaṃ māṃ tūrṇam aśvān pracodaya
d samare yudhyamānaṃ hi kaunteyo māṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ
d notsahetābhyatikrāntuṃ velām iva mahārṇavaḥ
d adyārjunaṃ sagovindaṃ māninaṃ ca vṛkodaram
d nihatya śiṣṭāñ śatrūṃś ca karṇasyānṛṇyam āpnuyām
d tac chrutvā kururājasya śūrāryasadṛśaṃ vacaḥ
d sūto hemaparicchannāñ śanair aśvān acodayat
d gajāśvarathahīnās tu pādātāś caiva māriṣa
d pañcaviṃśatisāhasrāḥ prādravañ śanakair iva
d tān bhīmasenaḥ saṃkruddho dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥ
d balena caturaṅgeṇa parikṣipyāhanac charaiḥ
d pratyayudhyanta te sarve bhīmasenaṃ sapārṣatam
d pārthapārṣatayoś cānye jagṛhus tatra nāmanī
d akrudhyata raṇe bhīmas tair mṛdhe pratyavasthitaiḥ
d so 'vatīrya rathāt tūrṇaṃ gadāpāṇir ayudhyata
d na tān rathastho bhūmiṣṭhān dharmāpekṣī vṛkodaraḥ
d yodhayām āsa kaunteyo bhujavīryaṃ samāśritaḥ
d jātarūpaparicchannāṃ pragṛhya mahatīṃ gadām
d nyavadhīt tāvakān sarvān daṇḍapāṇir ivāntakaḥ
d padātayo hi saṃrabdhās tyaktajīvitabāndhavāḥ
d bhīmam abhyadravan saṃkhye pataṃgā jvalanaṃ yathā
d āsādya bhīmasenaṃ te saṃrabdhā yuddhadurmadāḥ
d vineśuḥ sahasā dṛṣṭvā bhūtagrāmā ivāntakam
d śyenavad vyacarad bhīmaḥ khaḍgena gadayā tathā
d pañcaviṃśatisāhasrāṃs tāvakānām apothayat
d hatvā tat puruṣānīkaṃ bhīmaḥ satyaparākramaḥ
d dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ puraskṛtya punas tasthau mahābalaḥ
d dhanaṃjayo rathānīkam anvapadyata vīryavān
d mādrīputrau ca śakuniṃ sātyakiś ca mahābalaḥ
d javenābhyapatan hṛṣṭā ghnanto dauryodhanaṃ balam
d tasyāśvavārān subahūṃs te nihatya śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
d tam anvadhāvaṃs tvaritās tatra yuddham avartata
d tato dhanaṃjayo rājan rathānīkam agāhata
d viśrutaṃ triṣu lokeṣu gāṇḍīvaṃ vyākṣipan dhanuḥ
d kṛṣṇasārathim āyāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā śvetahayaṃ ratham
d arjunaṃ cāpi yoddhāraṃ tvadīyāḥ prādravan bhayāt
d viprahīnarathāśvāś ca śaraiś ca parivāritāḥ
d pañcaviṃśatisāhasrāḥ pārtham ārchan padātayaḥ
d hatvā tat puruṣānīkaṃ pāñcālānāṃ mahārathaḥ
d bhīmasenaṃ puraskṛtya na cirāt pratyadṛśyata
d mahādhanurdharaḥ śrīmān amitragaṇamardanaḥ
d putraḥ pāñcālarājasya dhṛṣṭadyumno mahāyaśāḥ
d pārāvatasavarṇāśvaṃ kovidāravaradhvajam
d dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ raṇe dṛṣṭvā tvadīyāḥ prādravan bhayāt
d gāndhārarājaṃ śīghrāstram anusṛtya yaśasvinau
d nacirāt pratyadṛśyetāṃ mādrīputrau sasātyakī
d cekitānaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca draupadeyāś ca māriṣa
d hatvā tvadīyaṃ sumahat sainyaṃ śaṅkhān athādhaman
d te sarve tāvakān prekṣya dravato vai parāṅmukhān
d abhyadhāvanta nighnanto vṛṣāñ jitvā vṛṣā iva
d senāvaśeṣaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā tava putrasya pāṇḍavaḥ
d vyavasthitaṃ savyasācī cukrodha balavan nṛpa
d tata enaṃ śarai rājan sahasā samavākirat
d rajasā codgatenātha na sma kiṃ cana dṛśyate
d andhakārīkṛte loke śarībhūte mahītale
d diśaḥ sarvā mahārāja tāvakāḥ prādravan bhayāt
d bhajyamāneṣu sainyeṣu kururājo viśāṃ pate
d pareṣām ātmanaś caiva samantāt samupādravat
d tato duryodhanaḥ sarvān ājuhāvātha pāṇḍavān
d yuddhāya bharataśreṣṭha devān iva purā baliḥ
d ta enam abhigarjantaṃ sahitāḥ samupādravan
d nānāśastrasṛjaḥ kruddhā bhartsayanto muhur muhuḥ
d duryodhano 'py asaṃbhrāntas tān arīn vyadhamac charaiḥ
d tatrādbhutam apaśyāma tava putrasya pauruṣam
d yad enaṃ pāṇḍavāḥ sarve na śekur ativartitum
d nātidūrāpayātaṃ tu kṛtabuddhiṃ palāyane
d duryodhanaḥ svakaṃ sainyam apaśyad bhṛśavikṣatam
d tato 'vasthāpya rājendra kṛtabuddhis tavātmajaḥ
d harṣayann iva tān yodhān idaṃ vacanam abravīt
d na taṃ deśaṃ prapaśyāmi pṛthivyāṃ parvateṣu ca
d yatra yātān na vo hanyuḥ pāṇḍavāḥ kiṃ sṛtena vaḥ
d svalpaṃ caiva balaṃ teṣāṃ kṛṣṇau ca bhṛśavikṣatau
d yadi sarve 'tra tiṣṭhāmo dhruvo no vijayo bhavet
d viprayātāṃs tu vo bhinnān pāṇḍavāḥ kṛtakilbiṣān
d anusṛtya haniṣyanti śreyo naḥ samare vadhaḥ
d sukhaḥ sāṃgrāmiko mṛtyuḥ kṣatradharmeṇa yudhyataḥ
d mṛto duḥkhaṃ na jānīte pretya cānantyam aśnute
d śṛṇvantu kṣatriyāḥ sarve yāvanto vai samāgatāḥ
d dviṣato bhīmasenasya kruddhasya vaśam eṣy atha
d pitāmahair ācaritaṃ na dharmaṃ hātum arhatha
d na hi karmāsti pāpīyaḥ kṣatriyasya palāyanāt
d na yuddhadharmāc chreyān hi panthāḥ svargasya kauravāḥ
d sucireṇārjitāṃl lokān sadyo yodhaḥ samaśnute
d tasya tad vacanaṃ rājñaḥ pūjayitvā mahārathāḥ
d punar evābhyavartanta kṣatriyāḥ pāṇḍavān prati
d parājayam amṛṣyantaḥ kṛtacittāś ca vikrame
d tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ punar eva sudāruṇam
d tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca devāsuraraṇopamam
d yudhiṣṭhirapurogāṃś ca sarvasainyena pāṇḍavān
d anvadhāvan mahārāja putro duryodhanas tava
a vimukhe tava putre tu śokopahatacetasi
b pātiteṣu turaṃgeṣu gajeṣu ca ratheṣu ca
c bhṛśodvigneṣu sainyeṣu dṛṣṭvā pārthasya vikramam
a dhyāyamāneṣu sainyeṣu duḥkhaṃ prāpteṣu bhārata
c balānāṃ mathyamānānāṃ śrutvā ninadam uttamam
a abhijñānaṃ narendrāṇāṃ vikṛtaṃ prekṣya saṃyuge
c patitān rathanīḍāṃś ca rathāṃś cāpi mahātmanām
a raṇe vinihatān nāgān dṛṣṭvā pattīṃś ca māriṣa
c āyodhanaṃ cātighoraṃ rudrasyākrīḍasaṃnibham
a aprakhyātiṃ gatānāṃ tu rājñāṃ śatasahasraśaḥ
c kṛpāviṣṭaḥ kṛpo rājan vayaḥśīlasamanvitaḥ
a abravīt tatra tejasvī so 'bhisṛtya janādhipam
c duryodhanaṃ manyuvaśād vacanaṃ vacanakṣamaḥ
a duryodhana nibodhedaṃ yat tvā vakṣyāmi kaurava
c śrutvā kuru mahārāja yadi te rocate 'nagha
a na yuddhadharmāc chreyān vai panthā rājendra vidyate
c yaṃ samāśritya yudhyante kṣatriyāḥ kṣatriyarṣabha
a putro bhrātā pitā caiva svasreyo mātulas tathā
c saṃbandhibāndhavāś caiva yodhyā vai kṣatrajīvinā
a vadhe caiva paro dharmas tathādharmaḥ palāyane
c te sma ghorāṃ samāpannā jīvikāṃ jīvitārthinaḥ
a tatra tvāṃ prativakṣyāmi kiṃ cid eva hitaṃ vacaḥ
c hate bhīṣme ca droṇe ca karṇe caiva mahārathe
a jayadrathe ca nihate tava bhrātṛṣu cānagha
c lakṣmaṇe tava putre ca kiṃ śeṣaṃ paryupāsmahe
a yeṣu bhāraṃ samāsajya rājye matim akurmahi
c te saṃtyajya tanūr yātāḥ śūrā brahmavidāṃ gatim
a vayaṃ tv iha vinābhūtā guṇavadbhir mahārathaiḥ
c kṛpaṇaṃ vartayiṣyāma pātayitvā nṛpān bahūn
a sarvair api ca jīvadbhir bībhatsur aparājitaḥ
c kṛṣṇanetro mahābāhur devair api durāsadaḥ
a indrakārmukavajrābham indraketum ivocchritam
c vānaraṃ ketum āsādya saṃcacāla mahācamūḥ
a siṃhanādena bhīmasya pāñcajanyasvanena ca
c gāṇḍīvasya ca nirghoṣāt saṃhṛṣyanti manāṃsi naḥ
a carantīva mahāvidyun muṣṇanti nayanaprabhām
c alātam iva cāviddhaṃ gāṇḍīvaṃ samadṛśyata
a jāmbūnadavicitraṃ ca dhūyamānaṃ mahad dhanuḥ
c dṛśyate dikṣu sarvāsu vidyud abhraghaneṣv iva
d śvetāś ca vegasaṃpannāḥ śaśikāśasamaprabhāḥ
d pibanta iva cākāśaṃ rathe yuktās tu vājinaḥ
a uhyamānaś ca kṛṣṇena vāyuneva balāhakaḥ
b jāmbūnadavicitrāṅgā vahante cārjunaṃ raṇe
c tāvakaṃ tad balaṃ rājann arjuno 'stravidāṃ varaḥ
e gahanaṃ śiśire kakṣaṃ dadāhāgnir ivotthitaḥ
a gāhamānam anīkāni mahendrasadṛśaprabham
c dhanaṃjayam apaśyāma caturdantam iva dvipam
a vikṣobhayantaṃ senāṃ te trāsayantaṃ ca pārthivān
c dhanaṃjayam apaśyāma nalinīm iva kuñjaram
a trāsayantaṃ tathā yodhān dhanur ghoṣeṇa pāṇḍavam
c bhūya enam apaśyāma siṃhaṃ mṛgagaṇā iva
a sarvalokamaheṣvāsau vṛṣabhau sarvadhanvinām
c āmuktakavacau kṛṣṇau lokamadhye virejatuḥ
a adya saptadaśāhāni vartamānasya bhārata
c saṃgrāmasyātighorasya vadhyatāṃ cābhito yudhi
a vāyuneva vidhūtāni tavānīkāni sarvaśaḥ
c śaradambhodajālāni vyaśīryanta samantataḥ
a tāṃ nāvam iva paryastāṃ bhrāntavātāṃ mahārṇave
c tava senāṃ mahārāja savyasācī vyakampayat
a kva nu te sūtaputro 'bhūt kva nu droṇaḥ sahānugaḥ
c ahaṃ kva ca kva cātmā te hārdikyaś ca tathā kva nu
e duḥśāsanaś ca bhrātā te bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitaḥ kva nu
a bāṇagocarasaṃprāptaṃ prekṣya caiva jayadratham
c saṃbandhinas te bhrātṝṃś ca sahāyān mātulāṃs tathā
a sarvān vikramya miṣato lokāṃś cākramya mūrdhani
c jayadratho hato rājan kiṃ nu śeṣam upāsmahe
a ko veha sa pumān asti yo vijeṣyati pāṇḍavam
b asti kaḥ puruṣaś cādya yo jeṣyati dhanaṃjayam
c tasya cāstrāṇi divyāni vividhāni mahātmanaḥ
e gāṇḍīvasya ca nirghoṣo vīryāṇi harate hi naḥ
a naṣṭacandrā yathā rātriḥ seneyaṃ hatanāyakā
a   kāminī ca mṛtapriyā
c nāgabhagnadrumā śuṣkā nadīvākulatāṃ gatā
d yathā nadī śuṣkajalā senā karṇaṃ vinā tathā
a dhvajinyāṃ hatanetrāyāṃ yatheṣṭaṃ śvetavāhanaḥ
c cariṣyati mahābāhuḥ kakṣe 'gnir iva saṃjvalan
a sātyakeś caiva yo vego bhīmasenasya cobhayoḥ
c dārayeta girīn sarvāñ śoṣayeta ca sāgarān
a uvāca vākyaṃ yad bhīmaḥ sabhāmadhye viśāṃ pate
c kṛtaṃ tat sakalaṃ tena bhūyaś caiva kariṣyati
a pramukhasthe tadā karṇe balaṃ pāṇḍavarakṣitam
c durāsadaṃ tathā guptaṃ gūḍhaṃ gāṇḍīvadhanvanā
a yuṣmābhis tāni cīrṇāni yāny asādhūni sādhuṣu
c akāraṇakṛtāny eva teṣāṃ vaḥ phalam āgatam
a ātmano 'rthe tvayā loko yatnataḥ sarva āhṛtaḥ
c sa te saṃśayitas tāta ātmā ca bharatarṣabha
a rakṣa duryodhanātmānam ātmā sarvasya bhājanam
c bhinne hi bhājane tāta diśo gacchati tadgatam
a hīyamānena vai saṃdhiḥ paryeṣṭavyaḥ samena ca
c vigraho vardhamānena nītir eṣā bṛhaspateḥ
a te vayaṃ pāṇḍuputrebhyo hīnāḥ svabalaśaktitaḥ
c atra te pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdhaṃ saṃdhiṃ manye kṣamaṃ prabho
a na jānīte hi yaḥ śreyaḥ śreyasaś cāvamanyate
c sa kṣipraṃ bhraśyate rājyān na ca śreyo 'nuvindati
a praṇipatya hi rājānaṃ rājyaṃ yadi labhemahi
c śreyaḥ syān na tu mauḍhyena rājan gantuṃ parābhavam
a vaicitravīryavacanāt kṛpāśīlo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c viniyuñjīta rājye tvāṃ govindavacanena ca
d ajātaśatruḥ kauravyo guruśuśrūṣaṇe rataḥ
d dhṛtarāṣṭrasya vacanaṃ nāvamaṃsyati dhārmikaḥ
d kurvanti bhrātaraś cāsya vacanaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ
a yad brūyād dhi hṛṣīkeśo rājānam aparājitam
c arjunaṃ bhīmasenaṃ ca sarvaṃ kuryur asaṃśayam
a nātikramiṣyate kṛṣṇo vacanaṃ kauravasya ha
c dhṛtarāṣṭrasya manye 'haṃ nāpi kṛṣṇasya pāṇḍavaḥ
a etat kṣamam ahaṃ manye tava pārthair avigraham
c na tvā bravīmi kārpaṇyān na prāṇaparirakṣaṇāt
e pathyaṃ rājan bravīmi tvāṃ tat parāsuḥ smariṣyasi
a iti vṛddho vilapyaitat kṛpaḥ śāradvato vacaḥ
c dīrgham uṣṇaṃ ca niḥśvasya śuśoca ca mumoha ca
 saṃjaya uvāca
a evam uktas tato rājā gautamena yaśasvinā
c niḥśvasya dīrgham uṣṇaṃ ca tūṣṇīm āsīd viśāṃ pate
a tato muhūrtaṃ sa dhyātvā dhārtarāṣṭro mahāmanāḥ
c kṛpaṃ śāradvataṃ vākyam ity uvāca paraṃtapaḥ
a yat kiṃ cit suhṛdā vācyaṃ tat sarvaṃ śrāvito hy aham
c kṛtaṃ ca bhavatā sarvaṃ prāṇān saṃtyajya yudhyatā
a gāhamānam anīkāni yudhyamānaṃ mahārathaiḥ
c pāṇḍavair atitejobhir lokas tvām anudṛṣṭavān
a suhṛdā yad idaṃ vācyaṃ bhavatā śrāvito hy aham
c na māṃ prīṇāti tat sarvaṃ mumūrṣor iva bheṣajam
a hetukāraṇasaṃyuktaṃ hitaṃ vacanam uttamam
c ucyamānaṃ mahābāho na me viprāgrya rocate
a rājyād vinikṛto 'smābhiḥ kathaṃ so 'smāsu viśvaset
c akṣadyūte ca nṛpatir jito 'smābhir mahādhanaḥ
e sa kathaṃ mama vākyāni śraddadhyād bhūya eva tu
a tathā dautyena saṃprāptaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ pārthahite rataḥ
c pralabdhaś ca hṛṣīkeśas tac ca karma virodhitam
e sa ca me vacanaṃ brahman katham evābhimaṃsyate
a vilalāpa hi yat kṛṣṇā sabhāmadhye sameyuṣī
c na tan marṣayate kṛṣṇo na rājyaharaṇaṃ tathā
a ekaprāṇāv ubhau kṛṣṇāv anyonyaṃ prati saṃhatau
c purā yac chrutam evāsīd adya paśyāmi tat prabho
a svasrīyaṃ ca hataṃ śrutvā duḥkhaṃ svapiti keśavaḥ
c kṛtāgaso vayaṃ tasya sa madarthaṃ kathaṃ kṣamet
a abhimanyor vināśena na śarma labhate 'rjunaḥ
c sa kathaṃ maddhite yatnaṃ prakariṣyati yācitaḥ
a madhyamaḥ pāṇḍavas tīkṣṇo bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
c pratijñātaṃ ca tenograṃ sa bhajyeta na saṃnamet
d sa haniṣyati māṃ rudrahastenāpi hi rakṣitam
a ubhau tau baddhanistriṃśāv ubhau cābaddhakaṅkaṭau
c kṛtavairāv ubhau vīrau yamāv api yamopamau
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca kṛtavairau mayā saha
c tau kathaṃ maddhite yatnaṃ prakuryātāṃ dvijottama
a duḥśāsanena yat kṛṣṇā ekavastrā rajasvalā
c parikliṣṭā sabhāmadhye sarvalokasya paśyataḥ
a tathā vivasanāṃ dīnāṃ smaranty adyāpi pāṇḍavāḥ
b kṛṣṇaḥ pratyaham evedaṃ vakti nāśe mamoditaḥ
b teṣu jīvatsu pārtheṣu tasmiñ jīvati keśave
b vināśam eva yāsyāmi svapāpenaiva sānujaḥ
c na nivārayituṃ śakyāḥ saṃgrāmāt te paraṃtapāḥ
a yadā ca draupadī kṛṣṇā madvināśāya duḥkhitā
c ugraṃ tepe tapaḥ kṛṣṇā bhartṝṇām arthasiddhaye
e sthaṇḍile nityadā śete yāvad vairasya yātanā
a nikṣipya mānaṃ darpaṃ ca vāsudevasahodarā

a iti sarvaṃ samunnaddhaṃ na nirvāti kathaṃ cana
c abhimanyor vināśena sa saṃdheyaḥ kathaṃ mayā
a kathaṃ ca nāma bhuktvemāṃ pṛthivīṃ sāgarāmbarām

a upary upari rājñāṃ vai jvalito bhāskaro yathā
c yudhiṣṭhiraṃ kathaṃ paścād anuyāsyāmi dāsavat
a kathaṃ bhuktvā svayaṃ bhogān dattvā dāyāṃś ca puṣkalān
c kṛpaṇaṃ vartayiṣyāmi kṛpaṇaiḥ saha jīvikām

c na tu saṃdhim ahaṃ manye prāptakālaṃ kathaṃ cana

c nāyaṃ klībayituṃ kālaḥ saṃyoddhuṃ kāla eva naḥ
a iṣṭaṃ me bahubhir yajñair dattā vipreṣu dakṣiṇāḥ
c prāptāḥ kramaśrutā vedāḥ śatrūṇāṃ mūrdhni ca sthitam

b notsahe 'dya dvijaśreṣṭha pāṇḍavān vaktum īdṛśam
c yātāni pararāṣṭrāṇi svarāṣṭram anupālitam
a bhuktāś ca vividhā bhogās trivargaḥ sevito mayā
c pitṝṇāṃ gatam ānṛṇyaṃ kṣatradharmasya cobhayoḥ
a na dhruvaṃ sukham astīha kuto rājyaṃ kuto yaśaḥ
c iha kīrtir vidhātavyā sā ca yuddhena nānyathā

c adharmaḥ sumahān eṣa yac chayyāmaraṇaṃ gṛhe
a araṇye yo vimuñceta saṃgrāme vā tanuṃ naraḥ
c kratūn āhṛtya mahato mahimānaṃ sa gacchati
a kṛpaṇaṃ vilapann ārto jarayābhipariplutaḥ
c mriyate rudatāṃ madhye jñātīnāṃ na sa pūruṣaḥ

c apīdānīṃ suyuddhena gaccheyaṃ satsalokatām

a śastrāvabhṛtham āptānāṃ dhruvaṃ vāsas triviṣṭape
c mudā nūnaṃ prapaśyanti śubhrā hy apsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ
d mṛdhe tanutyajo yodhān prekṣanty apsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ
d nūnaṃ mudopatiṣṭhanti svarge tān apsarogaṇāḥ
a paśyanti nūnaṃ pitaraḥ pūjitāñ śakrasaṃsadi

a pitāmahena vṛddhena tathācāryeṇa dhīmatā

d sārdhaṃ duryodhanaḥ svarge khelatāṃ yuddhapātitaḥ
a ghaṭamānā madarthe 'smin hatāḥ śūrā janādhipāḥ
c śerate lohitāktāṅgāḥ pṛthivyāṃ śaravikṣatāḥ
a uttamāstravidaḥ śūrā yathoktakratuyājinaḥ
c tyaktvā prāṇān yathānyāyam indrasadmasu dhiṣṭhitāḥ

c jīvitaṃ yadi rakṣeyaṃ loko māṃ garhayed dhruvam
a kīdṛśaṃ ca bhaved rājyaṃ mama hīnasya bandhubhiḥ
c sakhibhiś ca suhṛdbhiś ca praṇipatya ca pāṇḍavam
a so 'ham etādṛśaṃ kṛtvā jagato 'sya parābhavam
c suyuddhena tataḥ svargaṃ prāpsyāmi na tad anyathā
a evaṃ duryodhanenoktaṃ sarve saṃpūjya tad vacaḥ
b tac chrutvā tava putrasya sattvayuktasya bhāṣitam

c paryavasthāpya cātmānam anyonyena punas tadā

 saṃjaya uvāca
a atha haimavate prasthe sthitvā yuddhābhinandinaḥ
c sarva eva mahārāja yodhās tatra samāgatāḥ
a śalyaś ca citrasenaś ca śakuniś ca mahārathaḥ
c aśvatthāmā kṛpaś caiva kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥ
a suṣeṇo 'riṣṭasenaś ca dhṛtasenaś ca vīryavān
c jayatsenaś ca rājānas te rātrim uṣitās tataḥ

c sarvayuddhavibhāgajñam antakapratimaṃ yudhi

c ādityasya tviṣā tulyaṃ buddhyā cośanasā samam

c sāṅgāṃś ca caturo vedān samyag ākhyānapañcamān
a ārādhya tryambakaṃ yatnād vratair ugrair mahātapāḥ
c ayonijāyām utpanno droṇenāyonijena yaḥ
a tam apratimakarmāṇaṃ rūpeṇāsadṛśaṃ bhuvi

e tam abhyetyātmajas tubhyam aśvatthāmānam abravīt
a yaṃ puraskṛtya sahitā yudhi jeṣyāma pāṇḍavān
c guruputro 'dya sarveṣām asmākaṃ paramā gatiḥ

 drauṇir uvāca
a ayaṃ kulena vīryeṇa tejasā yaśasā śriyā
c sarvair guṇaiḥ samuditaḥ śalyo no 'stu camūpatiḥ
a bhāgineyān nijāṃs tyaktvā kṛtajño 'smān upāgataḥ
c mahāseno mahābāhur mahāsena ivāparaḥ
a enaṃ senāpatiṃ kṛtvā nṛpatiṃ nṛpasattama
c śakyaḥ prāptuṃ jayo 'smābhir devaiḥ skandam ivājitam
a tathokte droṇaputreṇa sarva eva narādhipāḥ
c parivārya sthitāḥ śalyaṃ jayaśabdāṃś ca cakrire
e yuddhāya ca matiṃ cakrūr āveśaṃ ca paraṃ yayuḥ
a tato duryodhanaḥ śalyaṃ bhūmau sthitvā rathe sthitam
c uvāca prāñjalir bhūtvā rāmabhīṣmasamaṃ raṇe
a ayaṃ sa kālaḥ saṃprāpto mitrāṇāṃ mitravatsala
c yatra mitram amitraṃ vā parīkṣante budhā janāḥ
a sa bhavān astu naḥ śūraḥ praṇetā vāhinīmukhe
c raṇaṃ ca yāte bhavati pāṇḍavā mandacetasaḥ
e bhaviṣyanti sahāmātyāḥ pāñcālāś ca nirudyamāḥ
f duryodhanavacaḥ śrutvā śalyo madrādhipas tadā
f uvāca vākyaṃ dharmajño rājānaṃ rājasaṃnidhau
 śalya uvāca
a yat tu māṃ manyase rājan kururāja karomi tat
c tvatpriyārthaṃ hi me sarvaṃ prāṇā rājyaṃ dhanāni ca
 duryodhana uvāca
a senāpatyena varaye tvām ahaṃ mātulātulam
c so 'smān pāhi yudhāṃ śreṣṭha skando devān ivāhave
a abhiṣicyasva rājendra devānām iva pāvakiḥ
c jahi śatrūn raṇe vīra mahendro dānavān iva
 saṃjaya uvāca
a etac chrutvā vaco rājño madrarājaḥ pratāpavān
c duryodhanaṃ tadā rājan vākyam etad uvāca ha
a duryodhana mahābāho śṛṇu vākyavidāṃ vara
c yāv etau manyase kṛṣṇau rathasthau rathināṃ varau
e na me tulyāv ubhāv etau bāhuvīrye kathaṃ cana
a udyatāṃ pṛthivīṃ sarvāṃ sasurāsuramānavām
c yodhayeyaṃ raṇamukhe saṃkruddhaḥ kim u pāṇḍavān
e vijeṣye ca raṇe pārthān somakāṃś ca samāgatān
a ahaṃ senāpraṇetā te bhaviṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ

a evam uktas tato rājā madrādhipatim añjasā

a abhiṣikte tatas tasmin siṃhanādo mahān abhūt
c tava sainyeṣv avādyanta vāditrāṇi ca bhārata
a hṛṣṭāś cāsaṃs tadā yodhā madrakāś ca mahārathāḥ
c tuṣṭuvuś caiva rājānaṃ śalyam āhavaśobhinam
a jaya rājaṃś ciraṃ jīva jahi śatrūn samāgatān
c tava bāhubalaṃ prāpya dhārtarāṣṭrā mahābalāḥ
e nikhilāṃ pṛthivīṃ sarvāṃ praśāsantu hatadviṣaḥ
a tvaṃ hi śakto raṇe jetuṃ sasurāsuramānavān
c martyadharmāṇa iha tu kim u somakasṛñjayān
a evaṃ saṃstūyamānas tu madrāṇām adhipo balī
c harṣaṃ prāpa tadā vīro durāpam akṛtātmabhiḥ
 śalya uvāca
a adyaivāhaṃ raṇe sarvān pāñcālān saha pāṇḍavaiḥ
c nihaniṣyāmi rājendra svargaṃ yāsyāmi vā hataḥ
a adya paśyantu māṃ lokā vicarantam abhītavat
c adya pāṇḍusutāḥ sarve vāsudevaḥ sasātyakiḥ
a pāñcālāś cedayaś caiva draupadeyāś ca sarvaśaḥ
c dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca sarve cāpi prabhadrakāḥ
a vikramaṃ mama paśyantu dhanuṣaś ca mahad balam

c yādṛśaṃ me balaṃ bāhvoḥ saṃpad astreṣu yā ca me
a adya me vikramaṃ dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥ

 saṃjaya uvāca
a abhiṣikte tadā śalye tava sainyeṣu mānada

a hṛṣṭāḥ sumanasaś caiva babhūvus tatra sainikāḥ

a praharṣaṃ prāpya senā tu tāvakī bharatarṣabha

c bhavān netā ca goptā ca vidhatsva yad anantaram

c kṛtī ca citrayodhī ca saṃyukto lāghavena ca

d evam ukte tu kṛṣṇena dharmarājo viśāṃ patiḥ

c babhūva pāṇḍaveyānāṃ sainyaṃ pramuditaṃ niśi
e sūtaputrasya nidhane jayaṃ labdhvā ca māriṣa

 saṃjaya uvāca
a vyatītāyāṃ rajanyāṃ tu rājā duryodhanas tadā

c ayojayan rathāṃs tūrṇaṃ paryadhāvaṃs tathāpare

c pravibhajya balaṃ sarvam anīkeṣu vyavasthitāḥ

a anye ca pārthivāḥ śeṣāḥ samayaṃ cakrire tadā

d adyācāryasuto drauṇir naiko yudhyeta śatrubhiḥ

 saṃjaya uvāca
a kṣayaṃ manuṣyadehānāṃ rathanāgāśvasaṃkṣayam
c śṛṇu rājan sthiro bhūtvā saṃgrāmaṃ śaṃsato mama
d śṛṇu rājann avahito gajāśvanarasaṃkṣayam
d vakṣye 'haṃ sarvayodhānāṃ saṃgrāmaṃ tava dāruṇam
a āśā balavatī rājan putrāṇāṃ te 'bhavat tadā
c hate bhīṣme ca droṇe ca sūtaputre ca pātite
e śalyaḥ pārthān raṇe sarvān nihaniṣyati māriṣa
a tām āśāṃ hṛdaye kṛtvā samāśvāsya ca bhārata
c madrarājaṃ ca samare samāśritya mahāratham
e nāthavantam athātmānam amanyata sutas tava
a yadā karṇe hate pārthāḥ siṃhanādaṃ pracakrire
c tadā rājan dhārtarāṣṭrān āviveśa mahad bhayam
a tān samāśvāsya tu tadā madrarājaḥ pratāpavān
c vyūhya vyūhaṃ mahārāja sarvatobhadram ṛddhimat
a pratyudyāto raṇe pārthān madrarājaḥ pratāpavān
c vidhunvan kārmukaṃ citraṃ bhāraghnaṃ vegavattaram
a rathapravaram āsthāya saindhavāśvaṃ mahārathaḥ
c tasya sītā mahārāja rathasthāśobhayad ratham
d tasya sthitvā mahārāja mukhe vyūhasya daṃśitaḥ
a sa tena saṃvṛto vīro rathenāmitrakarśanaḥ
c tasthau śūro mahārāja putrāṇāṃ te bhayapraṇut
a prayāṇe madrarājo 'bhūn mukhaṃ vyūhasya daṃśitaḥ
c madrakaiḥ sahito vīraiḥ karṇaputraiś ca durjayaiḥ
a savye 'bhūt kṛtavarmā ca trigartaiḥ parivāritaḥ
c gautamo dakṣiṇe pārśve śakaiś ca yavanaiḥ saha
a aśvatthāmā pṛṣṭhato 'bhūt kāmbojaiḥ parivāritaḥ
c duryodhano 'bhavan madhye rakṣitaḥ kurupuṃgavaiḥ
a hayānīkena mahatā saubalaś cāpi saṃvṛtaḥ
c prayayau sarvasainyena kaitavyaś ca mahārathaḥ
a pāṇḍavāś ca maheṣvāsā vyūhya sainyam ariṃdamāḥ
c tridhā bhūtvā mahārāja tava sainyam upādravan
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca sātyakiś ca mahārathaḥ
c śalyasya vāhinīṃ tūrṇam abhidudruvur āhave
a tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā svenānīkena saṃvṛtaḥ
c śalyam evābhidudrāva jighāṃsur bharatarṣabha
a hārdikyaṃ tu maheṣvāsam arjunaḥ śatrupūgahā
c saṃśaptakagaṇāṃś caiva vegato 'bhividudruve
a gautamaṃ bhīmaseno vai somakāś ca mahārathāḥ
c abhyadravanta rājendra jighāṃsantaḥ parān yudhi
a mādrīputrau tu śakunim ulūkaṃ ca mahārathau
c sasainyau sahasenau tāv upatasthatur āhave
a tathaivāyutaśo yodhās tāvakāḥ pāṇḍavān raṇe
c abhyadravanta saṃkruddhā vividhāyudhapāṇayaḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a hate bhīṣme maheṣvāse droṇe karṇe mahārathe
c kuruṣv alpāvaśiṣṭeṣu pāṇḍaveṣu ca saṃyuge
a susaṃrabdheṣu pārtheṣu parākrānteṣu saṃjaya
c māmakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca kiṃ śiṣṭam abhavad balam
 saṃjaya uvāca
a yathā vayaṃ pare rājan yuddhāya samavasthitāḥ
c yāvac cāsīd balaṃ śiṣṭaṃ saṃgrāme tan nibodha me
a ekādaśa sahasrāṇi rathānāṃ bharatarṣabha
c daśa dantisahasrāṇi sapta caiva śatāni ca
a pūrṇe śatasahasre dve hayānāṃ bharatarṣabha
c narakoṭyas tathā tisro balam etat tavābhavat
a rathānāṃ ṣaṭsahasrāṇi ṣaṭsahasrāś ca kuñjarāḥ
c daśa cāśvasahasrāṇi pattikoṭī ca bhārata
a etad balaṃ pāṇḍavānām abhavac cheṣam āhave
b svalpam apy etad eveha balavat parirakṣitam
c eta eva samājagmur yuddhāya bharatarṣabha
d śastrāstreṣv abhavan ghorāḥ ketavaḥ kṣayakāriṇaḥ
d bhrāntyāśvāḥ śataśas tatra netrāṇy uccair avarṣayan
a evaṃ vibhajya rājendra madrarājamate sthitāḥ
c pāṇḍavān pratyudīyāma jayagṛddhāḥ pramanyavaḥ
a tathaiva pāṇḍavāḥ śūrāḥ samare jitakāśinaḥ
c upayātā naravyāghrāḥ pāñcālāś ca yaśasvinaḥ
a evam ete balaughena parasparavadhaiṣiṇaḥ
c upayātā naravyāghrāḥ pūrvāṃ saṃdhyāṃ prati prabho
a tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ ghorarūpaṃ bhayānakam
c tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca nighnatām itaretaram
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ kurūṇāṃ bhayavardhanam
c sṛñjayaiḥ saha rājendra ghoraṃ devāsuropamam
a narā rathā gajaughāś ca sādinaś ca sahasraśaḥ
c vājinaś ca parākrāntāḥ samājagmuḥ parasparam
a nāgānāṃ bhīmarūpāṇāṃ dravatāṃ nisvano mahān
c aśrūyata yathā kāle jaladānāṃ nabhastale
a nāgair abhyāhatāḥ ke cit sarathā rathino 'patan
c vyadravanta raṇe vīrā drāvyamāṇā madotkaṭaiḥ
a hayaughān pādarakṣāṃś ca rathinas tatra śikṣitāḥ
c śaraiḥ saṃpreṣayām āsuḥ paralokāya bhārata
a sādinaḥ śikṣitā rājan parivārya mahārathān
c vicaranto raṇe 'bhyaghnan prāsaśaktyṛṣṭibhis tathā
a dhanvinaḥ puruṣāḥ ke cit saṃnivārya mahārathān
c ekaṃ bahava āsādya preṣayeyur yamakṣayam
a nāgaṃ rathavarāṃś cānye parivārya mahārathāḥ
c sottarāyudhinaṃ jaghnur dravamāṇā mahāravam
a tathā ca rathinaṃ kruddhaṃ vikirantaṃ śarān bahūn
c nāgā jaghnur mahārāja parivārya samantataḥ
a nāgo nāgam abhidrutya rathī ca rathinaṃ raṇe
c śaktitomaranārācair nijaghnus tatra tatra ha
a pādātān avamṛdnanto rathavāraṇavājinaḥ
c raṇamadhye vyadṛśyanta kurvanto mahad ākulam
a hayāś ca paryadhāvanta cāmarair upaśobhitāḥ
c haṃsā himavataḥ prasthe pibanta iva medinīm
a teṣāṃ tu vājināṃ bhūmiḥ khuraiś citrā viśāṃ pate
c aśobhata yathā nārī karajakṣatavikṣatā
a vājināṃ khuraśabdena rathanemisvanena ca
c pattīnāṃ cāpi śabdena nāgānāṃ bṛṃhitena ca
a vāditrāṇāṃ ca ghoṣeṇa śaṅkhānāṃ nisvanena ca
c abhavan nāditā bhūmir nirghātair iva bhārata
a dhanuṣāṃ kūjamānānāṃ nistriṃśānāṃ ca dīpyatām
c kavacānāṃ prabhābhiś ca na prājñāyata kiṃ cana
a bahavo bāhavaś chinnā nāgarājakaropamāḥ
c udveṣṭante viveṣṭante vegaṃ kurvanti dāruṇam
a śirasāṃ ca mahārāja patatāṃ vasudhātale
c cyutānām iva tālebhyaḥ phalānāṃ śrūyate svanaḥ
a śirobhiḥ patitair bhāti rudhirārdrair vasuṃdharā
c tapanīyanibhaiḥ kāle nalinair iva bhārata
a udvṛttanayanais tais tu gatasattvaiḥ suvikṣataiḥ
c vyabhrājata mahārāja puṇḍarīkair ivāvṛtā
a bāhubhiś candanādigdhaiḥ sakeyūrair mahādhanaiḥ
c patitair bhāti rājendra mahī śakradhvajair iva
a ūrubhiś ca narendrāṇāṃ vinikṛttair mahāhave
c hastihastopamair anyaiḥ saṃvṛtaṃ tad raṇāṅgaṇam
a kabandhaśatasaṃkīrṇaṃ chatracāmaraśobhitam
c senāvanaṃ tac chuśubhe vanaṃ puṣpācitaṃ yathā
a tatra yodhā mahārāja vicaranto hy abhītavat
c dṛśyante rudhirāktāṅgāḥ puṣpitā iva kiṃśukāḥ
a mātaṅgāś cāpy adṛśyanta śaratomarapīḍitāḥ
c patantas tatra tatraiva chinnābhrasadṛśā raṇe
a gajānīkaṃ mahārāja vadhyamānaṃ mahātmabhiḥ
c vyadīryata diśaḥ sarvā vātanunnā ghanā iva
a te gajā ghanasaṃkāśāḥ petur urvyāṃ samantataḥ
c vajrarugṇā iva babhuḥ parvatā yugasaṃkṣaye
a hayānāṃ sādibhiḥ sārdhaṃ patitānāṃ mahītale
c rāśayaḥ saṃpradṛśyante girimātrās tatas tataḥ
a saṃjajñe raṇabhūmau tu paralokavahā nadī
c śoṇitodā rathāvartā dhvajavṛkṣāsthiśarkarā
a bhujanakrā dhanuḥsrotā hastiśailā hayopalā
c medomajjākardaminī chatrahaṃsā gadoḍupā
a kavacoṣṇīṣasaṃchannā patākāruciradrumā
c cakracakrāvalījuṣṭā triveṇūdaṇḍakāvṛtā
a śūrāṇāṃ harṣajananī bhīrūṇāṃ bhayavardhinī
c prāvartata nadī raudrā kurusṛñjayasaṃkulā
a tāṃ nadīṃ pitṛlokāya vahantīm atibhairavām
c terur vāhananaubhis te śūrāḥ parighabāhavaḥ
a vartamāne tathā yuddhe nirmaryāde viśāṃ pate
c caturaṅgakṣaye ghore pūrvaṃ devāsuropame
a akrośan bāndhavān anye tatra tatra paraṃtapa
c krośadbhir bāndhavaiś cānye bhayārtā na nivartire
a nirmaryāde tathā yuddhe vartamāne bhayānake
c arjuno bhīmasenaś ca mohayāṃ cakratuḥ parān
a sā vadhyamānā mahatī senā tava janādhipa
c amuhyat tatra tatraiva yoṣin madavaśād iva
a mohayitvā ca tāṃ senāṃ bhīmasenadhanaṃjayau
c dadhmatur vārijau tatra siṃhanādaṃ ca nedatuḥ
a śrutvaiva tu mahāśabdaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnaśikhaṇḍinau
c dharmarājaṃ puraskṛtya madrarājam abhidrutau
a tatrāścaryam apaśyāma ghorarūpaṃ viśāṃ pate
c śalyena saṃgatāḥ śūrā yad ayudhyanta bhāgaśaḥ
a mādrīputrau sarabhasau kṛtāstrau yuddhadurmadau
c abhyayātāṃ tvarāyuktau jigīṣantau balaṃ tava
a tato nyavartata balaṃ tāvakaṃ bharatarṣabha
c śaraiḥ praṇunnaṃ bahudhā pāṇḍavair jitakāśibhiḥ
a vadhyamānā camūḥ sā tu putrāṇāṃ prekṣatāṃ tava
c bheje diśo mahārāja praṇunnā dṛḍhadhanvibhiḥ
e hāhākāro mahāñ jajñe yodhānāṃ tava bhārata
a tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti vāg āsīd drāvitānāṃ mahātmanām
c kṣatriyāṇāṃ tadānyonyaṃ saṃyuge jayam icchatām
e ādravann eva bhagnās te pāṇḍavais tava sainikāḥ
a tyaktvā yuddhe priyān putrān bhrātṝn atha pitāmahān
c mātulān bhāgineyāṃś ca tathā saṃbandhibāndhavān
a hayān dvipāṃs tvarayanto yodhā jagmuḥ samantataḥ
c ātmatrāṇakṛtotsāhās tāvakā bharatarṣabha
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tat prabhagnaṃ balaṃ dṛṣṭvā madrarājaḥ pratāpavān
c uvāca sārathiṃ tūrṇaṃ codayāśvān mahājavān
a eṣa tiṣṭhati vai rājā pāṇḍuputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c chatreṇa dhriyamāṇena pāṇḍureṇa virājatā
a atra māṃ prāpaya kṣipraṃ paśya me sārathe balam
c na samarthā hi me pārthāḥ sthātum adya puro yudhi
a evam uktas tataḥ prāyān madrarājasya sārathiḥ
c yatra rājā satyasaṃdho dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a āpatantaṃ ca sahasā pāṇḍavānāṃ mahad balam
c dadhāraiko raṇe śalyo velevoddhṛtam arṇavam
a pāṇḍavānāṃ balaughas tu śalyam āsādya māriṣa
c vyatiṣṭhata tadā yuddhe sindhor vega ivācalam
a madrarājaṃ tu samare dṛṣṭvā yuddhāya viṣṭhitam
c kuravaḥ saṃnyavartanta mṛtyuṃ kṛtvā nivartanam
a teṣu rājan nivṛtteṣu vyūḍhānīkeṣu bhāgaśaḥ
c prāvartata mahāraudraḥ saṃgrāmaḥ śoṇitodakaḥ
e samārchac citrasenena nakulo yuddhadurmadaḥ
f nātheva ca mahārāja citrasenas tu pāṇḍavam
a tau parasparam āsādya citrakārmukadhāriṇau
c meghāv iva yathodvṛttau dakṣiṇottaravarṣiṇau
a śaratoyaiḥ siṣicatus tau parasparam āhave
c nāntaraṃ tatra paśyāmi pāṇḍavasyetarasya vā
a ubhau kṛtāstrau balinau rathacaryāviśāradau
c parasparavadhe yattau chidrānveṣaṇatatparau
a citrasenas tu bhallena pītena niśitena ca
c nakulasya mahārāja muṣṭideśe 'cchinad dhanuḥ
a athainaṃ chinnadhanvānaṃ rukmapuṅkhaiḥ śilāśitaiḥ
c tribhiḥ śarair asaṃbhrānto lalāṭe vai samarpayat
a hayāṃś cāsya śarais tīkṣṇaiḥ preṣayām āsa mṛtyave
c tathā dhvajaṃ sārathiṃ ca tribhis tribhir apātayat
a sa śatrubhujanirmuktair lalāṭasthais tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
c nakulaḥ śuśubhe rājaṃs triśṛṅga iva parvataḥ
a sa chinnadhanvā virathaḥ khaḍgam ādāya carma ca
c rathād avātarad vīraḥ śailāgrād iva kesarī
a padbhyām āpatatas tasya śaravṛṣṭim avāsṛjat
c nakulo 'py agrasat tāṃ vai carmaṇā laghuvikramaḥ
a citrasenarathaṃ prāpya citrayodhī jitaśramaḥ
c āruroha mahābāhuḥ sarvasainyasya paśyataḥ
a sakuṇḍalaṃ samukuṭaṃ sunasaṃ svāyatekṣaṇam
c citrasenaśiraḥ kāyād apāharata pāṇḍavaḥ
e sa papāta rathopasthād divākarasamaprabhaḥ
a citrasenaṃ viśastaṃ tu dṛṣṭvā tatra mahārathāḥ
b citrasenaṃ hataṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve pāṇḍavasainikāḥ
b citraseno mahārāja nakulena hato raṇe
c sādhuvādasvanāṃś cakruḥ siṃhanādāṃś ca puṣkalān
a viśastaṃ bhrātaraṃ dṛṣṭvā karṇaputrau mahārathau
c suṣeṇaḥ satyasenaś ca muñcantau niśitāñ śarān
a tato 'bhyadhāvatāṃ tūrṇaṃ pāṇḍavaṃ rathināṃ varam
c jighāṃsantau yathā nāgaṃ vyāghrau rājan mahāvane
a tāv abhyadhāvatāṃ tīkṣṇau dvāv apy enaṃ mahāratham
c śaraughān samyag asyantau jīmūtau salilaṃ yathā
a sa śaraiḥ sarvato viddhaḥ prahṛṣṭa iva pāṇḍavaḥ
b nakulo bharataśreṣṭhas tābhyāṃ parabalārdanaḥ
c anyat kārmukam ādāya ratham āruhya vīryavān
e atiṣṭhata raṇe vīraḥ kruddharūpa ivāntakaḥ
a tasya tau bhrātarau rājañ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c rathaṃ viśakalīkartuṃ samārabdhau viśāṃ pate
a tataḥ prahasya nakulaś caturbhiś caturo raṇe
c jaghāna niśitais tīkṣṇaiḥ satyasenasya vājinaḥ
a tataḥ saṃdhāya nārācaṃ rukmapuṅkhaṃ śilāśitam
c dhanuś ciccheda rājendra satyasenasya pāṇḍavaḥ
a athānyaṃ ratham āsthāya dhanur ādāya cāparam
c satyasenaḥ suṣeṇaś ca pāṇḍavaṃ paryadhāvatām
a avidhyat tāv asaṃbhrāntau mādrīputraḥ pratāpavān
c dvābhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ mahārāja śarābhyāṃ raṇamūrdhani
a suṣeṇas tu tataḥ kruddhaḥ pāṇḍavasya mahad dhanuḥ
c ciccheda prahasan yuddhe kṣurapreṇa mahārathaḥ
a athānyad dhanur ādāya nakulaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
c suṣeṇaṃ pañcabhir viddhvā dhvajam ekena cicchide
a satyasenasya ca dhanur hastāvāpaṃ ca māriṣa
c ciccheda tarasā yuddhe tata uccukruśur janāḥ
a athānyad dhanur ādāya vegaghnaṃ bhārasādhanam
c śaraiḥ saṃchādayām āsa samantāt pāṇḍunandanam
a saṃnivārya tu tān bāṇān nakulaḥ paravīrahā
c satyasenaṃ suṣeṇaṃ ca dvābhyāṃ dvābhyām avidhyata
d tataḥ śaktiṃ samudyamya satyasenāya cikṣipe
a tāv enaṃ pratyavidhyetāṃ pṛthak pṛthag ajihmagaiḥ
c sārathiṃ cāsya rājendra śarair vivyadhatuḥ śitaiḥ
a satyaseno ratheṣāṃ tu nakulasya dhanus tathā
c pṛthak śarābhyāṃ ciccheda kṛtahastaḥ pratāpavān
a sa rathe 'tirathas tiṣṭhan rathaśaktiṃ parāmṛśat
c svarṇadaṇḍām akuṇṭhāgrāṃ tailadhautāṃ sunirmalām
a lelihānām iva vibho nāgakanyāṃ mahāviṣām
c samudyamya ca cikṣepa satyasenasya saṃyuge
a sā tasya hṛdayaṃ saṃkhye bibheda śatadhā nṛpa
c sa papāta rathād bhūmau gatasattvo 'lpacetanaḥ
a bhrātaraṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā suṣeṇaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
c abhyavarṣac charais tūrṇaṃ padātiṃ pāṇḍunandanam
d caturbhiś caturo vāhān dhvajaṃ chittvā tu pañcabhiḥ
d tribhir vai sārathiṃ hatvā karṇaputro nanāda ha
a nakulaṃ virathaṃ dṛṣṭvā draupadeyo mahābalaḥ
c sutasomo 'bhidudrāva parīpsan pitaraṃ raṇe
a tato 'dhiruhya nakulaḥ sutasomasya taṃ ratham
c śuśubhe bharataśreṣṭho giristha iva kesarī
e so 'nyat kārmukam ādāya suṣeṇaṃ samayodhayat
a tāv ubhau śaravarṣābhyāṃ samāsādya parasparam
c parasparavadhe yatnaṃ cakratuḥ sumahārathau
a suṣeṇas tu tataḥ kruddhaḥ pāṇḍavaṃ viśikhais tribhiḥ
c sutasomaṃ ca viṃśatyā bāhvor urasi cārpayat
a tataḥ kruddho mahārāja nakulaḥ paravīrahā
c śarais tasya diśaḥ sarvāś chādayām āsa vīryavān
a tato gṛhītvā tīkṣṇāgram ardhacandraṃ sutejanam
c sa vegayuktaṃ cikṣepa karṇaputrasya saṃyuge
a tasya tena śiraḥ kāyāj jahāra nṛpasattama
c paśyatāṃ sarvasainyānāṃ tad adbhutam ivābhavat
a sa hataḥ prāpatad rājan nakulena mahātmanā
c nadīvegād ivārugṇas tīrajaḥ pādapo mahān
a karṇaputravadhaṃ dṛṣṭvā nakulasya ca vikramam
c pradudrāva bhayāt senā tāvakī bharatarṣabha
a tāṃ tu senāṃ mahārāja madrarājaḥ pratāpavān
c apālayad raṇe śūraḥ senāpatir ariṃdamaḥ
d sā senā vidrutā rājan diśo daśa bhayadrutā
a vibhīs tasthau mahārāja vyavasthāpya ca vāhinīm
c siṃhanādaṃ bhṛśaṃ kṛtvā dhanuḥśabdaṃ ca dāruṇam
a tāvakāḥ samare rājan rakṣitā dṛḍhadhanvanā
c pratyudyayur arātīṃs te samantād vigatavyathāḥ
a madrarājaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ parivārya samantataḥ
c sthitā rājan mahāsenā yoddhukāmāḥ samantataḥ
a sātyakir bhīmasenaś ca mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavau
c yudhiṣṭhiraṃ puraskṛtya hrīniṣedham ariṃdamam
a parivārya raṇe vīrāḥ siṃhanādaṃ pracakrire
c bāṇaśabdaravāṃś cogrān kṣveḍāṃś ca vividhān dadhuḥ
a tathaiva tāvakāḥ sarve madrādhipatim añjasā
c parivārya susaṃrabdhāḥ punar yuddham arocayan
a tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ bhīrūṇāṃ bhayavardhanam
c tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca mṛtyuṃ kṛtvā nivartanam
a yathā devāsuraṃ yuddhaṃ pūrvam āsīd viśāṃ pate
c abhītānāṃ tathā rājan yamarāṣṭravivardhanam
a tataḥ kapidhvajo rājan hatvā saṃśaptakān raṇe
c abhyadravata tāṃ senāṃ kauravīṃ pāṇḍunandanaḥ
a tathaiva pāṇḍavāḥ śeṣā dhṛṣṭadyumnapurogamāḥ
c abhyadhāvanta tāṃ senāṃ visṛjantaḥ śitāñ śarān
a pāṇḍavair avakīrṇānāṃ saṃmohaḥ samajāyata
c na ca jajñur anīkāni diśo vā pradiśas tathā
a āpūryamāṇā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ pāṇḍavacoditaiḥ
c hatapravīrā vidhvastā kīryamāṇā samantataḥ
e kauravy avadhyata camūḥ pāṇḍuputrair mahārathaiḥ
a tathaiva pāṇḍavī senā śarai rājan samantataḥ
c raṇe 'hanyata putrais te śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a te sene bhṛśasaṃtapte vadhyamāne parasparam
c vyākule samapadyetāṃ varṣāsu saritāv iva
a āviveśa tatas tīvraṃ tāvakānāṃ mahad bhayam
c pāṇḍavānāṃ ca rājendra tathābhūte mahāhave
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tasmin vilulite sainye vadhyamāne parasparam
c dravamāṇeṣu yodheṣu ninadatsu ca dantiṣu
a kūjatāṃ stanatāṃ caiva padātīnāṃ mahāhave
c vidruteṣu mahārāja hayeṣu bahudhā tadā
a prakṣaye dāruṇe jāte saṃhāre sarvadehinām
c nānāśastrasamāvāpe vyatiṣaktarathadvipe
a harṣaṇe yuddhaśauṇḍānāṃ bhīrūṇāṃ bhayavardhane
c gāhamāneṣu yodheṣu parasparavadhaiṣiṣu
a prāṇādāne mahāghore vartamāne durodare
c saṃgrāme ghorarūpe tu yamarāṣṭravivardhane
a pāṇḍavās tāvakaṃ sainyaṃ vyadhaman niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c tathaiva tāvakā yodhā jaghnuḥ pāṇḍavasainikān
a tasmiṃs tathā vartamāne yuddhe bhīrubhayāvahe
c pūrvāhṇe caiva saṃprāpte bhāskarodayanaṃ prati
a labdhalakṣāḥ pare rājan rakṣitāś ca mahātmanā
c ayodhayaṃs tava balaṃ mṛtyuṃ kṛtvā nivartanam
a balibhiḥ pāṇḍavair dṛptair labdhalakṣaiḥ prahāribhiḥ
c kauravy asīdat pṛtanā mṛgīvāgnisamākulā
a tāṃ dṛṣṭvā sīdatīṃ senāṃ paṅke gām iva durbalām
c ujjihīrṣus tadā śalyaḥ prāyāt pāṇḍucamūṃ prati
a madrarājas tu saṃkruddho gṛhītvā dhanur uttamam
c abhyadravata saṃgrāme pāṇḍavān ātatāyinaḥ
a pāṇḍavāś ca mahārāja samare jitakāśinaḥ
c madrarājaṃ samāsādya vivyadhur niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
d tathaiva tāvakā yaudhā dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
a tataḥ śaraśatais tīkṣṇair madrarājo mahābalaḥ
c ardayām āsa tāṃ senāṃ dharmarājasya paśyataḥ
a prādurāsaṃs tato rājan nānārūpāṇy anekaśaḥ
c cacāla śabdaṃ kurvāṇā mahī cāpi saparvatā
a sadaṇḍaśūlā dīptāgrāḥ śīryamāṇāḥ samantataḥ
c ulkā bhūmiṃ divaḥ petur āhatya ravimaṇḍalam
a mṛgāś ca māhiṣāś cāpi pakṣiṇaś ca viśāṃ pate
c apasavyaṃ tadā cakruḥ senāṃ te bahuśo nṛpa
d bhṛgusūnudharāputrau śaśijena samanvitau
d caramaṃ pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ purastāt sarvabhūbhujām
d śastrāgreṣv abhavaj jvālā netrāṇy āhatya varṣatī
d śiraḥ svalīyanta bhṛśaṃ kākolūkāś ca ketuṣu
a tatas tad yuddham atyugram abhavat saṃghacāriṇām
c tathā sarvāṇy anīkāni saṃnipatya janādhipa
e abhyayuḥ kauravā rājan pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm
a śalyas tu śaravarṣeṇa varṣann iva sahasradṛk
c abhyavarṣad adīnātmā kuntīputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
a bhīmasenaṃ śaraiś cāpi rukmapuṅkhaiḥ śilāśitaḥ
c draupadeyāṃs tathā sarvān mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavau
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca śaineyaṃ śikhaṇḍinam athāpi ca
c ekaikaṃ daśabhir bāṇair vivyādha ca mahābalaḥ
e tato 'sṛjad bāṇavarṣaṃ gharmānte maghavān iva
a tataḥ prabhadrakā rājan somakāś ca sahasraśaḥ
c patitāḥ pātyamānāś ca dṛśyante śalyasāyakaiḥ
a bhramarāṇām iva vrātāḥ śalabhānām iva vrajāḥ
c hrādinya iva meghebhyaḥ śalyasya nyapatañ śarāḥ
a dviradās turagāś cārtāḥ pattayo rathinas tathā
c śalyasya bāṇair nyapatan babhramur vyanadaṃs tathā
a āviṣṭa iva madreśo manyunā pauruṣeṇa ca
c prācchādayad arīn saṃkhye kālasṛṣṭa ivāntakaḥ
e vinardamāno madreśo meghahrādo mahābalaḥ
a sā vadhyamānā śalyena pāṇḍavānām anīkinī
b pradudrāva mahārāja śalyabāṇaiḥ prapīḍitā
c ajātaśatruṃ kaunteyam abhyadhāvad yudhiṣṭhiram
a tāṃ samarpya tataḥ saṃkhye laghuhastaḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c śaravarṣeṇa mahatā yudhiṣṭhiram apīḍayat
d vavarṣa samare kruddho dharmaputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
a tam āpatantaṃ pattyaśvaiḥ kruddho rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c avārayac charais tīkṣṇair mattaṃ dvipam ivāṅkuśaiḥ
a tasya śalyaḥ śaraṃ ghoraṃ mumocāśīviṣopamam
c so 'bhyavidhyan mahātmānaṃ vegenābhyapatac ca gām
a tato vṛkodaraḥ kruddhaḥ śalyaṃ vivyādha saptabhiḥ
c pañcabhiḥ sahadevas tu nakulo daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ
a draupadeyāś ca śatrughnaṃ śūram ārtāyaniṃ śaraiḥ
c abhyavarṣan mahābhāgaṃ meghā iva mahīdharam
a tato dṛṣṭvā tudyamānaṃ śalyaṃ pārthaiḥ samantataḥ
c kṛtavarmā kṛpaś caiva saṃkruddhāv abhyadhāvatām
a ulūkaś ca patatrī ca śakuniś cāpi saubalaḥ
c smayamānaś ca śanakair aśvatthāmā mahārathaḥ
e tava putrāś ca kārtsnyena jugupuḥ śalyam āhave
a bhīmasenaṃ tribhir viddhvā kṛtavarmā śilīmukhaiḥ
c bāṇavarṣeṇa mahatā kruddharūpam avārayat
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ kṛpaḥ kruddho bāṇavarṣair apīḍayat
c draupadeyāṃś ca śakunir yamau ca drauṇir abhyayāt
a duryodhano yudhāṃ śreṣṭhāv āhave keśavārjunau
c samabhyayād ugratejāḥ śaraiś cābhyahanad balī
a evaṃ dvaṃdvaśatāny āsaṃs tvadīyānāṃ paraiḥ saha
c ghorarūpāṇi citrāṇi tatra tatra viśāṃ pate
a ṛśyavarṇāñ jaghānāśvān bhojo bhīmasya saṃyuge
c so 'vatīrya rathopasthād dhatāśvaḥ pāṇḍunandanaḥ
e kālo daṇḍam ivodyamya gadāpāṇir ayudhyata
a pramukhe sahadevasya jaghānāśvāṃś ca madrarāṭ
c tataḥ śalyasya tanayaṃ sahadevo 'sināvadhīt
a gautamaḥ punar ācāryo dhṛṣṭadyumnam ayodhayat
c asaṃbhrāntam asaṃbhrānto yatnavān yatnavattaram
a draupadeyāṃs tathā vīrān ekaikaṃ daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ
c avidhyad ācāryasuto nātikruddhaḥ smayann iva
d yuktāśvasya punar madhyaṃ rathasyāroham icchataḥ
d punaś ca bhīmasenasya jaghānāśvāṃs tathāhave
d so 'vatīrya rathāt tūrṇaṃ hatāśvaḥ pāṇḍunandanaḥ
d kālo daṇḍam ivodyamya gadāṃ kruddho mahābalaḥ
d pothayām āsa turagān rathaṃ ca kṛtavarmaṇaḥ
d kṛtavarmā tv avaplutya rathāt tasmād apākramat
a śalyo 'pi rājan saṃkruddho nighnan somakapāṇḍavān
c punar eva śitair bāṇair yudhiṣṭhiram apīḍayat
a tasya bhīmo raṇe kruddhaḥ saṃdaṣṭadaśanacchadaḥ
c vināśāyābhisaṃdhāya gadām ādatta vīryavān
a yamadaṇḍapratīkāśāṃ kālarātrim ivodyatām
c gajavājimanuṣyāṇāṃ prāṇāntakaraṇīm api
a hemapaṭṭaparikṣiptām ulkāṃ prajvalitām iva
c śaikyāṃ vyālīm ivātyugrāṃ vajrakalpām ayasmayīm
a candanāgurupaṅkāktāṃ pramadām īpsitām iva
c vasāmedosṛgādigdhāṃ jihvāṃ vaivasvatīm iva
a paṭughaṇṭāravaśatāṃ vāsavīm aśanīm iva
c nirmuktāśīviṣākārāṃ pṛktāṃ gajamadair api
a trāsanīṃ ripusainyānāṃ svasainyapariharṣiṇīm
c manuṣyaloke vikhyātāṃ giriśṛṅgavidāriṇīm
a yayā kailāsabhavane maheśvarasakhaṃ balī
c āhvayām āsa kaunteyaḥ saṃkruddham alakādhipam
a yayā māyāvino dṛptān subahūn dhanadālaye
c jaghāna guhyakān kruddho mandārārthe mahābalaḥ
e nivāryamāṇo bahubhir draupadyāḥ priyam āsthitaḥ
a tāṃ vajramaṇiratnaughām aṣṭāśriṃ vajragauravām
c samudyamya mahābāhuḥ śalyam abhyadravad raṇe
a gadayā yuddhakuśalas tayā dāruṇanādayā
c pothayām āsa śalyasya caturo 'śvān mahājavān
a tataḥ śalyo raṇe kruddhaḥ pīne vakṣasi tomaram
c nicakhāna nadan vīro varma bhittvā ca so 'bhyagāt
a vṛkodaras tv asaṃbhrātas tam evoddhṛtya tomaram
b cikṣepa bhīmasenasya so 'sravac choṇitaṃ bahu
b tam evādāya bhīmas tu tataḥ kopasamanvitaḥ
c yantāraṃ madrarājasya nirbibheda tato hṛdi
a sa bhinnavarmā rudhiraṃ vaman vitrastamānasaḥ
c papātābhimukho dīno madrarājas tv apākramat
a kṛtapratikṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā śalyo vismitamānasaḥ
c gadām āśritya dhīrātmā pratyamitram avaikṣata
a tataḥ sumanasaḥ pārthā bhīmasenam apūjayan
b viyatsthitā jātaharṣās tataḥ siddhā babhāṣire
b pūrvajanmani prahlādo dṛṣṭo 'smābhir ayaṃ baliḥ
c tad dṛṣṭvā karma saṃgrāme ghoram akliṣṭakarmaṇaḥ
d taṃ dṛṣṭvā karma śalyasya sarvasiddhās tv apūjayan
 saṃjaya uvāca
a patitaṃ prekṣya yantāraṃ śalyaḥ sarvāyasīṃ gadām
c ādāya tarasā rājaṃs tasthau girir ivācalaḥ
a taṃ dīptam iva kālāgniṃ pāśahastam ivāntakam
c saśṛṅgam iva kailāsaṃ savajram iva vāsavam
a saśūlam iva haryakṣaṃ vane mattam iva dvipam
a   sacakram iva cakriṇam
a saśaktim iva senānyaṃ
c javenābhyapatad bhīmaḥ pragṛhya mahatīṃ gadām
d madrarājam asaṃbhrāntaḥ paśyatāṃ sarvadhanvinām
a tataḥ śaṅkhapraṇādaś ca tūryāṇāṃ ca sahasraśaḥ
c siṃhanādaś ca saṃjajñe śūrāṇāṃ harṣavardhanaḥ
a prekṣantaḥ sarvatas tau hi yodhā yodhamahādvipau
c tāvakāś ca pare caiva sādhu sādhv ity athābruvan
a na hi madrādhipād anyo rāmād vā yadunandanāt
c soḍhum utsahate vegaṃ bhīmasenasya saṃyuge
a tathā madrādhipasyāpi gadāvegaṃ mahātmanaḥ
c soḍhum utsahate nānyo yodho yudhi vṛkodarāt
a tau vṛṣāv iva nardantau maṇḍalāni viceratuḥ
c āvalgitau gadāhastau madrarājavṛkodarau
a maṇḍalāvartamārgeṣu gadāviharaṇeṣu ca
c nirviśeṣam abhūd yuddhaṃ tayoḥ puruṣasiṃhayoḥ
a taptahemamayaiḥ śubhrair babhūva bhayavardhanī
c agnijvālair ivāviddhā paṭṭaiḥ śalyasya sā gadā
a tathaiva carato mārgān maṇḍaleṣu mahātmanaḥ
c vidyud abhrapratīkāśā bhīmasya śuśubhe gadā
a tāḍitā madrarājena bhīmasya gadayā gadā
c dīpyamāneva vai rājan sasṛje pāvakārciṣaḥ
a tathā bhīmena śalyasya tāḍitā gadayā gadā
c aṅgāravarṣaṃ mumuce tad adbhutam ivābhavat
a dantair iva mahānāgau śṛṅgair iva maharṣabhau
c tottrair iva tadānyonyaṃ gadāgrābhyāṃ nijaghnatuḥ
a tau gadānihatair gātraiḥ kṣaṇena rudhirokṣitau
c prekṣaṇīyatarāv āstāṃ puṣpitāv iva kiṃśukau
a gadayā madrarājena savyadakṣiṇam āhataḥ
c bhīmaseno mahābāhur na cacālācalo yathā
a tathā bhīmagadāvegais tāḍyamāno muhur muhuḥ
c śalyo na vivyathe rājan dantinevāhato giriḥ
a śuśruve dikṣu sarvāsu tayoḥ puruṣasiṃhayoḥ
c gadānipātasaṃhrādo vajrayor iva nisvanaḥ
a nivṛtya tu mahāvīryau samucchritagadāv ubhau
c punar antaramārgasthau maṇḍalāni viceratuḥ
a athābhyetya padāny aṣṭau saṃnipāto 'bhavat tayoḥ
c udyamya lohadaṇḍābhyām atimānuṣakarmaṇoḥ
a prārthayānau tadānyo 'nyaṃ maṇḍalāni viceratuḥ
c kriyāviśeṣaṃ kṛtinau darśayām āsatus tadā
a athodyamya gade ghore saśṛṅgāv iva parvatau
c tāv ājaghnatur anyonyaṃ yathā bhūmicale 'calau
a tau parasparavegāc ca gadābhyāṃ ca bhṛśāhatau
c yugapat petatur vīrāv ubhāv indradhvajāv iva
a ubhayoḥ senayor vīrās tadā hāhākṛto 'bhavan
c bhṛśaṃ marmaṇy abhihatāv ubhāv āstāṃ suvihvalau
a tataḥ sagadam āropya madrāṇām ṛṣabhaṃ rathe
c apovāha kṛpaḥ śalyaṃ tūrṇam āyodhanād api
a kṣībavad vihvalatvāt tu nimeṣāt punar utthitaḥ
c bhīmaseno gadāpāṇiḥ samāhvayata madrapam
a tatas tu tāvakāḥ śūrā nānāśastrasamāyutāḥ
c nānāvāditraśabdena pāṇḍusenām ayodhayan
a bhujāv ucchritya śastraṃ ca śabdena mahatā tataḥ
c abhyadravan mahārāja duryodhanapurogamāḥ
a tad anīkam abhiprekṣya tatas te pāṇḍunandanāḥ
c prayayuḥ siṃhanādena duryodhanavadhepsayā
a teṣām āpatatāṃ tūrṇaṃ putras te bharatarṣabha
c prāsena cekitānaṃ vai vivyādha hṛdaye bhṛśam
a sa papāta rathopasthe tava putreṇa tāḍitaḥ
c rudhiraughapariklinnaḥ praviśya vipulaṃ tamaḥ
a cekitānaṃ hataṃ dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥ
c prasaktam abhyavarṣanta śaravarṣāṇi bhāgaśaḥ
a tāvakānām anīkeṣu pāṇḍavā jitakāśinaḥ
c vyacaranta mahārāja prekṣaṇīyāḥ samantataḥ
a kṛpaś ca kṛtavarmā ca saubalaś ca mahābalaḥ
c ayodhayan dharmarājaṃ madrarājapuraskṛtāḥ
a bhāradvājasya hantāraṃ bhūrivīryaparākramam
c duryodhano mahārāja dhṛṣṭadyumnam ayodhayat
a trisāhasrā rathā rājaṃs tava putreṇa coditāḥ
c ayodhayanta vijayaṃ droṇaputrapuraskṛtāḥ
a vijaye dhṛtasaṃkalpāḥ samabhityaktajīvitāḥ
c prāviśaṃs tāvakā rājan haṃsā iva mahat saraḥ
a tato yuddham abhūd ghoraṃ parasparavadhaiṣiṇām
c anyonyavadhasaṃyuktam anyonyaprītivardhanam
a tasmin pravṛtte saṃgrāme rājan vīravarakṣaye
c anileneritaṃ ghoram uttasthau pārthivaṃ rajaḥ
a śravaṇān nāmadheyānāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca kīrtanāt
c parasparaṃ vijānīmo ye cāyudhyann abhītavat
a tad rajaḥ puruṣavyāghra śoṇitena praśāmitam
c diśaś ca vimalā jajñus tasmin rajasi śāmite
a tathā pravṛtte saṃgrāme ghorarūpe bhayānake
c tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca nāsīt kaś cit parāṅmukhaḥ
a brahmalokaparā bhūtvā prārthayanto jayaṃ yudhi
c suyuddhena parākrāntā narāḥ svargam abhīpsavaḥ
a bhartṛpiṇḍavimokṣārthaṃ bhartṛkāryaviniścitāḥ
c svargasaṃsaktamanaso yodhā yuyudhire tadā
a nānārūpāṇi śastrāṇi visṛjanto mahārathāḥ
c anyonyam abhigarjantaḥ praharantaḥ parasparam
a hata vidhyata gṛhṇīta praharadhvaṃ nikṛntata
c iti sma vācaḥ śrūyante tava teṣāṃ ca vai bale
a tataḥ śalyo mahārāja dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
c vivyādha niśitair bāṇair hantukāmo mahāratham
a tasya pārtho mahārāja nārācān vai caturdaśa
c marmāṇy uddiśya marmajño nicakhāna hasann iva
a taṃ vārya pāṇḍavaṃ bāṇair hantukāmo mahāyaśāḥ
c vivyādha samare kruddho bahubhiḥ kaṅkapatribhiḥ
a atha bhūyo mahārāja śareṇa nataparvaṇā
c yudhiṣṭhiraṃ samājaghne sarvasainyasya paśyataḥ
a dharmarājo 'pi saṃkruddho madrarājaṃ mahāyaśāḥ
c vivyādha niśitair bāṇaiḥ kaṅkabarhiṇavājitaiḥ
a candrasenaṃ ca saptatyā sūtaṃ ca navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
c drumasenaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭyā nijaghāna mahārathaḥ
a cakrarakṣe hate śalyaḥ pāṇḍavena mahātmanā
c nijaghāna tato rājaṃś cedīn vai pañcaviṃśatim
a sātyakiṃ pañcaviṃśatyā bhīmasenaṃ ca pañcabhiḥ
c mādrīputrau śatenājau vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a evaṃ vicaratas tasya saṃgrāme rājasattama
