a athānyad dhanur ādāya mādrīputro mahārathaḥ
c madrarājarathaṃ tūrṇaṃ pūrayām āsa patribhiḥ
a yudhiṣṭhiras tu madreśaṃ sahadevaś ca māriṣa
c daśabhir daśabhir bāṇair urasy enam avidhyatām
a bhīmasenas tataḥ ṣaṣṭyā sātyakir navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
c madrarājam abhidrutya jaghnatuḥ kaṅkapatribhiḥ
a madrarājas tataḥ kruddhaḥ sātyakiṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
c vivyādha bhūyaḥ saptatyā śarāṇāṃ nataparvaṇām
a athāsya saśaraṃ cāpaṃ muṣṭau ciccheda māriṣa
c hayāṃś ca caturaḥ saṃkhye preṣayām āsa mṛtyave
a virathaṃ sātyakiṃ kṛtvā madrarājo mahābalaḥ
c viśikhānāṃ śatenainam ājaghāna samantataḥ
a mādrīputrau tu saṃrabdhau bhīmasenaṃ ca pāṇḍavam
c yudhiṣṭhiraṃ ca kauravya vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ
a tatrādbhutam apaśyāma madrarājasya pauruṣam
c yad enaṃ sahitāḥ pārthā nābhyavartanta saṃyuge
a athānyaṃ ratham āsthāya sātyakiḥ satyavikramaḥ
c pīḍitān pāṇḍavān dṛṣṭvā madrarājavaśaṃ gatān
e abhidudrāva vegena madrāṇām adhipaṃ balī
a āpatantaṃ rathaṃ tasya śalyaḥ samitiśobhanaḥ
c pratyudyayau rathenaiva matto mattam iva dvipam
a sa saṃnipātas tumulo babhūvādbhutadarśanaḥ
c sātyakeś caiva śūrasya madrāṇām adhipasya ca
e yādṛśo vai purā vṛttaḥ śambarāmararājayoḥ
a sātyakiḥ prekṣya samare madrarājaṃ vyavasthitam
c vivyādha daśabhir bāṇais tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīt
a madrarājas tu subhṛśaṃ viddhas tena mahātmanā
c sātyakiṃ prativivyādha citrapuṅkhaiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a tataḥ pārthā maheṣvāsāḥ sātvatābhisṛtaṃ nṛpam
c abhyadravan rathais tūrṇaṃ mātulaṃ vadhakāmyayā
a tata āsīt parāmardas tumulaḥ śoṇitodakaḥ
c śūrāṇāṃ yudhyamānānāṃ siṃhānām iva nardatām
a teṣām āsīn mahārāja vyatikṣepaḥ parasparam
c siṃhānām āmiṣepsūnāṃ kūjatām iva saṃyuge
a teṣāṃ bāṇasahasraughair ākīrṇā vasudhābhavat
c antarikṣaṃ ca sahasā bāṇabhūtam abhūt tadā
a śarāndhakāraṃ bahudhā kṛtaṃ tatra samantataḥ
c abhracchāyeva saṃjajñe śarair muktair mahātmabhiḥ
a tatra rājañ śarair muktair nirmuktair iva pannagaiḥ
c svarṇapuṅkhaiḥ prakāśadbhir vyarocanta diśas tathā
a tatrādbhutaṃ paraṃ cakre śalyaḥ śatrunibarhaṇaḥ
c yad ekaḥ samare śūro yodhayām āsa vai bahūn
a madrarājabhujotsṛṣṭaiḥ kaṅkabarhiṇavājitaiḥ
c saṃpatadbhiḥ śarair ghorair avākīryata medinī
a tatra śalyarathaṃ rājan vicarantaṃ mahāhave
c apaśyāma yathā pūrvaṃ śakrasyāsurasaṃkṣaye
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tataḥ sainyās tava vibho madrarājapuraskṛtāḥ
c punar abhyadravan pārthān vegena mahatā raṇe
a pīḍitās tāvakāḥ sarve pradhāvanto raṇotkaṭāḥ
c kṣaṇenaiva ca pārthāṃs te bahutvāt samaloḍayan
a te vadhyamānāḥ kurubhiḥ pāṇḍavā nāvatasthire
c nivāryamāṇā bhīmena paśyatoḥ kṛṣṇapārthayoḥ
a tato dhanaṃjayaḥ kruddhaḥ kṛpaṃ saha padānugaiḥ
c avākirac charaugheṇa kṛtavarmāṇam eva ca
a śakuniṃ sahadevas tu sahasainyam avārayat
c nakulaḥ pārśvataḥ sthitvā madrarājam avaikṣata
a draupadeyā narendrāṃś ca bhūyiṣṭhaṃ samavārayan
c droṇaputraṃ ca pāñcālyaḥ śikhaṇḍī samavārayat
a bhīmasenas tu rājānaṃ gadāpāṇir avārayat
c śalyaṃ tu saha sainyena kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a tataḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ saṃsaktaṃ tatra tatra ha
c tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca saṃgrāmeṣv anivartinām
a tatra paśyāmahe karma śalyasyātimahad raṇe
c yad ekaḥ sarvasainyāni pāṇḍavānām ayudhyata
a vyadṛśyata tadā śalyo yudhiṣṭhirasamīpataḥ
c raṇe candramaso 'bhyāśe śanaiścara iva grahaḥ
a pīḍayitvā tu rājānaṃ śarair āśīviṣopamaiḥ
c abhyadhāvat punar bhīmaṃ śaravarṣair avākirat
a tasya tal lāghavaṃ dṛṣṭvā tathaiva ca kṛtāstratām
c apūjayann anīkāni pareṣāṃ tāvakāni ca
a pīḍyamānās tu śalyena pāṇḍavā bhṛśavikṣatāḥ
c prādravanta raṇaṃ hitvā krośamāne yudhiṣṭhire
a vadhyamāneṣv anīkeṣu madrarājena pāṇḍavaḥ
c amarṣavaśam āpanno dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
e tataḥ pauruṣam āsthāya madrarājam apīḍayat
a jayo vāstu vadho veti kṛtabuddhir mahārathaḥ
c samāhūyābravīt sarvān bhrātṝn kṛṣṇaṃ ca mādhavam
a bhīṣmo droṇaś ca karṇaś ca ye cānye pṛthivīkṣitaḥ
c kauravārthe parākrāntāḥ saṃgrāme nidhanaṃ gatāḥ
a yathābhāgaṃ yathotsāhaṃ bhavantaḥ kṛtapauruṣāḥ
c bhāgo 'vaśiṣṭa eko 'yaṃ mama śalyo mahārathaḥ
a so 'ham adya yudhā jetum āśaṃse madrakeśvaram
c tatra yan mānasaṃ mahyaṃ tat sarvaṃ nigadāmi vaḥ
a cakrarakṣāv imau śūrau mama mādravatīsutau
c ajeyau vāsavenāpi samare vīrasaṃmatau
a sādhv imau mātulaṃ yuddhe kṣatradharmapuraskṛtau
c madarthaṃ pratiyudhyetāṃ mānārhau satyasaṃgarau
d kiṃ vā pralapitenātha vyarthenānena kiṃ cana
a māṃ vā śalyo raṇe hantā taṃ vāhaṃ bhadram astu vaḥ
c iti satyām imāṃ vāṇīṃ lokavīrā nibodhata
a yotsye 'haṃ mātulenādya kṣatradharmeṇa pārthivāḥ
c svayaṃ samabhisaṃdhāya vijayāyetarāya vā
a tasya me 'bhyadhikaṃ śastraṃ sarvopakaraṇāni ca
c saṃyuñjantu raṇe kṣipraṃ śāstravad rathayojakāḥ
a śaineyo dakṣiṇaṃ cakraṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnas tathottaram
c pṛṣṭhagopo bhavatv adya mama pārtho dhanaṃjayaḥ
a puraḥsaro mamādyāstu bhīmaḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
c evam abhyadhikaḥ śalyād bhaviṣyāmi mahāmṛdhe
a evam uktās tathā cakruḥ sarve rājñaḥ priyaiṣiṇaḥ
c tataḥ praharṣaḥ sainyānāṃ punar āsīt tadā nṛpa
a pāñcālānāṃ somakānāṃ matsyānāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ
c pratijñāṃ tāṃ ca saṃgrāme dharmarājasya pūrayan
d pratijñāṃ tāṃ tadā rājā kṛtvā madreśam abhyayāt
a tataḥ śaṅkhāṃś ca bherīś ca śataśaś caiva puṣkarān
c avādayanta pāñcālāḥ siṃhanādāṃś ca nedire
a te 'bhyadhāvanta saṃrabdhā madrarājaṃ tarasvinaḥ
c mahatā harṣajenātha nādena kurupuṃgavāḥ
a hrādena gajaghaṇṭānāṃ śaṅkhānāṃ ninadena ca
c tūryaśabdena mahatā nādayantaś ca medinīm
a tān pratyagṛhṇāt putras te madrarājaś ca vīryavān
c mahāmeghān iva bahūñ śailāv astodayāv ubhau
a śalyas tu samaraślāghī dharmarājam ariṃdamam
c vavarṣa śaravarṣeṇa varṣeṇa maghavān iva
a tathaiva kururājo 'pi pragṛhya ruciraṃ dhanuḥ
c droṇopadeśān vividhān darśayāno mahāmanāḥ
d saṃdadhe vividhān bāṇān darśayan hastalāghavam
a vavarṣa śaravarṣāṇi citraṃ laghu ca suṣṭhu ca
c na cāsya vivaraṃ kaś cid dadarśa carato raṇe
a tāv ubhau vividhair bāṇais tatakṣāte parasparam
c śārdūlāv āmiṣaprepsū parākrāntāv ivāhave
a bhīmas tu tava putreṇa raṇaśauṇḍena saṃgataḥ
c pāñcālyaḥ sātyakiś caiva mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavau
e śakunipramukhān vīrān pratyagṛhṇan samantataḥ
a tadāsīt tumulaṃ yuddhaṃ punar eva jayaiṣiṇām
c tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca rājan durmantrite tava
a duryodhanas tu bhīmasya śareṇānataparvaṇā
c cicchedādiśya saṃgrāme dhvajaṃ hemavibhūṣitam
a sakiṅkiṇīkajālena mahatā cārudarśanaḥ
c papāta ruciraḥ siṃho bhīmasenasya nānadan
a punaś cāsya dhanuś citraṃ gajarājakaropamam
c kṣureṇa śitadhāreṇa pracakarta narādhipaḥ
a sa cchinnadhanvā tejasvī rathaśaktyā sutaṃ tava
c bibhedorasi vikramya sa rathopastha āviśat
a tasmin moham anuprāpte punar eva vṛkodaraḥ
c yantur eva śiraḥ kāyāt kṣurapreṇāharat tadā
a hatasūtā hayās tasya ratham ādāya bhārata
c vyadravanta diśo rājan hāhākāras tadābhavat
a tam abhyadhāvat trāṇārthaṃ droṇaputro mahārathaḥ
c kṛpaś ca kṛtavarmā ca putraṃ te 'bhiparīpsavaḥ
a tasmin vilulite sainye trastās tasya padānugāḥ
c gāṇḍīvadhanvā visphārya dhanus tān ahanac charaiḥ
a yudhiṣṭhiras tu madreśam abhyadhāvad amarṣitaḥ
c svayaṃ saṃcodayann aśvān dantavarṇān manojavān
a tatrādbhutam apaśyāma kuntīputre yudhiṣṭhire
c purā bhūtvā mṛdur dānto yat tadā dāruṇo 'bhavat
a vivṛtākṣaś ca kaunteyo vepamānaś ca manyunā
c ciccheda yodhān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ śatasahasraśaḥ
a yāṃ yāṃ pratyudyayau senāṃ tāṃ tāṃ jyeṣṭhaḥ sa pāṇḍavaḥ
c śarair apātayad rājan girīn vajrair ivottamaiḥ
a sāśvasūtadhvajarathān rathinaḥ pātayan bahūn
c ākrīḍad eko balavān pavanas toyadān iva
a sāśvārohāṃś ca turagān pattīṃś caiva sahasraśaḥ
c vyapothayata saṃgrāme kruddho rudraḥ paśūn iva
a śūnyam āyodhanaṃ kṛtvā śaravarṣaiḥ samantataḥ
c abhyadravata madreśaṃ tiṣṭha śalyeti cābravīt
a tasya tac caritaṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃgrāme bhīmakarmaṇaḥ
c vitresus tāvakāḥ sarve śalyas tv enaṃ samabhyayāt
a tatas tau tu susaṃrabdhau pradhmāpya salilodbhavau
c samāhūya tadānyonyaṃ bhartsayantau samīyatuḥ
a śalyas tu śaravarṣeṇa yudhiṣṭhiram avākirat
c madrarājaṃ ca kaunteyaḥ śaravarṣair avākirat
a vyadṛśyetāṃ tadā rājan kaṅkapatribhir āhave
c udbhinnarudhirau śūrau madrarājayudhiṣṭhirau
a puṣpitāv iva rejāte vane śalmalikiṃśukā
b puṣpitau śuśubhāte tau vasante kiṃśukau yathā
c dīpyamānau mahātmānau prāṇayor yuddhadurmadau
a dṛṣṭvā sarvāṇi sainyāni nādhyavasyaṃs tayor jayam
c hatvā madrādhipaṃ pārtho bhokṣyate 'dya vasuṃdharām
a śalyo vā pāṇḍavaṃ hatvā dadyād duryodhanāya gām
c itīva niścayo nābhūd yodhānāṃ tatra bhārata
a pradakṣiṇam abhūt sarvaṃ dharmarājasya yudhyataḥ
a tataḥ śaraśataṃ śalyo mumocāśu yudhiṣṭhire
c dhanuś cāsya śitāgreṇa bāṇena nirakṛntata
a so 'nyat kārmukam ādāya śalyaṃ śaraśatais tribhiḥ
c avidhyat kārmukaṃ cāsya kṣureṇa nirakṛntata
a athāsya nijaghānāśvāṃś caturo nataparvabhiḥ
c dvābhyām atha śitāgrābhyām ubhau ca pārṣṇisārathī
a tato 'sya dīpyamānena pītena niśitena ca
c pramukhe vartamānasya bhallenāpāharad dhvajam
e tataḥ prabhagnaṃ tat sainyaṃ dauryodhanam ariṃdama
a tato madrādhipaṃ drauṇir abhyadhāvat tathākṛtam
c āropya cainaṃ svarathaṃ tvaramāṇaḥ pradudruve
a muhūrtam iva tau gatvā nardamāne yudhiṣṭhire
c sthitvā tato madrapatir anyaṃ syandanam āsthitaḥ
a vidhivat kalpitaṃ śubhraṃ mahāmbudaninādinam
c sajjayantropakaraṇaṃ dviṣatāṃ romaharṣaṇam
d sukūbaraṃ sucakrākṣaṃ vidheyāśvaṃ susārathim
 saṃjaya uvāca
a athānyad dhanur ādāya balavad vegavattaram
c yudhiṣṭhiraṃ madrapatir viddhvā siṃha ivānadat
a tataḥ sa śaravarṣeṇa parjanya iva vṛṣṭimān
c abhyavarṣad ameyātmā kṣatriyān kṣatriyarṣabhaḥ
a sātyakiṃ daśabhir viddhvā bhīmasenaṃ tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
c sahadevaṃ tribhir viddhvā yudhiṣṭhiram apīḍayat
a tāṃs tān anyān maheṣvāsān sāśvān sarathakuñjarān
b ardayām āsa viśikhair ulkābhir iva kuñjarān
c kuñjarān kuñjarārohān aśvān aśvaprayāyinaḥ
e rathāṃś ca rathibhiḥ sārdhaṃ jaghāna rathināṃ varaḥ
a bāhūṃś ciccheda ca tathā sāyudhān ketanāni ca
c cakāra ca mahīṃ yodhais tīrṇāṃ vedīṃ kuśair iva
a tathā tam arisainyāni ghnantaṃ mṛtyum ivāntakam
c parivavrur bhṛśaṃ kruddhāḥ pāṇḍupāñcālasomakāḥ
a taṃ bhīmasenaś ca śineś ca naptā
mādryāś ca putrau puruṣapravīrau
c samāgataṃ bhīmabalena rājñā
paryāpur anyonyam athāhvayantaḥ
a tatas tu śūrāḥ samare narendraṃ
madreśvaraṃ prāpya yudhāṃ variṣṭham
c āvārya cainaṃ samare nṛvīrā
jaghnuḥ śaraiḥ patribhir ugravegaiḥ
a saṃrakṣito bhīmasenena rājā
mādrīsutābhyām atha mādhavena
c madrādhipaṃ patribhir ugravegaiḥ
stanāntare dharmasuto nijaghne
a tato raṇe tāvakānāṃ rathaughāḥ
samīkṣya madrādhipatiṃ śarārtam
c paryāvavruḥ pravarāḥ sarvaśaś ca
duryodhanasyānumate samantāt
a tato drutaṃ madrajanādhipo raṇe
yudhiṣṭhiraṃ saptabhir abhyavidhyat
c taṃ cāpi pārtho navabhiḥ pṛṣatkair
vivyādha rājaṃs tumule mahātmā
a ākarṇapūrṇāyatasaṃprayuktaiḥ
śarais tadā saṃyati tailadhautaiḥ
c anyonyam ācchādayatāṃ mahārathau
madrādhipaś cāpi yudhiṣṭhiraś ca
a tatas tu tūrṇaṃ samare mahārathau
parasparasyāntaram īkṣamāṇau
c śarair bhṛśaṃ vivyadhatur nṛpottamau
mahābalau śatrubhir apradhṛṣyau
a tayor dhanurjyātalanisvano mahān
mahendravajrāśanitulyanisvanaḥ
c parasparaṃ bāṇagaṇair mahātmanoḥ
pravarṣator madrapapāṇḍuvīrayoḥ
a tau ceratur vyāghraśiśuprakāśau
mahāvaneṣv āmiṣagṛddhināv iva
c viṣāṇinau nāgavarāv ivobhau
tatakṣatuḥ saṃyugajātadarpau
a tatas tu madrādhipatir mahātmā
yudhiṣṭhiraṃ bhīmabalaṃ prasahya
c vivyādha vīraṃ hṛdaye 'tivegaṃ
śareṇa sūryāgnisamaprabheṇa
a tato 'tividdho 'tha yudhiṣṭhiro 'pi
susaṃprayuktena śareṇa rājan
b tataḥ sa viddho vidhidharmasūnunā
b mahābalenendraparākrameṇa
c jaghāna madrādhipatiṃ mahātmā
mudaṃ ca lebhe ṛṣabhaḥ kurūṇām
a tato muhūrtād iva pārthivendro
labdhvā saṃjñāṃ krodhasaṃraktanetraḥ
c śatena pārthaṃ tvarito jaghāna
sahasranetrapratimaprabhāvaḥ
a tvaraṃs tato dharmasuto mahātmā
śalyasya kruddho navabhiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ
c bhittvā hy uras tapanīyaṃ ca varma
jaghāna ṣaḍbhis tv aparaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ
a tatas tu madrādhipatiḥ prahṛṣṭo
dhanur vikṛṣya vyasṛjat pṛṣatkān
c dvābhyāṃ kṣurābhyāṃ ca tathaiva rājñaś
ciccheda cāpaṃ kurupuṃgavasya
a navaṃ tato 'nyat samare pragṛhya
rājā dhanur ghorataraṃ mahātmā
c śalyaṃ tu viddhvā niśitaiḥ samantād
yathā mahendro namuciṃ śitāgraiḥ
a tatas tu śalyo navabhiḥ pṛṣatkair
bhīmasya rājñaś ca yudhiṣṭhirasya
c nikṛtya raukme paṭuvarmaṇī tayor
vidārayām āsa bhujau mahātmā
a tato 'pareṇa jvalitārkatejasā
kṣureṇa rājño dhanur unmamātha
c kṛpaś ca tasyaiva jaghāna sūtaṃ
ṣaḍbhiḥ śaraiḥ so 'bhimukhaṃ papāta
a madrādhipaś cāpi yudhiṣṭhirasya
śaraiś caturbhir nijaghāna vāhān
c vāhāṃś ca hatvā vyakaron mahātmā
yodhakṣayaṃ dharmasutasya rājñaḥ
d yad adbhutaṃ karma na śakyam anyaiḥ
d suduḥsahaṃ tat kṛtavantam ekam
d śalyaṃ narendraḥ sa viṣaṇṇabhāvād
d vicintayām āsa mṛdaṅgaketuḥ
d kim etad indrāvarajasya vākyaṃ
d moghaṃ bhavaty adya vidher balena
d jahīti śalyaṃ hy avadat tadājau
d na lokanāthasya vaco 'nyathā syāt
a tathā kṛte rājani bhīmaseno
madrādhipasyāśu tato mahātmā
c chittvā dhanur vegavatā śareṇa
dvābhyām avidhyat subhṛśaṃ narendram
a athāpareṇāsya jahāra yantuḥ
kāyāc chiraḥ saṃnahanīyamadhyāt
c jaghāna cāśvāṃś caturaḥ sa śīghraṃ
tathā bhṛśaṃ kupito bhīmasenaḥ
a tam agraṇīḥ sarvadhanurdharāṇām
ekaṃ carantaṃ samare 'tivegam
c bhīmaḥ śatena vyakirac charāṇāṃ
mādrīputraḥ sahadevas tathaiva
a taiḥ sāyakair mohitaṃ vīkṣya śalyaṃ
bhīmaḥ śarair asya cakarta varma
b bhīmaḥ śarair niśitais tigmatejaiḥ
b śilīmukhair asya cakarta varma
c sa bhīmasenena nikṛttavarmā
madrādhipaś carma sahasratāram
a pragṛhya khaḍgaṃ ca rathān mahātmā
praskandya kuntīsutam abhyadhāvat
c chittvā ratheṣāṃ nakulasya so 'tha
yudhiṣṭhiraṃ bhīmabalo 'bhyadhāvat
a taṃ cāpi rājānam athotpatantaṃ
kruddhaṃ yathaivāntakam āpatantam
c dhṛṣṭadyumno draupadeyāḥ śikhaṇḍī
śineś ca naptā sahasā parīyuḥ
a athāsya carmāpratimaṃ nyakṛntad
bhīmo mahātmā daśabhiḥ pṛṣatkaḥ
c khaḍgaṃ ca bhallair nicakarta muṣṭau
nadan prahṛṣṭas tava sainyamadhye
a tat karma bhīmasya samīkṣya hṛṣṭās
te pāṇḍavānāṃ pravarā rathaughāḥ
c nādaṃ ca cakrur bhṛśam utsmayantaḥ
śaṅkhāṃś ca dadhmuḥ śaśisaṃnikāśān
a tenātha śabdena vibhīṣaṇena
tavābhitaptaṃ balam aprahṛṣṭam
c svedābhibhūtaṃ rudhirokṣitāṅgaṃ
visaṃjñakalpaṃ ca tathā viṣaṇṇam
a sa madrarājaḥ sahasāvakīrṇo
bhīmāgragaiḥ pāṇḍavayodhamukhyaiḥ
c yudhiṣṭhirasyābhimukhaṃ javena
siṃho yathā mṛgahetoḥ prayātaḥ
a sa dharmarājo nihatāśvasūtaṃ
krodhena dīptajvalanaprakāśam
c dṛṣṭvā tu madrādhipatiṃ sa tūrṇaṃ
samabhyadhāvat tam ariṃ balena
a govindavākyaṃ tvaritaṃ vicintya
dadhre matiṃ śalyavināśanāya
c sa dharmarājo nihatāśvasūte
rathe tiṣṭhañ śaktim evābhikāṅkṣan
a tac cāpi śalyasya niśamya karma
mahātmano bhāgam athāvaśiṣṭam
c smṛtvā manaḥ śalyavadhe yatātmā
yathoktam indrāvarajasya cakre
a sa dharmarājo maṇihemadaṇḍāṃ
jagrāha śaktiṃ kanakaprakāśām
c netre ca dīpte sahasā vivṛtya
madrādhipaṃ kruddhamanā niraikṣat
a nirīkṣito vai naradeva rājñā
pūtātmanā nirhṛtakalmaṣeṇa
c abhūn na yad bhasmasān madrarājas
tad adbhutaṃ me pratibhāti rājan
a tatas tu śaktiṃ rucirogradaṇḍāṃ
maṇipravālojjvalitāṃ pradīptām
c cikṣepa vegāt subhṛśaṃ mahātmā
madrādhipāya pravaraḥ kurūṇām
a dīptām athaināṃ mahatā balena
savisphuliṅgāṃ sahasā patantīm
c praikṣanta sarve kuravaḥ sametā
yathā yugānte mahatīm ivolkām
a tāṃ kālarātrīm iva pāśahastāṃ
yamasya dhātrīm iva cograrūpām
c sabrahmadaṇḍapratimām amoghāṃ
sasarja yatto yudhi dharmarājaḥ
a gandhasrag agryāsanapānabhojanair
abhyarcitāṃ pāṇḍusutaiḥ prayatnāt
c saṃvartakāgnipratimāṃ jvalantīṃ
kṛtyām atharvāṅgirasīm ivogrām
a īśānahetoḥ pratinirmitāṃ tāṃ
tvaṣṭrā ripūṇām asudehabhakṣām
c bhūmyantarikṣādijalāśayāni
prasahya bhūtāni nihantum īśām
a ghaṇṭāpatākāmaṇivajrabhājaṃ
vaiḍūryacitrāṃ tapanīyadaṇḍām
c tvaṣṭrā prayatnān niyamena kḷptāṃ
brahmadviṣām antakarīm amoghām
a balaprayatnād adhirūḍhavegāṃ
mantraiś ca ghorair abhimantrayitvā
c sasarja mārgeṇa ca tāṃ pareṇa
vadhāya madrādhipates tadānīm
a hato 'sy asāv ity abhigarjamāno
rudro 'ntakāyāntakaraṃ yatheṣum
c prasārya bāhuṃ sudṛḍhaṃ supāṇiṃ
krodhena nṛtyann iva dharmarājaḥ
d sphuratprabhāmaṇḍalam aṃśujālair
d dharmātmajo madravināśakāle
d puratrayaproddharaṇe purastān
d māheśvaraṃ rūpam abhūt tadānīm
d āvartanākuñcitabāhudaṇḍaḥ
d saṃdhyāvihārī tanuvṛttamadhyaḥ
d viśālavakṣā bhagavān haro yathā
d sudurnirīkṣyo 'bhavad arjunāgrajaḥ
a tāṃ sarvaśaktyā prahitāṃ sa śaktiṃ
yudhiṣṭhireṇāprativāryavīryām
c pratigrahāyābhinanarda śalyaḥ
samyag ghutām agnir ivājyadhārām
a sā tasya marmāṇi vidārya śubhram
uro viśālaṃ ca tathaiva varma
c viveśa gāṃ toyam ivāprasaktā
yaśo viśālaṃ nṛpater dahantī
a nāsākṣikarṇāsyaviniḥsṛtena
prasyandatā ca vraṇasaṃbhavena
c saṃsiktagātro rudhireṇa so 'bhūt
krauñco yathā skandahato mahādriḥ
a prasārya bāhū sa rathād gato gāṃ
saṃchinnavarmā kurunandanena
c mahendravāhapratimo mahātmā
vajrāhataṃ śṛṅgam ivācalasya
a bāhū prasāryābhimukho dharmarājasya madrarāṭ
b bāhū prasāryābhimukho 'titūrṇaṃ
b sa dharmarājasya samīpamadradrirāṭ
c tato nipatito bhūmāv indradhvaja ivocchritaḥ
a sa tathā bhinnasarvāṅgo rudhireṇa samukṣitaḥ
c pratyudgata iva premṇā bhūmyā sa narapuṃgavaḥ
a priyayā kāntayā kāntaḥ patamāna ivorasi
c ciraṃ bhuktvā vasumatīṃ priyāṃ kāntām iva prabhuḥ
e sarvair aṅgaiḥ samāśliṣya prasupta iva so 'bhavat
a dharmye dharmātmanā yuddhe nihato dharmasūnunā
c samyag ghuta iva sviṣṭaḥ praśānto 'gnir ivādhvare
a śaktyā vibhinnahṛdayaṃ vipraviddhāyudhadhvajam
c saṃśāntam api madreśaṃ lakṣmīr naiva vyamuñcata
a tato yudhiṣṭhiraś cāpam ādāyendradhanuṣprabham
c vyadhamad dviṣataḥ saṃkhye khagarāḍ iva pannagān
e dehāsūn niśitair bhallai ripūṇāṃ nāśayan kṣaṇāt
a tataḥ pārthasya bāṇaughair āvṛtāḥ sainikās tava
c nimīlitākṣāḥ kṣiṇvanto bhṛśam anyonyam arditāḥ
e saṃnyastakavacā dehair vipatrāyudhajīvitāḥ
a tataḥ śalye nipatite madrarājānujo yuvā
c bhrātuḥ sarvair guṇais tulyo rathī pāṇḍavam abhyayāt
a vivyādha ca naraśreṣṭho nārācair bahubhis tvaran
c hatasyāpacitiṃ bhrātuś cikīrṣur yuddhadurmadaḥ
a taṃ vivyādhāśugaiḥ ṣaḍbhir dharmarājas tvarann iva
c kārmukaṃ cāsya ciccheda kṣurābhyāṃ dhvajam eva ca
a tato 'sya dīpyamānena sudṛḍhena śitena ca
c pramukhe vartamānasya bhallenāpāharac chiraḥ
d śiraś ciccheda bāṇena bhallena nataparvaṇā
a sakuṇḍalaṃ tad dadṛśe patamānaṃ śiro rathāt
c puṇyakṣayam iva prāpya patantaṃ svargavāsinam
a tasyāpakṛṣṭaśīrṣaṃ tac charīraṃ patitaṃ rathāt
c rudhireṇāvasiktāṅgaṃ dṛṣṭvā sainyam abhajyata
a vicitrakavace tasmin hate madranṛpānuje
c hāhākāraṃ vikurvāṇāḥ kuravo vipradudruvuḥ
a śalyānujaṃ hataṃ dṛṣṭvā tāvakās tyaktajīvitāḥ
c vitresuḥ pāṇḍavabhayād rajodhvastās tathā bhṛśam
a tāṃs tathā bhajyatas trastān kauravān bharatarṣabha
b tat sainyaṃ tava putrasya vidrutaṃ sarvato bhayāt
c śiner naptā kiran bāṇair abhyavartata sātyakiḥ
a tam āyāntaṃ maheṣvāsam aprasahyaṃ durāsadam
c hārdikyas tvarito rājan pratyagṛhṇād abhītavat
a tau sametau mahātmānau vārṣṇeyāv aparājitau
c hārdikyaḥ sātyakiś caiva siṃhāv iva madotkaṭau
a iṣubhir vimalābhāsaiś chādayantau parasparam
c arcirbhir iva sūryasya divākarasamaprabhau
a cāpamārgabaloddhūtān mārgaṇān vṛṣṇisiṃhayoḥ
c ākāśe samapaśyāma pataṃgān iva śīghragān
a sātyakiṃ daśabhir viddhvā hayāṃś cāsya tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
c cāpam ekena ciccheda hārdikyo nataparvaṇā
a tan nikṛttaṃ dhanuḥ śreṣṭham apāsya śinipuṃgavaḥ
c anyad ādatta vegena vegavattaram āyudham
a tad ādāya dhanuḥ śreṣṭhaṃ variṣṭhaḥ sarvadhanvinām
c hārdikyaṃ daśabhir bāṇaiḥ pratyavidhyat stanāntare
a tato rathaṃ yugeṣāṃ ca chittvā bhallaiḥ susaṃyataiḥ
c aśvāṃs tasyāvadhīt tūrṇam ubhau ca pārṣṇisārathī
d hārdikyaṃ virathaṃ dṛṣṭvā kṛpaḥ śāradvataḥ prabho
d apovāha tataḥ kṣipraṃ ratham āropya vīryavān
a madrarāje hate rājan virathe kṛtavarmaṇi
c duryodhanabalaṃ sarvaṃ punar āsīt parāṅmukham
a tatpare nāvabudhyanta sainyena rajasā vṛte
c balaṃ tu hatabhūyiṣṭhaṃ tat tadāsīt parāṅmukham
a tato muhūrtāt te 'paśyan rajo bhaumaṃ samutthitam
c vividhaiḥ śoṇitasrāvaiḥ praśāntaṃ puruṣarṣabha
d vividhān saritaś coghāñ śoṇitasya viśāṃ pate
a tato duryodhano dṛṣṭvā bhagnaṃ svabalam antikāt
c javenāpatataḥ pārthān ekaḥ sarvān avārayat
a pāṇḍavān sarathān dṛṣṭvā dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca pārṣatam
c ānartaṃ ca durādharṣaṃ śitair bāṇair avākirat
a taṃ pare nābhyavartanta martyā mṛtyum ivāgatam
c athānyaṃ ratham āsthāya hārdikyo 'pi nyavartata
d pragṛhya ca dhanur ghoram abhyadhāvad yudhiṣṭhiram
a tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā tvaramāṇo mahārathaḥ
c caturbhir nijaghānāśvān patribhiḥ kṛtavarmaṇaḥ
e vivyādha gautamaṃ cāpi ṣaḍbhir bhallaiḥ sutejanaiḥ
a aśvatthāmā tato rājñā hatāśvaṃ virathīkṛtam
c samapovāha hārdikyaṃ svarathena yudhiṣṭhirāt
a tataḥ śāradvato 'ṣṭābhiḥ pratyavidhyad yudhiṣṭhiram
c vivyādha cāśvān niśitais tasyāṣṭābhiḥ śilīmukhaiḥ
a evam etan mahārāja yuddhaśeṣam avartata
c tava durmantrite rājan sahaputrasya bhārata
a tasmin maheṣvāsavare viśaste
saṃgrāmamadhye kurupuṃgavena
c pārthāḥ sametāḥ paramaprahṛṣṭāḥ
śaṅkhān pradadhmur hatam īkṣya śalyam
a yudhiṣṭhiraṃ ca praśaśaṃsur ājau
purā surā vṛtravadhe yathendram
c cakruś ca nānāvidhavādyaśabdān
ninādayanto vasudhāṃ samantāt
 saṃjaya uvāca
a śalye tu nihate rājan madrarājapadānugāḥ
c rathāḥ saptaśatā vīrā niryayur mahato balāt
a duryodhanas tu dviradam āruhyācalasaṃnibham
c chatreṇa dhriyamāṇena vījyamānaś ca cāmaraiḥ
e na gantavyaṃ na gantavyam iti madrān avārayat
a duryodhanena te vīrā vāryamāṇāḥ punaḥ punaḥ
c yudhiṣṭhiraṃ jighāṃsantaḥ pāṇḍūnāṃ prāviśan balam
a te tu śūrā mahārāja kṛtacittāḥ sma yodhane
c dhanuḥśabdaṃ mahat kṛtvā sahāyudhyanta pāṇḍavaiḥ
a śrutvā tu nihataṃ śalyaṃ dharmaputraṃ ca pīḍitam
c madrarājapriye yuktair madrakāṇāṃ mahārathaiḥ
a ājagāma tataḥ pārtho gāṇḍīvaṃ vikṣipan dhanuḥ
c pūrayan rathaghoṣeṇa diśaḥ sarvā mahārathaḥ
a tato 'rjunaś ca bhīmaś ca mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavau
c sātyakiś ca naravyāghro draupadeyāś ca sarvaśaḥ
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca pāñcālāḥ saha somakaiḥ
c yudhiṣṭhiraṃ parīpsantaḥ samantāt paryavārayan
a te samantāt parivṛtāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ puruṣarṣabhāḥ
c kṣobhayanti sma tāṃ senāṃ makarāḥ sāgaraṃ yathā
a purovātena gaṅgeva kṣobhyamānā mahānadī
c akṣobhyata tadā rājan pāṇḍūnāṃ dhvajinī punaḥ
a praskandya senāṃ mahatīṃ tyaktātmāno mahārathāḥ
c vṛkṣān iva mahāvātāḥ kampayanti sma tāvakāḥ
a bahavaś cukruśus tatra kva sa rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c bhrātaro vāsya te śūrā dṛśyante neha ke cana
a pāñcālānāṃ mahāvīryāḥ śikhaṇḍī ca mahārathaḥ
c dhṛṣṭadyumno 'tha śaineyo draupadeyāś ca sarvaśaḥ
a evaṃ tān vādinaḥ śūrān draupadeyā mahārathāḥ
c abhyaghnan yuyudhānaś ca madrarājapadānugān
a cakrair vimathitaiḥ ke cit ke cic chinnair mahādhvajaiḥ
c pratyadṛśyanta samare tāvakā nihatāḥ paraiḥ
a ālokya pāṇḍavān yuddhe yodhā rājan samantataḥ
c vāryamāṇā yayur vegāt tava putreṇa bhārata
a duryodhanas tu tān vīrān vārayām āsa sāntvayan
c na cāsya śāsanaṃ kaś cit tatra cakre mahārathaḥ
a tato gāndhārarājasya putraḥ śakunir abravīt
c duryodhanaṃ mahārāja vacanaṃ vacanakṣamaḥ
a kiṃ naḥ saṃprekṣamāṇānāṃ madrāṇāṃ hanyate balam
c na yuktam etat samare tvayi tiṣṭhati bhārata
a sahitair nāma yoddhavyam ity eṣa samayaḥ kṛtaḥ
c atha kasmāt parān eva ghnato marṣayase nṛpa
 duryodhana uvāca
a vāryamāṇā mayā pūrvaṃ naite cakrur vaco mama
c ete hi nihatāḥ sarve praskannāḥ pāṇḍuvāhinīm
 śakunir uvāca
 vāryamāṇo sic
mayā pūrvaṃ na kṛtaṃ vacanaṃ tvayā
a na bhartuḥ śāsanaṃ vīrā raṇe kurvanty amarṣitāḥ
c alaṃ kroddhuṃ tathaiteṣāṃ nāyaṃ kāla upekṣitum
a yāmaḥ sarve 'tra saṃbhūya savājirathakuñjarāḥ
c paritrātuṃ maheṣvāsān madrarājapadānugān
a anyonyaṃ parirakṣāmo yatnena mahatā nṛpa
c evaṃ sarve 'nusaṃcintya prayayur yatra sainikāḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a evam uktas tato rājā balena mahatā vṛtaḥ
c prayayau siṃhanādena kampayan vai vasuṃdharām
a hata vidhyata gṛhṇīta praharadhvaṃ nikṛntata
c ity āsīt tumulaḥ śabdas tava sainyasya bhārata
a pāṇḍavās tu raṇe dṛṣṭvā madrarājapadānugān
b paśyatāṃ tava putrāṇāṃ pāṇḍuputrair asaṃbhramam
c sahitān abhyavartanta gulmam āsthāya madhyamam
a te muhūrtād raṇe vīrā hastāhastaṃ viśāṃ pate
c nihatāḥ pratyadṛśyanta madrarājapadānugāḥ
a tato naḥ saṃprayātānāṃ hatāmitrās tarasvinaḥ
c hṛṣṭāḥ kilakilāśabdam akurvan sahitāḥ pare
a athotthitāni ruṇḍāni samadṛśyanta sarvaśaḥ
c papāta mahatī colkā madhyenādityamaṇḍalam
a rathair bhagnair yugākṣaiś ca nihataiś ca mahārathaiḥ
c aśvair nipatitaiś caiva saṃchannābhūd vasuṃdharā
a vātāyamānais turagair yugāsaktais turaṃgamaiḥ
c adṛśyanta mahārāja yodhās tatra raṇājire
a bhagnacakrān rathān ke cid avahaṃs turagā raṇe
c rathārdhaṃ ke cid ādāya diśo daśa vibabhramuḥ
e tatra tatra ca dṛśyante yoktraiḥ śliṣṭāḥ sma vājinaḥ
a rathinaḥ patamānāś ca vyadṛśyanta narottama
c gaganāt pracyutāḥ siddhāḥ puṇyānām iva saṃkṣaye
a nihateṣu ca śūreṣu madrarājānugeṣu ca
c asmān āpatataś cāpi dṛṣṭvā pārthā mahārathāḥ
a abhyavartanta vegena jayagṛdhrāḥ prahāriṇaḥ
c bāṇaśabdaravān kṛtvā vimiśrāñ śaṅkhanisvanaiḥ
a asmāṃs tu punar āsādya labdhalakṣāḥ prahāriṇaḥ
c śarāsanāni dhunvānāḥ siṃhanādān pracukruśuḥ
a tato hatam abhiprekṣya madrarājabalaṃ mahat
c madrarājaṃ ca samare dṛṣṭvā śūraṃ nipātitam
e duryodhanabalaṃ sarvaṃ punar āsīt parāṅmukham
a vadhyamānaṃ mahārāja pāṇḍavair jitakāśibhiḥ
c diśo bheje 'tha saṃbhrāntaṃ trāsitaṃ dṛḍhadhanvibhiḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a pātite yudhi durdharṣe madrarāje mahārathe
c tāvakās tava putrāś ca prāyaśo vimukhābhavan
a vaṇijo nāvi bhinnāyāṃ yathāgādhe 'plave 'rṇave
c apāre pāram icchanto hate śūre mahātmani
a madrarāje mahārāja vitrastāḥ śaravikṣatāḥ
c anāthā nātham icchanto mṛgāḥ siṃhārditā iva
a vṛṣā yathā bhagnaśṛṅgāḥ śīrṇadantā gajā iva
c madhyāhne pratyapāyāma nirjitā dharmasūnunā
a na saṃdhātum anīkāni na ca rājan parākrame
c āsīd buddhir hate śalye tava yodhasya kasya cit
a bhīṣme droṇe ca nihate sūtaputre ca bhārata
c yad duḥkhaṃ tava yodhānāṃ bhayaṃ cāsīd viśāṃ pate
e tad bhayaṃ sa ca naḥ śoko bhūya evābhyavartata
a nirāśāś ca jaye tasmin hate śalye mahārathe
b nirāśaś ca hate śalye rājā rājan mahāyaśāḥ
c hatapravīrā vidhvastā vikṛttāś ca śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
e madrarāje hate rājan yodhās te prādravan bhayāt
a aśvān anye gajān anye rathān anye mahārathāḥ
c āruhya javasaṃpannāḥ pādātāḥ prādravan bhayāt
a dvisāhasrāś ca mātaṅgā girirūpāḥ prahāriṇaḥ
c saṃprādravan hate śalye aṅkuśāṅguṣṭhacoditāḥ
a te raṇād bharataśreṣṭha tāvakāḥ prādravan diśaḥ
c dhāvantaś cāpy adṛśyanta śvasamānāḥ śarāturāḥ
a tān prabhagnān drutān dṛṣṭvā hatotsāhān parājitān
c abhyadravanta pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavāś ca jayaiṣiṇaḥ
a bāṇaśabdaravaś cāpi siṃhanādaś ca puṣkalaḥ
c śaṅkhaśabdaś ca śūrāṇāṃ dāruṇaḥ samapadyata
a dṛṣṭvā tu kauravaṃ sainyaṃ bhayatrastaṃ pravidrutam
c anyonyaṃ samabhāṣanta pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha
a adya rājā satyadhṛtir jitāmitro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c adya duryodhano hīno dīptayā nṛpatiśriyā
d adya diṣṭyā kṣmāśayanaṃ niratāmāmucakṣuṣaḥ sic
d draupadyā yaś ca saṃkalpaḥ saṃsiddha iti ghuṣyatām
a adya śrutvā hataṃ putraṃ dhṛtarāṣṭro janeśvaraḥ
c niḥsaṃjñaḥ patito bhūmau kilbiṣaṃ pratipadyatām
a adya jānātu kaunteyaṃ samarthaṃ sarvadhanvinām
c adyātmānaṃ ca durmedhā garhayiṣyati pāpakṛt
e adya kṣattur vacaḥ satyaṃ smaratāṃ bruvato hitam
a adyaprabhṛti pārthāṃś ca preṣyabhūta upācaran
b adyaiva ca hi pārthānāṃ yat kṛtaṃ pūrvakarmabhiḥ
c vijānātu nṛpo duḥkhaṃ yat prāptaṃ pāṇḍunandanaiḥ
a adya kṛṣṇasya māhātmyaṃ jānātu sa mahīpatiḥ
c adyārjunadhanurghoṣaṃ ghoraṃ jānātu saṃyuge
d putrāṇāṃ ca vadhaṃ ghoraṃ bhīmena śroṣyate nṛpaḥ
a astrāṇāṃ ca balaṃ sarvaṃ bāhvoś ca balam āhave
c adya jñāsyati bhīmasya balaṃ ghoraṃ mahātmanaḥ
a hate duryodhane yuddhe śakreṇevāsure maye
c yat kṛtaṃ bhīmasenena duḥśāsanavadhe tadā
e nānyaḥ kartāsti loke tad ṛte bhīmaṃ mahābalam
a jānītām adya jyeṣṭhasya pāṇḍavasya parākramam
c madrarājaṃ hataṃ śrutvā devair api suduḥsaham
a adya jñāsyati saṃgrāme mādrīputrau mahābalau
c nihate saubale śūre gāndhāreṣu ca sarvaśaḥ
a kathaṃ teṣāṃ jayo na syād yeṣāṃ yoddhā dhanaṃjayaḥ
c sātyakir bhīmasenaś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥ
a draupadyās tanayāḥ pañca mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavau
c śikhaṇḍī ca maheṣvāso rājā caiva yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a yeṣāṃ ca jagatāṃ nātho nāthaḥ kṛṣṇo janārdanaḥ
c kathaṃ teṣāṃ jayo na syād yeṣāṃ dharmo vyapāśrayaḥ
d lābhas teṣāṃ jayas teṣāṃ kutas teṣāṃ parābhavaḥ
d yeṣāṃ nātho hṛṣīkeśaḥ sarvalokavibhur hariḥ
a bhīṣmaṃ droṇaṃ ca karṇaṃ ca madrarājānam eva ca
c tathānyān nṛpatīn vīrāñ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a ko 'nyaḥ śakto raṇe jetum ṛte pārthaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
c yasya nātho hṛṣīkeśaḥ sadā dharmayaśonidhiḥ
a ity evaṃ vadamānās te harṣeṇa mahatā yutāḥ
c prabhagnāṃs tāvakān rājan sṛñjayāḥ pṛṣṭhato 'nvayuḥ
a dhanaṃjayo rathānīkam abhyavartata vīryavān
c mādrīputrau ca śakuniṃ sātyakiś ca mahārathaḥ
a tān prekṣya dravataḥ sarvān bhīmasenabhayārditān
c duryodhanas tadā sūtam abravīd utsmayann iva
a na mātikramate pārtho dhanuṣpāṇim avasthitam
c jaghane sarvasainyānāṃ mamāśvān pratipādaya
a jaghane yudhyamānaṃ hi kaunteyo māṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ
c notsahetābhyatikrāntuṃ velām iva mahodadhiḥ
a paśya sainyaṃ mahat sūta pāṇḍavaiḥ samabhidrutam
c sainyareṇuṃ samuddhūtaṃ paśyasvainaṃ samantataḥ
a siṃhanādāṃś ca bahuśaḥ śṛṇu ghorān bhayānakān
c tasmād yāhi śanaiḥ sūta jaghanaṃ paripālaya
a mayi sthite ca samare niruddheṣu ca pāṇḍuṣu
c punarāvartate tūrṇaṃ māmakaṃ balam ojasā
a tac chrutvā tava putrasya śūrāgryasadṛśaṃ vacaḥ
c sārathir hemasaṃchannāñ śanair aśvān acodayat
a gajāśvarathibhir hīnās tyaktātmānaḥ padātayaḥ
c ekaviṃśatisāhasrāḥ saṃyugāyāvatasthire
a nānādeśasamudbhūtā nānārañjitavāsasaḥ
c avasthitās tadā yodhāḥ prārthayanto mahad yaśaḥ
a teṣām āpatatāṃ tatra saṃhṛṣṭānāṃ parasparam
c saṃmardaḥ sumahāñ jajñe ghorarūpo bhayānakaḥ
a bhīmasenaṃ tadā rājan dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca pārṣatam
c balena caturaṅgeṇa nānādeśyā nyavārayan
a bhīmam evābhyavartanta raṇe 'nye tu padātayaḥ
c prakṣveḍyāsphoṭya saṃhṛṣṭā vīralokaṃ yiyāsavaḥ
a āsādya bhīmasenaṃ tu saṃrabdhā yuddhadurmadāḥ
c dhārtarāṣṭrā vinedur hi nānyāṃ cākathayan kathām
d nigṛhītuṃ tadā kruddhāḥ samantāt paryavārayan
e parivārya raṇe bhīmaṃ nijaghnus te samantataḥ
a sa vadhyamānaḥ samare padātigaṇasaṃvṛtaḥ
c na cacāla rathopasthe maināka iva parvataḥ
a te tu kruddhā mahārāja pāṇḍavasya mahāratham
c nigrahītuṃ pracakrur hi yodhāṃś cānyān avārayan
a akrudhyata raṇe bhīmas tais tadā paryavasthitaiḥ
c so 'vatīrya rathāt tūrṇaṃ padātiḥ samavasthitaḥ
a jātarūpaparicchannāṃ pragṛhya mahatīṃ gadām
c avadhīt tāvakān yodhān daṇḍapāṇir ivāntakaḥ
a rathāśvadvipahīnāṃs tu tān bhīmo gadayā balī
b viprahīnarathāśvāṃs tān narān sa puruṣarṣabhaḥ
b bhīmaseno gadāpāṇir gadayā vajrakalpayā
c ekaviṃśatisāhasrān padātīn avapothayat
a hatvā tat puruṣānīkaṃ bhīmaḥ satyaparākramaḥ
c dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ puraskṛtya nacirāt pratyadṛśyata
a pādātā nihatā bhūmau śiśyire rudhirokṣitāḥ
c saṃbhagnā iva vātena karṇikārāḥ supuṣpitāḥ
a nānāpuṣpasrajopetā nānākuṇḍaladhāriṇaḥ
c nānājātyā hatās tatra nānādeśasamāgatāḥ
a patākādhvajasaṃchannaṃ padātīnāṃ mahad balam
c nikṛttaṃ vibabhau tatra ghorarūpaṃ bhayānakam
a yudhiṣṭhirapurogās tu sarvasainyamahārathāḥ
c abhyadhāvan mahātmānaṃ putraṃ duryodhanaṃ tava
a te sarve tāvakān dṛṣṭvā maheṣvāsān parāṅmukhān
b samabhyadhāvaṃs tvaritā yuddhāya jitakāśinaḥ
c nābhyavartanta te putraṃ veleva makarālayam
a tad adbhutam apaśyāma tava putrasya pauruṣam
c yad ekaṃ sahitāḥ pārthā na śekur ativartitum
a nātidūrāpayātaṃ tu kṛtabuddhiṃ palāyane
c duryodhanaḥ svakaṃ sainyam abravīd bhṛśavikṣatam
a na taṃ deśaṃ prapaśyāmi pṛthivyāṃ parvateṣu vā
c yatra yātān na vo hanyuḥ pāṇḍavāḥ kiṃ sṛtena vaḥ
a alpaṃ ca balam eteṣāṃ kṛṣṇau ca bhṛśavikṣatau
c yadi sarve 'tra tiṣṭhāmo dhruvo no vijayo bhavet
a viprayātāṃs tu vo bhinnān pāṇḍavāḥ kṛtakilbiṣān
c anusṛtya haniṣyanti śreyo naḥ samare sthitam
a śṛṇudhvaṃ kṣatriyāḥ sarve yāvantaḥ stha samāgatāḥ
c yadā śūraṃ ca bhīruṃ ca mārayaty antakaḥ sadā
e ko nu mūḍho na yudhyeta puruṣaḥ kṣatriyabruvaḥ
a śreyo no bhīmasenasya kruddhasya pramukhe sthitam
c sukhaḥ sāṃgrāmiko mṛtyuḥ kṣatradharmeṇa yudhyatām
d martyenāvaśyamartavyaṃ gṛheṣv api kadā cana
d yudhyataḥ kṣatradharmeṇa mṛtyur eṣa sanātanaḥ
e jitveha sukham āpnoti hataḥ pretya mahat phalam
a na yuddhadharmāc chreyān vai panthāḥ svargasya kauravāḥ
c acireṇa jitāṃl lokān hato yuddhe samaśnute
a śrutvā tu vacanaṃ tasya pūjayitvā ca pārthivāḥ
c punar evānvavartanta pāṇḍavān ātatāyinaḥ
a tān āpatata evāśu vyūḍhānīkāḥ prahāriṇaḥ
c pratyudyayus tadā pārthā jayagṛdhrāḥ prahāriṇaḥ
a dhanaṃjayo rathenājāv abhyavartata vīryavān
c viśrutaṃ triṣu lokeṣu gāṇḍīvaṃ vikṣipan dhanuḥ
a mādrīputrau ca śakuniṃ sātyakiś ca mahābalaḥ
c javenābhyapatan hṛṣṭā yato vai tāvakaṃ balam
 saṃjaya uvāca
a saṃnivṛtte balaughe tu śālvo mlecchagaṇādhipaḥ
c abhyavartata saṃkruddhaḥ pāṇḍūnāṃ sumahad balam
a āsthāya sumahānāgaṃ prabhinnaṃ parvatopamam
c dṛptam airāvataprakhyam amitragaṇamardanam
a yo 'sau mahābhadrakulaprasūtaḥ
supūjito dhārtarāṣṭreṇa nityam
c sukalpitaḥ śāstraviniścayajñaiḥ
sadopavāhyaḥ samareṣu rājan
d airāvataṃ daityagaṇān vimṛdnañ
d śakro yathā saṃjanayan bhayāni
a tam āsthito rājavaro babhūva
yathodayasthaḥ savitā kṣapānte
c sa tena nāgapravareṇa rājann
abhyudyayau pāṇḍusutān samantāt
e śitaiḥ pṛṣatkair vidadāra cāpi
mahendravajrapratimaiḥ sughoraiḥ
a tataḥ śarān vai sṛjato mahāraṇe
yodhāṃś ca rājan nayato yamāya
b tataḥ śarān vai sṛjatā nṛpeṇa
b yodhāḥ samastā gamitā yamālayam
c nāsyāntaraṃ dadṛśuḥ sve pare vā
yathā purā vajradharasya daityāḥ
d airāvaṇasthasya camūvimarde
d daityāḥ purā vāsavasyeva rājan
a te pāṇḍavāḥ somakāḥ sṛñjayāś ca
tam eva nāgaṃ dadṛśuḥ samantāt
c sahasraśo vai vicarantam ekaṃ
yathā mahendrasya gajaṃ samīpe
a saṃdrāvyamāṇaṃ tu balaṃ pareṣāṃ
parītakalpaṃ vibabhau samantāt
c naivāvatasthe samare bhṛśaṃ bhayād
vimardamānaṃ tu parasparaṃ tadā
a tataḥ prabhagnā sahasā mahācamūḥ
sā pāṇḍavī tena narādhipena
c diśaś catasraḥ sahasā pradhāvitā
gajendravegaṃ tam apārayantī
a dṛṣṭvā ca tāṃ vegavatā prabhagnāṃ
sarve tvadīyā yudhi yodhamukhyāḥ
c apūjayaṃs tatra narādhipaṃ taṃ
dadhmuś ca śaṅkhāñ śaśisaṃnikāśān
a śrutvā ninādaṃ tv atha kauravāṇāṃ
harṣād vimuktaṃ saha śaṅkhaśabdaiḥ
c senāpatiḥ pāṇḍavasṛñjayānāṃ
pāñcālaputro na mamarṣa roṣāt
a tatas tu taṃ vai dviradaṃ mahātmā
pratyudyayau tvaramāṇo jayāya
c jambho yathā śakrasamāgame vai
nāgendram airāvaṇam indravāhyam
a tam āpatantaṃ sahasā tu dṛṣṭvā
pāñcālarājaṃ yudhi rājasiṃhaḥ
c taṃ vai dvipaṃ preṣayām āsa tūrṇaṃ
vadhāya rājan drupadātmajasya
a sa taṃ dvipaṃ sahasābhyāpatantam
avidhyad arkapratimaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ
c karmāradhautair niśitair jvaladbhir
nārācamukhyais tribhir ugravegaiḥ
a tato 'parān pañca śitān mahātmā
nārācamukhyān visasarja kumbhe
c sa tais tu viddhaḥ paramadvipo raṇe
tadā parāvṛtya bhṛśaṃ pradudruve
a taṃ nāgarājaṃ sahasā praṇunnaṃ
vidrāvyamāṇaṃ ca nigṛhya śālvaḥ
c tottrāṅkuśaiḥ preṣayām āsa tūrṇaṃ
pāñcālarājasya rathaṃ pradiśya
a dṛṣṭvāpatantaṃ sahasā tu nāgaṃ
dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ svarathāc chīghram eva
c gadāṃ pragṛhyāśu javena vīro
bhūmiṃ prapanno bhayavihvalāṅgaḥ
a sa taṃ rathaṃ hemavibhūṣitāṅgaṃ
sāśvaṃ sasūtaṃ sahasā vimṛdya
c utkṣipya hastena tadā mahādvipo
vipothayām āsa vasuṃdharātale
a pāñcālarājasya sutaṃ sa dṛṣṭvā
tadārditaṃ nāgavareṇa tena
c tam abhyadhāvat sahasā javena
bhīmaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca śineś ca naptā
a śaraiś ca vegaṃ sahasā nigṛhya
tasyābhito 'bhyāpatato gajasya
c sa saṃgṛhīto rathibhir gajo vai
cacāla tair vāryamāṇaś ca saṃkhye
a tataḥ pṛṣatkān pravavarṣa rājā
sūryo yathā raśmijālaṃ samantāt
c tenāśugair vadhyamānā rathaughāḥ
pradudruvus tatra tatas tu sarve
a tat karma śālvasya samīkṣya sarve
pāñcālamatsyā nṛpa sṛñjayāś ca
c hāhākārair nādayantaḥ sma yuddhe
dvipaṃ samantād rurudhur narāgryāḥ
a pāñcālarājas tvaritas tu śūro
gadāṃ pragṛhyācalaśṛṅgakalpām
c asaṃbhramaṃ bhārata śatrughātī
javena vīro 'nusasāra nāgam
a tato 'tha nāgaṃ dharaṇīdharābhaṃ
madaṃ sravantaṃ jaladaprakāśam
c gadāṃ samāvidhya bhṛśaṃ jaghāna
pāñcālarājasya sutas tarasvī
a sa bhinnakumbhaḥ sahasā vinadya
mukhāt prabhūtaṃ kṣatajaṃ vimuñcan
c papāta nāgo dharaṇīdharābhaḥ
kṣitiprakampāc calito yathādriḥ
a nipātyamāne tu tadā gajendre
hāhākṛte tava putrasya sainye
c sa śālvarājasya śinipravīro
jahāra bhallena śiraḥ śitena
a hṛtottamāṅgo yudhi sātvatena
papāta bhūmau saha nāgarājñā
c yathādriśṛṅgaṃ sumahat praṇunnaṃ
vajreṇa devādhipacoditena
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tasmiṃs tu nihate śūre śālve samitiśobhane
c tavābhajyad balaṃ vegād vāteneva mahādrumaḥ
a tat prabhagnaṃ balaṃ dṛṣṭvā kṛtavarmā mahārathaḥ
c dadhāra samare śūraḥ śatrusainyaṃ mahābalaḥ
a saṃnivṛttās tu te śūrā dṛṣṭvā sātvatam āhave
c śailopamaṃ sthitaṃ rājan kīryamāṇaṃ śarair yudhi
a tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha
c nivṛttānāṃ mahārāja mṛtyuṃ kṛtvā nivartanam
a tatrāścaryam abhūd yuddhaṃ sātvatasya paraiḥ saha
c yad eko vārayām āsa pāṇḍusenāṃ durāsadām
a teṣām anyonyasuhṛdāṃ kṛte karmaṇi duṣkare
c siṃhanādaḥ prahṛṣṭānāṃ divaḥspṛk sumahān abhūt
a tena śabdena vitrastān pāñcālān bharatarṣabha
c śiner naptā mahābāhur anvapadyata sātyakiḥ
d śatavarmāṇam atyugraṃ mahāvīraṃ mahābalam
a sa samāsādya rājānaṃ kṣemadhūrtiṃ mahābalam
c saptabhir niśitair bāṇair anayad yamasādanam
a tam āyāntaṃ mahābāhuṃ pravapantaṃ śitāñ śarān
c javenābhyapatad dhīmān hārdikyaḥ śinipuṃgavam
a tau siṃhāv iva nardantau dhanvinau rathināṃ varau
c anyonyam abhyadhāvetāṃ śastrapravaradhāriṇau
a pāṇḍavāḥ saha pāñcālair yodhāś cānye nṛpottamāḥ
c prekṣakāḥ samapadyanta tayoḥ puruṣasiṃhayoḥ
a nārācair vatsadantaiś ca vṛṣṇyandhakamahārathau
c abhijaghnatur anyonyaṃ prahṛṣṭāv iva kuñjarau
a carantau vividhān mārgān hārdikyaśinipuṃgavau
c muhur antardadhāte tau bāṇavṛṣṭyā parasparam
a cāpavegabaloddhūtān mārgaṇān vṛṣṇisiṃhayoḥ
c ākāśe samapaśyāma pataṃgān iva śīghragān
a tam ekaṃ satyakarmāṇam āsādya hṛdikātmajaḥ
c avidhyan niśitair bāṇaiś caturbhiś caturo hayān
a sa dīrghabāhuḥ saṃkruddhas tottrārdita iva dvipaḥ
c aṣṭābhiḥ kṛtavarmāṇam avidhyat parameṣubhiḥ
a tataḥ pūrṇāyatotsṛṣṭaiḥ kṛtavarmā śilāśitaiḥ
c sātyakiṃ tribhir āhatya dhanur ekena cicchide
a nikṛttaṃ tad dhanuḥśreṣṭham apāsya śinipuṃgavaḥ
c anyad ādatta vegena śaineyaḥ saśaraṃ dhanuḥ
a tad ādāya dhanuḥśreṣṭhaṃ variṣṭhaḥ sarvadhanvinām
c āropya ca mahāvīryo mahābuddhir mahābalaḥ
a amṛṣyamāṇo dhanuṣaś chedanaṃ kṛtavarmaṇā
c kupito 'tirathaḥ śīghraṃ kṛtavarmāṇam abhyayāt
a tataḥ suniśitair bāṇair daśabhiḥ śinipuṃgavaḥ
c jaghāna sūtam aśvāṃś ca dhvajaṃ ca kṛtavarmaṇaḥ
a tato rājan maheṣvāsaḥ kṛtavarmā mahārathaḥ
c hatāśvasūtaṃ saṃprekṣya rathaṃ hemapariṣkṛtam
a roṣeṇa mahatāviṣṭaḥ śūlam udyamya māriṣa
c cikṣepa bhujavegena jighāṃsuḥ śinipuṃgavam
a tac chūlaṃ sātvato hy ājau nirbhidya niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c cūrṇitaṃ pātayām āsa mohayann iva mādhavam
e tato 'pareṇa bhallena hṛdy enaṃ samatāḍayat
a sa yuddhe yuyudhānena hatāśvo hatasārathiḥ
c kṛtavarmā kṛtāstreṇa dharaṇīm anvapadyata
a tasmin sātyakinā vīre dvairathe virathīkṛte
c samapadyata sarveṣāṃ sainyānāṃ sumahad bhayam
a putrasya tava cātyarthaṃ viṣādaḥ samapadyata
c hatasūte hatāśve ca virathe kṛtavarmaṇi
a hatāśvaṃ ca samālakṣya hatasūtam ariṃdamam
c abhyadhāvat kṛpo rājañ jighāṃsuḥ śinipuṃgavam
a tam āropya rathopasthe miṣatāṃ sarvadhanvinām
c apovāha mahābāhus tūrṇam āyodhanād api
a śaineye 'dhiṣṭhite rājan virathe kṛtavarmaṇi
c duryodhanabalaṃ sarvaṃ punar āsīt parāṅmukham
a tatpare nāvabudhyanta sainyena rajasāvṛte
c tāvakāḥ pradrutā rājan duryodhanam ṛte nṛpam
a duryodhanas tu saṃprekṣya bhagnaṃ svabalam antikāt
c javenābhyapatat tūrṇaṃ sarvāṃś caiko nyavārayat
a pāṇḍūṃś ca sarvān saṃkruddho dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca pārṣatam
c śikhaṇḍinaṃ draupadeyān pāñcālānāṃ ca ye gaṇāḥ
a kekayān somakāṃś caiva pāñcālāṃś caiva māriṣa
c asaṃbhramaṃ durādharṣaḥ śitair astrair avārayat
a atiṣṭhad āhave yattaḥ putras tava mahābalaḥ
c yathā yajñe mahān agnir mantrapūtaḥ prakāśayan
d tathā duryodhano rājā saṃgrāme sarvato 'bhavat
a taṃ pare nābhyavartanta martyā mṛtyum ivāhave
c athānyaṃ ratham āsthāya hārdikyaḥ samapadyata
 saṃjaya uvāca
a putras tu te mahārāja rathastho rathināṃ varaḥ
b durdharaḥ sa pumān kaś cit pāṇḍavān prati bhārata
c durutsaho babhau yuddhe yathā rudraḥ pratāpavān
a tasya bāṇasahasrais tu pracchannā hy abhavan mahī
c parāṃś ca siṣice bāṇair dhārābhir iva parvatān
a na ca so 'sti pumān kaś cit pāṇḍavānāṃ mahāhave
c hayo gajo ratho vāpi yo 'sya bāṇair avikṣataḥ
a yaṃ yaṃ hi samare yodhaṃ prapaśyāmi viśāṃ pate
c sa sa bāṇaiś cito 'bhūd vai putreṇa tava bhārata
a yathā sainyena rajasā samuddhūtena vāhinī
c pratyadṛśyata saṃchannā tathā bāṇair mahātmanaḥ
a bāṇabhūtām apaśyāma pṛthivīṃ pṛthivīpate
c duryodhanena prakṛtāṃ kṣiprahastena dhanvinā
a teṣu yodhasahasreṣu tāvakeṣu pareṣu ca
c eko duryodhano hy āsīt pumān iti matir mama
a tatrādbhutam apaśyāma tava putrasya vikramam
c yad ekaṃ sahitāḥ pārthā nātyavartanta bhārata
a yudhiṣṭhiraṃ śatenājau vivyādha bharatarṣabha
c bhīmasenaṃ ca saptatyā sahadevaṃ ca saptabhiḥ
a nakulaṃ ca catuḥṣaṣṭyā dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca pañcabhiḥ
c saptabhir draupadeyāṃś ca tribhir vivyādha sātyakim
e dhanuś ciccheda bhallena sahadevasya māriṣa
a tad apāsya dhanuś chinnaṃ mādrīputraḥ pratāpavān
c abhyadhāvata rājānaṃ pragṛhyānyan mahad dhanuḥ
e tato duryodhanaṃ saṃkhye vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ
a nakulaś ca tato vīro rājānaṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
c ghorarūpair maheṣvāso vivyādha ca nanāda ca
a sātyakiś cāpi rājānaṃ śareṇānataparvaṇā
c draupadeyās trisaptatyā dharmarājaś ca saptabhiḥ
e aśītyā bhīmasenaś ca śarai rājānam ārdayat
a samantāt kīryamāṇas tu bāṇasaṃghair mahātmabhiḥ
c na cacāla mahārāja sarvasainyasya paśyataḥ
a lāghavaṃ sauṣṭhavaṃ cāpi vīryaṃ caiva mahātmanaḥ
c ati sarvāṇi bhūtāni dadṛśuḥ sarvamānavāḥ
a dhārtarāṣṭrās tu rājendra yātvā tu svalpam antaram
c apaśyamānā rājānaṃ paryavartanta daṃśitāḥ
a teṣām āpatatāṃ ghoras tumulaḥ samajāyata
c kṣubdhasya hi samudrasya prāvṛṭkāle yathā niśi
a samāsādya raṇe te tu rājānam aparājitam
c pratyudyayur maheṣvāsāḥ pāṇḍavān ātatāyinaḥ
a bhīmasenaṃ raṇe kruddhaṃ droṇaputro nyavārayat
c tato bāṇair mahārāja pramuktaiḥ sarvatodiśam
e nājñāyanta raṇe vīrā na diśaḥ pradiśas tathā
a tāv ubhau krūrakarmāṇāv ubhau bhārata duḥsahau
c ghorarūpam ayudhyetāṃ kṛtapratikṛtaiṣiṇau
e trāsayantau jagat sarvaṃ jyākṣepavihatatvacau
a śakunis tu raṇe vīro yudhiṣṭhiram apīḍayat
c tasyāśvāṃś caturo hatvā subalasya suto vibhuḥ
d yantreṇa hanyamānau tu rathāṅgāv api cicchide
d maṇḍalāgraṃ dhanuś cāpi niśitāṃs tomarān api
d nārācān ardhanārācān supuṇyān mudgarān api
d svarṇadaṇḍāṃ ca śaktiṃ ca bhiṇḍipālān parasvadhān
d nirundhayan satyadhṛtiṃ kṛtvaitat karma dāruṇam
e nādaṃ cakāra balavān sarvasainyāni kampayan
a etasminn antare vīraṃ rājānam aparājitam
c apovāha rathenājau sahadevaḥ pratāpavān
a athānyaṃ ratham āsthāya dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c śakuniṃ navabhir viddhvā punar vivyādha pañcabhiḥ
e nanāda ca mahānādaṃ pravaraḥ sarvadhanvinām
a tad yuddham abhavac citraṃ ghorarūpaṃ ca māriṣa
c īkṣitṛprītijananaṃ siddhacāraṇasevitam
a ulūkas tu maheṣvāsaṃ nakulaṃ yuddhadurmadam
c abhyadravad ameyātmā śaravarṣaiḥ samantataḥ
a tathaiva nakulaḥ śūraḥ saubalasya sutaṃ raṇe
c śaravarṣeṇa mahatā samantāt paryavārayat
a tau tatra samare vīrau kulaputrau mahārathau
c yodhayantāv apaśyetāṃ parasparakṛtāgasau
a tathaiva kṛtavarmā tu śaineyaṃ śatrutāpanam
c yodhayañ śuśubhe rājan balaṃ śakra ivāhave
a duryodhano dhanuś chittvā dhṛṣṭadyumnasya saṃyuge
b pañcabhir niśitais tīkṣṇaiḥ śarair vivyādha marṣayan
c athainaṃ chinnadhanvānaṃ vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a dhṛṣṭadyumno 'pi samare pragṛhya paramāyudham
c rājānaṃ yodhayām āsa paśyatāṃ sarvadhanvinām
a tayor yuddhaṃ mahac cāsīt saṃgrāme bharatarṣabha
c prabhinnayor yathā saktaṃ mattayor varahastinoḥ
a gautamas tu raṇe kruddho draupadeyān mahābalān
c vivyādha bahubhiḥ śūraḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
a tasya tair abhavad yuddham indriyair iva dehinaḥ
c ghorarūpam asaṃvāryaṃ nirmaryādam atīva ca
a te ca taṃ pīḍayām āsur indriyāṇīva bāliśam
c sa ca tān pratisaṃrabdhaḥ pratyayodhayad āhave
a evaṃ citram abhūd yuddhaṃ tasya taiḥ saha bhārata
c utthāyotthāya hi yathā dehinām indriyair vibho
a narāś caiva naraiḥ sārdhaṃ dantino dantibhis tathā
c hayā hayaiḥ samāsaktā rathino rathibhis tathā
e saṃkulaṃ cābhavad bhūyo ghorarūpaṃ viśāṃ pate
a idaṃ citram idaṃ ghoram idaṃ raudram iti prabho
c yuddhāny āsan mahārāja ghorāṇi ca bahūni ca
a te samāsādya samare parasparam ariṃdamāḥ
c vivyadhuś caiva jaghnuś ca samāsādya mahāhave
a teṣāṃ śastrasamudbhūtaṃ rajas tīvram adṛśyata
c pravātenoddhataṃ rājan dhāvadbhiś cāśvasādibhiḥ
a rathanemisamudbhūtaṃ niḥśvāsaiś cāpi dantinām
c rajaḥ saṃdhyābhrakapilaṃ divākarapathaṃ yayau
d ekacchāyam ivākāśaṃ samabhūt tatra dhanvinām
a rajasā tena saṃpṛkte bhāskare niṣprabhīkṛte
c saṃchāditābhavad bhūmis te ca śūrā mahārathāḥ
a muhūrtād iva saṃvṛttaṃ nīrajaskaṃ samantataḥ
c vīraśoṇitasiktāyāṃ bhūmau bharatasattama
e upāśāmyat tatas tīvraṃ tad rajo ghoradarśanam
a tato 'paśyaṃ mahārāja dvaṃdvayuddhāni bhārata
c yathāprāgryaṃ yathājyeṣṭhaṃ madhyāhne vai sudāruṇe
e varmaṇāṃ tatra rājendra vyadṛśyantojjvalāḥ prabhāḥ
a śabdaḥ sutumulaḥ saṃkhye śarāṇāṃ patatām abhūt
c mahāveṇuvanasyeva dahyamānasya sarvataḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a vartamāne tathā yuddhe ghorarūpe bhayānake
c abhajyata balaṃ tatra tava putrasya pāṇḍavaiḥ
a tāṃs tu yatnena mahatā saṃnivārya mahārathān
c putras te yodhayām āsa pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm
a nivṛttāḥ sahasā yodhās tava putrapriyaiṣiṇaḥ
c saṃnivṛtteṣu teṣv evaṃ yuddham āsīt sudāruṇam
a tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca devāsuraraṇopamam
c pareṣāṃ tava sainye ca nāsīt kaś cit parāṅmukhaḥ
a anumānena yudhyante saṃjñābhiś ca parasparam
c teṣāṃ kṣayo mahān āsīd yudhyatām itaretaram
a tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā krodhena mahatā yutaḥ
c jigīṣamāṇaḥ saṃgrāme dhārtarāṣṭrān sarājakān
a tribhiḥ śāradvataṃ viddhvā rukmapuṅkhaiḥ śilāśitaiḥ
c caturbhir nijaghānāśvān kalyāṇān kṛtavarmaṇaḥ
a aśvatthāmā tu hārdikyam apovāha yaśasvinam
c atha śāradvato 'ṣṭābhiḥ pratyavidhyad yudhiṣṭhiram
a tato duryodhano rājā rathān saptaśatān raṇe
c preṣayad yatra rājāsau dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a te rathā rathibhir yuktā manomārutaraṃhasaḥ
c abhyadravanta saṃgrāme kaunteyasya rathaṃ prati
a te samantān mahārāja parivārya yudhiṣṭhiram
c adṛśyaṃ sāyakaiś cakrur meghā iva divākaram
d te dṛṣṭvā dharmarājānaṃ kauravais taṃ tathākṛtam
a nāmṛṣyanta susaṃrabdhāḥ śikhaṇḍipramukhā rathāḥ
c rathair agryajavair yuktaiḥ kiṅkiṇījālasaṃvṛtaiḥ
e ājagmur abhirakṣantaḥ kuntīputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
a tataḥ pravavṛte raudraḥ saṃgrāmaḥ śoṇitodakaḥ
a   devāsuraraṇopamam
a tathānyat sumahac caiva
c pāṇḍavānāṃ kurūṇāṃ ca yamarāṣṭravivardhanaḥ
a rathān saptaśatān hatvā kurūṇām ātatāyinām
c pāṇḍavāḥ saha pāñcālaiḥ punar evābhyavārayan
a tatra yuddhaṃ mahac cāsīt tava putrasya pāṇḍavaiḥ
c na ca nas tādṛśaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ naiva cāpi pariśrutam
a vartamāne tathā yuddhe nirmaryāde samantataḥ
c vadhyamāneṣu yodheṣu tāvakeṣv itareṣu ca
a ninadatsu ca yodheṣu śaṅkhavaryaiś ca pūritaiḥ
b jyāghoṣair yodhamukhyānāṃ talaghoṣaiḥ samaṃtataḥ
c utkṛṣṭaiḥ siṃhanādaiś ca garjitena ca dhanvinām
a atipravṛddhe yuddhe ca chidyamāneṣu marmasu
c dhāvamāneṣu yodheṣu jayagṛddhiṣu māriṣa
a saṃhāre sarvato jāte pṛthivyāṃ śokasaṃbhave
c bahvīnām uttamastrīṇāṃ sīmantoddharaṇe tathā
a nirmaryāde tathā yuddhe vartamāne sudāruṇe
c prādurāsan vināśāya tadotpātāḥ sudāruṇāḥ
e cacāla śabdaṃ kurvāṇā saparvatavanā mahī
a sadaṇḍāḥ solmukā rājañ śīryamāṇāḥ samantataḥ
c ulkāḥ petur divo bhūmāv āhatya ravimaṇḍalam
a viṣvagvātāḥ prādurāsan nīcaiḥ śarkaravarṣiṇaḥ
c aśrūṇi mumucur nāgā vepathuś cāspṛśad bhṛśam
a etān ghorān anādṛtya samutpātān sudāruṇān
c punar yuddhāya saṃmantrya kṣatriyās tasthur avyathāḥ
e ramaṇīye kurukṣetre puṇye svargaṃ yiyāsavaḥ
a tato gāndhārarājasya putraḥ śakunir abravīt
b śakuniḥ paramayā śaktyā pāṇḍavaṃ balam ādravat
c yudhyadhvam agrato yāvat pṛṣṭhato hanmi pāṇḍavān
d te yāvat pṛṣṭhato hanti pāṇḍavān raṇadurmadān
a tato naḥ saṃprayātānāṃ madrayodhās tarasvinaḥ
c hṛṣṭāḥ kilakilāśabdam akurvantāpare tathā
a asmāṃs tu punar āsādya labdhalakṣā durāsadāḥ
c śarāsanāni dhunvantaḥ śaravarṣair avākiran
a tato hataṃ parais tatra madrarājabalaṃ tadā
c duryodhanabalaṃ dṛṣṭvā punar āsīt parāṅmukham
a gāndhārarājas tu punar vākyam āha tato balī
c nivartadhvam adharmajñā yudhyadhvaṃ kiṃ sṛtena vaḥ
d suranārīratisukhaṃ vimardam evam anyathā
d utpāṭitaṃ dvāram etac chrīmat tridaśasadmanaḥ
d evam uktvā jagāmāśu śakunis tāṃ punaḥ punaḥ
d lakṣadhvajaṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ ca manonilajavaṃ mahat
a anīkaṃ daśasāhasram aśvānāṃ bharatarṣabha
c āsīd gāndhārarājasya vimalaprāsayodhinām
a balena tena vikramya vartamāne janakṣaye
c pṛṣṭhataḥ pāṇḍavānīkam abhyaghnan niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a tad abhram iva vātena kṣipyamāṇaṃ samantataḥ
c abhajyata mahārāja pāṇḍūnāṃ sumahad balam
a tato yudhiṣṭhiraḥ prekṣya bhagnaṃ svabalam antikāt
c abhyacodayad avyagraḥ sahadevaṃ mahābalam
a asau subalaputro no jaghanaṃ pīḍya daṃśitaḥ
c senāṃ nisūdayanty eṣa paśya pāṇḍava durmatim
a gaccha tvaṃ draupadeyāś ca śakuniṃ saubalaṃ jahi
c rathānīkam ahaṃ rakṣye pāñcālasahito 'nagha
a gacchantu kuñjarāḥ sarve vājinaś ca saha tvayā
c pādātāś ca trisāhasrāḥ śakuniṃ saubalaṃ jahi
d kiranto yatra caivāsmān pariśiṣṭo mahāmate
d mamānudhyānamahimā bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ
d na ca śāsanakartānyas tvattas tiṣṭhati kaś cana
d yad ājñāpayasīty evam avadat prītimānasaḥ
a tato gajāḥ saptaśatāś cāpapāṇibhir āsthitāḥ
c pañca cāśvasahasrāṇi sahadevaś ca vīryavān
a pādātāś ca trisāhasrā draupadeyāś ca sarvaśaḥ
c raṇe hy abhyadravaṃs te tu śakuniṃ yuddhadurmadam
a tatas tu saubalo rājann abhyatikramya pāṇḍavān
c jaghāna pṛṣṭhataḥ senāṃ jayagṛdhraḥ pratāpavān
a aśvārohās tu saṃrabdhāḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ tarasvinām
c prāviśan saubalānīkam abhyatikramya tān rathān
a te tatra sādinaḥ śūrāḥ saubalasya mahad balam
c gajamadhye 'vatiṣṭhantaḥ śaravarṣair avākiran
a tad udyatagadāprāsam akāpuruṣasevitam
c prāvartata mahad yuddhaṃ rājan durmantrite tava
a upāramanta jyāśabdāḥ prekṣakā rathino 'bhavan
c na hi sveṣāṃ pareṣāṃ vā viśeṣaḥ pratyadṛśyata
a śūrabāhuvisṛṣṭānāṃ śaktīnāṃ bharatarṣabha
c jyotiṣām iva saṃpātam apaśyan kurupāṇḍavāḥ
a ṛṣṭibhir vimalābhiś ca tatra tatra viśāṃ pate
c saṃpatantībhir ākāśam āvṛtaṃ bahv aśobhata
a prāsānāṃ patatāṃ rājan rūpam āsīt samantataḥ
c śalabhānām ivākāśe tadā bharatasattama
a rudhirokṣitasarvāṅgā vipraviddhair niyantṛbhiḥ
c hayāḥ paripatanti sma śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a anyonyaparipiṣṭāś ca samāsādya parasparam
c avikṣatāḥ sma dṛśyante vamanto rudhiraṃ mukhaiḥ
a tato 'bhavat tamo ghoraṃ sainyena rajasā vṛte
c tān apākramato 'drākṣaṃ tasmād deśād ariṃdamān
e aśvān rājan manuṣyāṃś ca rajasā saṃvṛte sati
a bhūmau nipatitāś cānye vamanto rudhiraṃ bahu
c keśākeśisamālagnā na śekuś ceṣṭituṃ janāḥ
a anyonyam aśvapṛṣṭhebhyo vikarṣanto mahābalāḥ
c mallā iva samāsādya nijaghnur itaretaram
e aśvaiś ca vyapakṛṣyanta bahavo 'tra gatāsavaḥ
a bhūmau nipatitāś cānye bahavo vijayaiṣiṇaḥ
c tatra tatra vyadṛśyanta puruṣāḥ śūramāninaḥ
a raktokṣitaiś chinnabhujair apakṛṣṭaśiroruhaiḥ
c vyadṛśyata mahī kīrṇā śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a dūraṃ na śakyaṃ tatrāsīd gantum aśvena kena cit
c sāśvārohair hatair aśvair āvṛte vasudhātale
a rudhirokṣitasaṃnāhair āttaśastrair udāyudhaiḥ
c nānāpraharaṇair ghoraiḥ parasparavadhaiṣibhiḥ
e susaṃnikṛṣṭaiḥ saṃgrāme hatabhūyiṣṭhasainikaiḥ
a sa muhūrtaṃ tato yuddhvā saubalo 'tha viśāṃ pate
c ṣaṭsahasrair hayaiḥ śiṣṭair apāyāc chakunis tataḥ
a tathaiva pāṇḍavānīkaṃ rudhireṇa samukṣitam
c ṣaṭsahasrair hayaiḥ śiṣṭair apāyāc chrāntavāhanam
a aśvārohās tu pāṇḍūnām abruvan rudhirokṣitāḥ
b śakuniṃ mārayāmo 'dya sahaputraṃ sabāndhavam
b tato duryodhanaṃ pāpaṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ prasādataḥ
c susaṃnikṛṣṭāḥ saṃgrāme bhūyiṣṭhaṃ tyaktajīvitāḥ
a neha śakyaṃ rathair yoddhuṃ kuta eva mahāgajaiḥ
c rathān eva rathā yāntu kuñjarāḥ kuñjarān api
d vayaṃ paścād gamiṣyāmaḥ sahitās tyaktajīvitāḥ
d bhṛśaṃ palāyane tasmād upādhiṃ samupāśritāḥ
a pratiyāto hi śakuniḥ svam anīkam avasthitaḥ
c na punaḥ saubalo rājā yuddham abhyāgamiṣyati
a tatas tu draupadeyāś ca te ca mattā mahādvipāḥ
c prayayur yatra pāñcālyo dhṛṣṭadyumno mahārathaḥ
a sahadevo 'pi kauravya rajomeghe samutthite
c ekākī prayayau tatra yatra rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a tatas teṣu prayāteṣu śakuniḥ saubalaḥ punaḥ
c pārśvato 'bhyahanat kruddho dhṛṣṭadyumnasya vāhinīm
a tat punas tumulaṃ yuddhaṃ prāṇāṃs tyaktvābhyavartata
c tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca parasparavadhaiṣiṇām
a te hy anyonyam avekṣanta tasmin vīrasamāgame
c yodhāḥ paryapatan rājañ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a asibhiś chidyamānānāṃ śirasāṃ lokasaṃkṣaye
c prādurāsīn mahāśabdas tālānāṃ patatām iva
a vimuktānāṃ śarīrāṇāṃ bhinnānāṃ patatāṃ bhuvi
c sāyudhānāṃ ca bāhūnām urūṇāṃ ca viśāṃ pate
e āsīt kaṭakaṭāśabdaḥ sumahān romaharṣaṇaḥ
a nighnanto niśitaiḥ śastrair bhrātṝn putrān sakhīn api
c yodhāḥ paripatanti sma yathāmiṣakṛte khagāḥ
a anyonyaṃ pratisaṃrabdhāḥ samāsādya parasparam
c ahaṃ pūrvam ahaṃ pūrvam iti nyaghnan sahasraśaḥ
a saṃghātair āsanabhraṣṭair aśvārohair gatāsubhiḥ
c hayāḥ paripatanti sma śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a sphuratāṃ pratipiṣṭānām aśvānāṃ śīghrasāriṇām
c stanatāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ saṃnaddhānāṃ viśāṃ pate
a śaktyṛṣṭiprāsaśabdaś ca tumulaḥ samajāyata
c bhindatāṃ paramarmāṇi rājan durmantrite tava
d evaṃ hi yodhāḥ saṃrabdhāḥ parasparasamāhatāḥ
a śramābhibhūtāḥ saṃrabdhāḥ śrāntavāhāḥ pipāsitāḥ
c vikṣatāś ca śitaiḥ śastrair abhyavartanta tāvakāḥ
a mattā rudhiragandhena bahavo 'tra vicetasaḥ
c jaghnuḥ parān svakāṃś caiva prāptān prāptān anantarān
a bahavaś ca gataprāṇāḥ kṣatriyā jayagṛddhinaḥ
c bhūmāv abhyapatan rājañ śaravṛṣṭibhir āvṛtāḥ
a vṛkagṛdhraśṛgālānāṃ tumule modane 'hani
c āsīd balakṣayo ghoras tava putrasya paśyataḥ
a narāśvakāyasaṃchannā bhūmir āsīd viśāṃ pate
c rudhirodakacitrā ca bhīrūṇāṃ bhayavardhinī
a asibhiḥ paṭṭiśaiḥ śūlais takṣamāṇāḥ punaḥ punaḥ
c tāvakāḥ pāṇḍavāś caiva nābhyavartanta bhārata
a praharanto yathāśakti yāvat prāṇasya dhāraṇam
c yodhāḥ paripatanti sma vamanto rudhiraṃ vraṇaiḥ
a śiro gṛhītvā keśeṣu kabandhaḥ samadṛśyata
c udyamya niśitaṃ khaḍgaṃ rudhireṇa samukṣitam
a athotthiteṣu bahuṣu kabandheṣu janādhipa
c tathā rudhiragandhena yodhāḥ kaśmalam āviśan
a mandībhūte tataḥ śabde pāṇḍavānāṃ mahad balam
c alpāvaśiṣṭais turagair abhyavartata saubalaḥ
a tato 'bhyadhāvaṃs tvaritāḥ pāṇḍavā jayagṛddhinaḥ
c padātayaś ca nāgāś ca sādinaś codyatāyudhāḥ
a koṣṭakīkṛtya cāpy enaṃ parikṣipya ca sarvaśaḥ
c śastrair nānāvidhair jaghnur yuddhapāraṃ titīrṣavaḥ
d drāvyamāṇaṃ balaṃ dṛṣṭvā tava putrasya paśyataḥ
a tvadīyās tāṃs tu saṃprekṣya sarvataḥ samabhidrutān
c sāśvapattidviparathāḥ pāṇḍavān abhidudruvuḥ
a ke cit padātayaḥ padbhir muṣṭibhiś ca parasparam
c nijaghnuḥ samare śūrāḥ kṣīṇaśastrās tato 'patan
a rathebhyo rathinaḥ petur dvipebhyo hastisādinaḥ
c vimānebhya iva bhraṣṭāḥ siddhāḥ puṇyakṣayād yathā
a evam anyonyam āyastā yodhā jaghnur mahāmṛdhe
c pitṝn bhrātṝn vayasyāṃś ca putrān api tathāpare
a evam āsīd amaryādaṃ yuddhaṃ bharatasattama
c prāsāsibāṇakalile vartamāne sudāruṇe
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tasmiñ śabde mṛdau jāte pāṇḍavair nihate bale
c aśvaiḥ saptaśataiḥ śiṣṭair upāvartata saubalaḥ
a sa yātvā vāhinīṃ tūrṇam abravīt tvarayan yudhi
c yudhyadhvam iti saṃhṛṣṭāḥ punaḥ punar ariṃdamaḥ
e apṛcchat kṣatriyāṃs tatra kva nu rājā mahārathaḥ
a śakunes tu vacaḥ śrutvā ta ūcur bharatarṣabha
c asau tiṣṭhati kauravyo raṇamadhye mahārathaḥ
a yatraitat sumahac chatraṃ pūrṇacandrasamaprabham
c yatraite satalatrāṇā rathās tiṣṭhanti daṃśitāḥ
a yatraiṣa śabdas tumulaḥ parjanyaninadopamaḥ
c tatra gaccha drutaṃ rājaṃs tato drakṣyasi kauravam
a evam uktas tu taiḥ śūraiḥ śakuniḥ saubalas tadā
c prayayau tatra yatrāsau putras tava narādhipa
e sarvataḥ saṃvṛto vīraiḥ samareṣv anivartibhiḥ
a tato duryodhanaṃ dṛṣṭvā rathānīke vyavasthitam
c sarathāṃs tāvakān sarvān harṣayañ śakunis tataḥ
a duryodhanam idaṃ vākyaṃ hṛṣṭarūpo viśāṃ pate
c kṛtakāryam ivātmānaṃ manyamāno 'bravīn nṛpam
a jahi rājan rathānīkam aśvāḥ sarve jitā mayā
c nātyaktvā jīvitaṃ saṃkhye śakyo jetuṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a hate tasmin rathānīke pāṇḍavenābhipālite
c gajān etān haniṣyāmaḥ padātīṃś cetarāṃs tathā
a śrutvā tu vacanaṃ tasya tāvakā jayagṛddhinaḥ
c javenābhyapatan hṛṣṭāḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm
a sarve vivṛtatūṇīrāḥ pragṛhītaśarāsanāḥ
c śarāsanāni dhunvānāḥ siṃhanādaṃ pracakrire
a tato jyātalanirghoṣaḥ punar āsīd viśāṃ pate
c prādurāsīc charāṇāṃ ca sumuktānāṃ sudāruṇaḥ
a tān samīpagatān dṛṣṭvā javenodyatakārmukān
c uvāca devakīputraṃ kuntīputro dhanaṃjayaḥ
a codayāśvān asaṃbhrāntaḥ praviśaitad balārṇavam
c antam adya gamiṣyāmi śatrūṇāṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a aṣṭādaśa dināny adya yuddhasyāsya janārdana
c vartamānasya mahataḥ samāsādya parasparam
a anantakalpā dhvajinī bhūtvā hy eṣāṃ mahātmanām
c kṣayam adya gatā yuddhe paśya daivaṃ yathāvidham
a samudrakalpaṃ tu balaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya mādhava
c asmān āsādya saṃjātaṃ goṣpadopamam acyuta
a hate bhīṣme ca saṃdadhyāc chivaṃ syād iha mādhava
c na ca tat kṛtavān mūḍho dhārtarāṣṭraḥ subāliśaḥ
a uktaṃ bhīṣmeṇa yad vākyaṃ hitaṃ pathyaṃ ca mādhava
c tac cāpi nāsau kṛtavān vītabuddhiḥ suyodhanaḥ
a tasmiṃs tu patite bhīṣme pracyute pṛthivītale
c na jāne kāraṇaṃ kiṃ nu yena yuddham avartata
d hate droṇe ca karṇe ca bhūriśravasi saṃgare
d duḥśāsane ca śālve ca śalye ca saparicchade
d bhagadatte ca vīrendre naivāśāmyata hā raṇaḥ
d yena bhīṣmas tathā droṇaḥ kṛpo vidura eva ca
d pitā mātā śamasyārthe pratyākhyātās tu pāpinā
a mūḍhāṃs tu sarvathā manye dhārtarāṣṭrān subāliśān
c patite śaṃtanoḥ putre ye 'kārṣuḥ saṃyugaṃ punaḥ
a anantaraṃ ca nihate droṇe brahmavidāṃ vare
c rādheye ca vikarṇe ca naivāśāmyata vaiśasam
d rādheye sūtaputre ca naiva śāmyati vaiśasam
a alpāvaśiṣṭe sainye 'smin sūtaputre ca pātite
c saputre vai naravyāghre naivāśāmyata vaiśasam
a śrutāyuṣi hate śūre jalasaṃdhe ca paurave
c śrutāyudhe ca nṛpatau naivāśāmyata vaiśasam
a bhūriśravasi śalye ca śālve caiva janārdana
c āvantyeṣu ca vīreṣu naivāśāmyata vaiśasam
a jayadrathe ca nihate rākṣase cāpy alāyudhe
c bāhlike somadatte ca naivāśāmyata vaiśasam
a bhagadatte hate śūre kāmboje ca sudakṣiṇe
b nānādeśasamutthe ca hate sainye pṛthagvidhe
c duḥśāsane ca nihate naivāśāmyata vaiśasam
a dṛṣṭvā ca nihatāñ śūrān pṛthaṅ māṇḍalikān nṛpān
c balinaś ca raṇe kṛṣṇa naivāśāmyata vaiśasam
a akṣauhiṇīpatīn dṛṣṭvā bhīmasenena pātitān
c mohād vā yadi vā lobhān naivāśāmyata vaiśasam
d hatapravīrāṃ vidhvastāṃ dṛṣṭvā cemāṃ camūṃ raṇe
d alambuse ca nihate naiva śāmyati vaiśasam
d bhrātṝn vinihatān dṛṣṭvā vayasyān mātulān api
d putrān vinihatān saṃkhye naiva śāmyati vaiśasam
a ko nu rājakule jātaḥ kauraveyo viśeṣataḥ
c nirarthakaṃ mahad vairaṃ kuryād anyaḥ suyodhanāt
d nṛpapravīrān vidhvastān dṛṣṭvā cemāṃ mahācamūm
a guṇato 'bhyadhikaṃ jñātvā balataḥ śauryato 'pi vā
c amūḍhaḥ ko nu yudhyeta jānan prājño hitāhitam
a yan na tasya mano hy āsīt tvayoktasya hitaṃ vacaḥ
c praśame pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdhaṃ so 'nyasya śṛṇuyāt katham
a yena śāṃtanavo bhīṣmo droṇo vidura eva ca
c pratyākhyātāḥ śamasyārthe kiṃ nu tasyādya bheṣajam
a maurkhyād yena pitā vṛddhaḥ pratyākhyāto janārdana
c tathā mātā hitaṃ vākyaṃ bhāṣamāṇā hitaiṣiṇī
e pratyākhyātā hy asatkṛtya sa kasmai rocayed vacaḥ
a kulāntakaraṇo vyaktaṃ jāta eṣa janārdana
c tathāsya dṛśyate ceṣṭā nītiś caiva viśāṃ pate
e naiṣa dāsyati no rājyam iti me matir acyuta
a ukto 'haṃ bahuśas tāta vidureṇa mahātmanā
c na jīvan dāsyate bhāgaṃ dhārtarāṣṭraḥ kathaṃ cana
a yāvat prāṇā dhamiṣyanti dhārtarāṣṭrasya mānada
c tāvad yuṣmāsv apāpeṣu pracariṣyati pātakam
a na sa yukto 'nyathā jetum ṛte yuddhena mādhava
c ity abravīt sadā māṃ hi viduraḥ satyadarśanaḥ
a tat sarvam adya jānāmi vyavasāyaṃ durātmanaḥ
c yad uktaṃ vacanaṃ tena vidureṇa mahātmanā
a yo hi śrutvā vacaḥ pathyaṃ jāmadagnyād yathātatham
c avāmanyata durbuddhir dhruvaṃ nāśamukhe sthitaḥ
a uktaṃ hi bahubhiḥ siddhair jātamātre suyodhane
c enaṃ prāpya durātmānaṃ kṣayaṃ kṣatraṃ gamiṣyati
a tad idaṃ vacanaṃ teṣāṃ niruktaṃ vai janārdana
c kṣayaṃ yātā hi rājāno duryodhanakṛte bhṛśam
a so 'dya sarvān raṇe yodhān nihaniṣyāmi mādhava
c kṣatriyeṣu hateṣv āśu śūnye ca śibire kṛte
a vadhāya cātmano 'smābhiḥ saṃyugaṃ rocayiṣyati
c tad antaṃ hi bhaved vairam anumānena mādhava
a evaṃ paśyāmi vārṣṇeya cintayan prajñayā svayā
c vidurasya ca vākyena ceṣṭayā ca durātmanaḥ
a saṃyāhi bhāratīṃ vīra yāvad dhanmi śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c duryodhanaṃ durātmānaṃ vāhinīṃ cāsya saṃyuge
a kṣemam adya kariṣyāmi dharmarājasya mādhava
c hatvaitad durbalaṃ sainyaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya paśyataḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a abhīśuhasto dāśārhas tathoktaḥ savyasācinā
c tad balaugham amitrāṇām abhītaḥ prāviśad raṇe
a śarāsanavaraṃ ghoraṃ śaktikaṇṭakasaṃvṛtam
c gadāparighapanthānaṃ rathanāgamahādrumam
a hayapattilatākīrṇaṃ gāhamāno mahāyaśāḥ
c vyacarat tatra govindo rathenātipatākinā
a te hayāḥ pāṇḍurā rājan vahanto 'rjunam āhave
c dikṣu sarvāsv adṛśyanta dāśārheṇa pracoditāḥ
a tataḥ prāyād rathenājau savyasācī paraṃtapaḥ
c kirañ śaraśatāṃs tīkṣṇān vāridhārā ivāmbudaḥ
a prādurāsīn mahāñ śabdaḥ śarāṇāṃ nataparvaṇām
c iṣubhiś chādyamānānāṃ samare savyasācinā
a asajjantas tanutreṣu śaraughāḥ prāpatan bhuvi
c indrāśanisamasparśā gāṇḍīvapreṣitāḥ śarāḥ
a narān nāgān samāhatya hayāṃś cāpi viśāṃ pate
c apatanta raṇe bāṇāḥ pataṃgā iva ghoṣiṇaḥ
a āsīt sarvam avacchannaṃ gāṇḍīvapreṣitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c na prājñāyanta samare diśo vā pradiśo 'pi vā
a sarvam āsīj jagat pūrṇaṃ pārthanāmāṅkitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c rukmapuṅkhais tailadhautaiḥ karmāraparimārjitaiḥ
a te dahyamānāḥ pārthena pāvakeneva kuñjarāḥ
c samāsīdanta kauravyā vadhyamānāḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a śaracāpadharaḥ pārthaḥ prajvalann iva bhārata
c dadāha samare yodhān kakṣam agnir iva jvalan
a yathā vanānte vanapair visṛṣṭaḥ
kakṣaṃ dahet kṛṣṇagatiḥ saghoṣaḥ
c bhūridrumaṃ śuṣkalatāvitānaṃ
bhṛśaṃ samṛddho jvalanaḥ pratāpī
a evaṃ sa nārācagaṇapratāpī
śarārcir uccāvacatigmatejāḥ
c dadāha sarvāṃ tava putrasenām
amṛṣyamāṇas tarasā tarasvī
a tasyeṣavaḥ prāṇaharāḥ sumuktā
nāsajjan vai varmasu rukmapuṅkhāḥ
c na ca dvitīyaṃ pramumoca bāṇaṃ
nare haye vā paramadvipe vā
a anekarūpākṛtibhir hi bāṇair
mahārathānīkam anupraviśya
c sa eva ekas tava putrasenāṃ
jaghāna daityān iva vajrapāṇiḥ
c dhanaṃjayaḥ saṃyati sāyakair vā
 saṃjaya uvāca
a asyatāṃ yatamānānāṃ śūrāṇām anivartinām
c saṃkalpam akaron moghaṃ gāṇḍīvena dhanaṃjayaḥ
a indrāśanisamasparśān aviṣahyān mahaujasaḥ
c visṛjan dṛśyate bāṇān dhārā muñcann ivāmbudaḥ
a tat sainyaṃ bharataśreṣṭha vadhyamānaṃ kirīṭinā
c saṃpradudrāva saṃgrāmāt tava putrasya paśyataḥ
d pitṝn bhrātṝn parityajya vayasyān api cāpare
a hatadhuryā rathāḥ ke cid dhatasūtās tathāpare
c bhagnākṣayugacakreṣāḥ ke cid āsan viśāṃ pate
a anyeṣāṃ sāyakāḥ kṣīṇās tathānye śarapīḍitāḥ
c akṣatā yugapat ke cit prādravan bhayapīḍitāḥ
a ke cit putrān upādāya hatabhūyiṣṭhavāhanāḥ
c vicukruśuḥ pitṝn anye sahāyān apare punaḥ
a bāndhavāṃś ca naravyāghra bhrātṝn saṃbandhinas tathā
c dudruvuḥ ke cid utsṛjya tatra tatra viśāṃ pate
a bahavo 'tra bhṛśaṃ viddhā muhyamānā mahārathāḥ
c niṣṭanantaḥ sma dṛśyante pārthabāṇahatā narāḥ
a tān anye ratham āropya samāśvāsya muhūrtakam
c viśrāntāś ca vitṛṣṇāś ca punar yuddhāya jagmire
a tān apāsya gatāḥ ke cit punar eva yuyutsavaḥ
c kurvantas tava putrasya śāsanaṃ yuddhadurmadāḥ
a pānīyam apare pītvā paryāśvāsya ca vāhanam
c varmāṇi ca samāropya ke cid bharatasattama
a samāśvāsyāpare bhrātṝn nikṣipya śibire 'pi ca
c putrān anye pitṝn anye punar yuddham arocayan
a sajjayitvā rathān ke cid yathāmukhyaṃ viśāṃ pate
c āplutya pāṇḍavānīkaṃ punar yuddham arocayan
a te śūrāḥ kiṅkiṇījālaiḥ samācchannā babhāsire
c trailokyavijaye yuktā yathā daiteyadānavāḥ
a āgamya sahasā ke cid rathaiḥ svarṇavibhūṣitaiḥ
c pāṇḍavānām anīkeṣu dhṛṣṭadyumnam ayodhayan
a dhṛṣṭadyumno 'pi pāñcālyaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca mahārathaḥ
c nākuliś ca śatānīko rathānīkam ayodhayan
a pāñcālyas tu tataḥ kruddhaḥ sainyena mahatā vṛtaḥ
c abhyadravat susaṃrabdhas tāvakān hantum udyataḥ
d abhyayus tāvakān yuddhe śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a tatas tv āpatatas tasya tava putro janādhipa
c bāṇasaṃghān anekān vai preṣayām āsa bhārata
d ekaikaṃ daśabhir bāṇair avidhyad bharatarṣabhaḥ
a dhṛṣṭadyumnas tato rājaṃs tava putreṇa dhanvinā
c nārācair bahubhiḥ kṣipraṃ bāhvor urasi cārpitaḥ
c nārācair ardhanārācair bahubhiḥ kṣiprakāribhiḥ
d vatsadantaiś ca bāṇaiś ca karmāraparimārjitaiḥ
d aśvāṃś ca caturo hatvā
a so 'tividdho maheṣvāsas tottrārdita iva dvipaḥ
c tasyāśvāṃś caturo bāṇaiḥ preṣayām āsa mṛtyave
e sāratheś cāsya bhallena śiraḥ kāyād apāharat
a tato duryodhano rājā pṛṣṭham āruhya vājinaḥ
c apākrāmad dhataratho nātidūram ariṃdamaḥ
a dṛṣṭvā tu hatavikrāntaṃ svam anīkaṃ mahābalaḥ
c tava putro mahārāja prayayau yatra saubalaḥ
a tato ratheṣu bhagneṣu trisāhasrā mahādvipāḥ
c pāṇḍavān rathinaḥ pañca samantāt paryavārayan
a te vṛtāḥ samare pañca gajānīkena bhārata
c aśobhanta naravyāghrā grahā vyāptā ghanair iva
a tato 'rjuno mahārāja labdhalakṣo mahābhujaḥ
c viniryayau rathenaiva śvetāśvaḥ kṛṣṇasārathiḥ
a taiḥ samantāt parivṛtaḥ kuñjaraiḥ parvatopamaiḥ
c nārācair vimalais tīkṣṇair gajānīkam apothayat
a tatraikabāṇanihatān apaśyāma mahāgajān
c patitān pātyamānāṃś ca vibhinnān savyasācinā
a bhīmasenas tu tān dṛṣṭvā nāgān mattagajopamaḥ
c kareṇa gṛhya mahatīṃ gadām abhyapatad balī
e avaplutya rathāt tūrṇaṃ daṇḍapāṇir ivāntakaḥ
a tam udyatagadaṃ dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavānāṃ mahāratham
c vitresus tāvakāḥ sainyāḥ śakṛnmūtraṃ prasusruvuḥ
e āvignaṃ ca balaṃ sarvaṃ gadāhaste vṛkodare
a gadayā bhīmasenena bhinnakumbhān rajasvalān
b pātyamānān prapaśyāma līnakumbhān kṣaradvraṇān
c dhāvamānān apaśyāma kuñjarān parvatopamān
a pradhāvya kuñjarās te tu bhīmasenagadāhatāḥ
c petur ārtasvaraṃ kṛtvā chinnapakṣā ivādrayaḥ
a tān bhinnakumbhān subahūn dravamāṇān itas tataḥ
c patamānāṃś ca saṃprekṣya vitresus tava sainikāḥ
a yudhiṣṭhiro 'pi saṃkruddho mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavau
c gṛdhrapakṣaiḥ śitair bāṇair jaghnur vai gajayodhinaḥ
a dhṛṣṭadyumnas tu samare parājitya narādhipam
c apakrānte tava sute hayapṛṣṭhaṃ samāśrite
a dṛṣṭvā ca pāṇḍavān sarvān kuñjaraiḥ parivāritān
c dhṛṣṭadyumno mahārāja saha sarvaiḥ prabhadrakaiḥ
e putraḥ pāñcālarājasya jighāṃsuḥ kuñjarān yayau
a adṛṣṭvā tu rathānīke duryodhanam ariṃdamam
c aśvatthāmā kṛpaś caiva kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥ
e apṛcchan kṣatriyāṃs tatra kva nu duryodhano gataḥ
a apaśyamānā rājānaṃ vartamāne janakṣaye
c manvānā nihataṃ tatra tava putraṃ mahārathāḥ
e viṣaṇṇavadanā bhūtvā paryapṛcchanta te sutam
a āhuḥ ke cid dhate sūte prayāto yatra saubalaḥ
c apare tv abruvaṃs tatra kṣatriyā bhṛśavikṣatāḥ
a duryodhanena kiṃ kāryaṃ drakṣyadhvaṃ yadi jīvati
c yudhyadhvaṃ sahitāḥ sarve kiṃ vo rājā kariṣyati
d tatas te kṣatriyāḥ sarve svadharmeṣu vyavasthitāḥ
a te kṣatriyāḥ kṣatair gātrair hatabhūyiṣṭhavāhanāḥ
c śaraiḥ saṃpīḍyamānāś ca nātivyaktam ivābruvan
a idaṃ sarvaṃ balaṃ hanmo yena sma parivāritāḥ
c ete sarve gajān hatvā upayānti sma pāṇḍavāḥ
a śrutvā tu vacanaṃ teṣām aśvatthāmā mahābalaḥ
c hitvā pāñcālarājasya tad anīkaṃ durutsaham
a kṛpaś ca kṛtavarmā ca prayayur yatra saubalaḥ
c rathānīkaṃ parityajya śūrāḥ sudṛḍhadhanvinaḥ
a tatas teṣu prayāteṣu dhṛṣṭadyumnapurogamāḥ
c āyayuḥ pāṇḍavā rājan vinighnantaḥ sma tāvakān
a dṛṣṭvā tu tān āpatataḥ saṃprahṛṣṭān mahārathān
c parākrāntāṃs tato vīrān nirāśāñ jīvite tadā
e vivarṇamukhabhūyiṣṭham abhavat tāvakaṃ balam
a parikṣīṇāyudhān dṛṣṭvā tān ahaṃ parivāritān
c rājan balena dvyaṅgena tyaktvā jīvitam ātmanaḥ
a ātmanāpañcamo 'yudhyaṃ pāñcālasya balena ha
c tasmin deśe vyavasthāpya yatra śāradvataḥ sthitaḥ
a saṃprayuddhā vayaṃ pañca kirīṭiśarapīḍitāḥ
c dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ mahānīkaṃ tatra no 'bhūd raṇo mahān
e jitās tena vayaṃ sarve vyapayāma raṇāt tataḥ
a athāpaśyaṃ sātyakiṃ tam upāyāntaṃ mahāratham
c rathaiś catuḥśatair vīro māṃ cābhyadravad āhave
a dhṛṣṭadyumnād ahaṃ muktaḥ kathaṃ cic chrāntavāhanaḥ
c patito mādhavānīkaṃ duṣkṛtī narakaṃ yathā
e tatra yuddham abhūd ghoraṃ muhūrtam atidāruṇam
a sātyakis tu mahābāhur mama hatvā paricchadam
c jīvagrāham agṛhṇān māṃ mūrchitaṃ patitaṃ bhuvi
d sarve jayāya dhāvanti mayā labdho 'dya saṃjayaḥ
d iti bruvāṇaḥ śaineyo rājan mām agrahīt tadā
a tato muhūrtād iva tad gajānīkam avadhyata
c gadayā bhīmasenena nārācair arjunena ca
a pratipiṣṭair mahānāgaiḥ samantāt parvatopamaiḥ
c nātiprasiddheva gatiḥ pāṇḍavānām ajāyata
d viniryayau rathenaiva śvetāśvaḥ kṛṣṇasārathiḥ
a rathamārgāṃs tataś cakre bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
c pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārāja vyapakarṣan mahāgajān
a aśvatthāmā kṛpaś caiva kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥ
c apaśyanto rathānīke duryodhanam ariṃdamam
e rājānaṃ mṛgayām āsus tava putraṃ mahāratham
a parityajya ca pāñcālaṃ prayātā yatra saubalaḥ
c rājño 'darśanasaṃvignā vartamāne janakṣaye
 saṃjaya uvāca
a gajānīke hate tasmin pāṇḍuputreṇa bhārata
c vadhyamāne bale caiva bhīmasenena saṃyuge
a carantaṃ ca tathā dṛṣṭvā bhīmasenam ariṃdamam
c daṇḍahastaṃ yathā kruddham antakaṃ prāṇahāriṇam
a sametya samare rājan hataśeṣāḥ sutās tava
c adṛśyamāne kauravye putre duryodhane tava
e sodaryāḥ sahitā bhūtvā bhīmasenam upādravan
f śrutavān saṃjayaś caiva jayatsenaḥ śrutāntakaḥ
f durvimocanakaś caiva tathā durviṣaho balī
f śrutavarmā śrutarvā ca sujāto durvimocanaḥ
a durmarṣaṇo mahārāja jaitro bhūribalo raviḥ
b jayatsenaḥ sujātaś ca tathā durviṣaho 'rihā
b durvimocananāmā ca duṣpradharṣas tathaiva ca
b śrutarvā ca mahābāhuḥ sarve yuddhaviśāradāḥ
c ity ete sahitā bhūtvā tava putrāḥ samantataḥ
e bhīmasenam abhidrutya rurudhuḥ sarvatodiśam
a tato bhīmo mahārāja svarathaṃ punar āsthitaḥ
c mumoca niśitān bāṇān putrāṇāṃ tava marmasu
a te kīryamāṇā bhīmena putrās tava mahāraṇe
c bhīmasenam apāsedhan pravaṇād iva kuñjaram
d bhīmam eva samājaghnuḥ smarantaṃ pūrvakilbiṣam
a tataḥ kruddho raṇe bhīmaḥ śiro durmarṣaṇasya ha
c kṣurapreṇa pramathyāśu pātayām āsa bhūtale
a tato 'pareṇa bhallena sarvāvaraṇabhedinā
c śrutāntam avadhīd bhīmas tava putraṃ mahārathaḥ
a jayatsenaṃ tato viddhvā nārācena hasann iva
c pātayām āsa kauravyaṃ rathopasthād ariṃdamaḥ
e sa papāta rathād rājan bhūmau tūrṇaṃ mamāra ca
a śrutarvā tu tato bhīmaṃ kruddho vivyādha māriṣa
c śatena gṛdhravājānāṃ śarāṇāṃ nataparvaṇām
a tataḥ kruddho raṇe bhīmo jaitraṃ bhūribalaṃ ravim
c trīn etāṃs tribhir ānarchad viṣāgnipratimaiḥ śaraiḥ
a te hatā nyapatan bhūmau syandanebhyo mahārathāḥ
c vasante puṣpaśabalā nikṛttā iva kiṃśukāḥ
a tato 'pareṇa tīkṣṇena nārācena paraṃtapaḥ
c durvimocanam āhatya preṣayām āsa mṛtyave
a sa hataḥ prāpatad bhūmau svarathād rathināṃ varaḥ
c gires tu kūṭajo bhagno māruteneva pādapaḥ
a duṣpradharṣaṃ tataś caiva sujātaṃ ca sutau tava
c ekaikaṃ nyavadhīt saṃkhye dvābhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ camūmukhe

a tato yatantam aparam abhivīkṣya sutaṃ tava
c bhallena yudhi vivyādha bhīmo durviṣahaṃ raṇe
e sa papāta hato vāhāt paśyatāṃ sarvadhanvinām
a dṛṣṭvā tu nihatān bhrātṝn bahūn ekena saṃyuge
c amarṣavaśam āpannaḥ śrutarvā bhīmam abhyayāt
a vikṣipan sumahac cāpaṃ kārtasvaravibhūṣitam
c visṛjan sāyakāṃś caiva viṣāgnipratimān bahūn
a sa tu rājan dhanuś chittvā pāṇḍavasya mahāmṛdhe
c athainaṃ chinnadhanvānaṃ viṃśatyā samavākirat
a tato 'nyad dhanur ādāya bhīmaseno mahārathaḥ
c avākirat tava sutaṃ tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīt
a mahad āsīt tayor yuddhaṃ citrarūpaṃ bhayānakam
c yādṛśaṃ samare pūrvaṃ jambhavāsavayor abhūt
a tayos tatra śarair muktair yamadaṇḍanibhaiḥ śubhaiḥ
a   avacchannā dharābhavat
c samācchannā dharā sarvā khaṃ ca sarvā diśas tathā
a tataḥ śrutarvā saṃkruddho dhanur āyamya sāyakaiḥ
c bhīmasenaṃ raṇe rājan bāhvor urasi cārpayat
a so 'tividdho mahārāja tava putreṇa dhanvinā
c bhīmaḥ saṃcukṣubhe kruddhaḥ parvaṇīva mahodadhiḥ
a tato bhīmo ruṣāviṣṭaḥ putrasya tava māriṣa
c sārathiṃ caturaś cāśvān bāṇair ninye yamakṣayam
a virathaṃ taṃ samālakṣya viśikhair lomavāhibhiḥ
c avākirad ameyātmā darśayan pāṇilāghavam
a śrutarvā viratho rājann ādade khaḍgacarmaṇī
c athāsyādadataḥ khaḍgaṃ śatacandraṃ ca bhānumat
e kṣurapreṇa śiraḥ kāyāt pātayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ
a chinnottamāṅgasya tataḥ kṣurapreṇa mahātmanaḥ
c papāta kāyaḥ sa rathād vasudhām anunādayan
a tasmin nipatite vīre tāvakā bhayamohitāḥ
c abhyadravanta saṃgrāme bhīmasenaṃ yuyutsavaḥ
a tān āpatata evāśu hataśeṣād balārṇavāt
c daṃśitaḥ pratijagrāha bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavān
e te tu taṃ vai samāsādya parivavruḥ samantataḥ
a tatas tu saṃvṛto bhīmas tāvakair niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c pīḍayām āsa tān sarvān sahasrākṣa ivāsurān
a tataḥ pañcaśatān hatvā savarūthān mahārathān
c jaghāna kuñjarānīkaṃ punaḥ saptaśataṃ yudhi
a hatvā daśa sahasrāṇi pattīnāṃ parameṣubhiḥ
c vājināṃ ca śatāny aṣṭau pāṇḍavaḥ sma virājate
a bhīmasenas tu kaunteyo hatvā yuddhe sutāṃs tava
c mene kṛtārtham ātmānaṃ saphalaṃ janma ca prabho
a taṃ tathā yudhyamānaṃ ca vinighnantaṃ ca tāvakān
c īkṣituṃ notsahante sma tava sainyāni bhārata
a vidrāvya tu kurūn sarvāṃs tāṃś ca hatvā padānugān
c dorbhyāṃ śabdaṃ tataś cakre trāsayāno mahādvipān
a hatabhūyiṣṭhayodhā tu tava senā viśāṃ pate
c kiṃciccheṣā mahārāja kṛpaṇā samapadyata
 saṃjaya uvāca
a duryodhano mahārāja sudarśaś cāpi te sutaḥ
c hataśeṣau tadā saṃkhye vājimadhye vyavasthitau
a tato duryodhanaṃ dṛṣṭvā vājimadhye vyavasthitam
c uvāca devakīputraḥ kuntīputraṃ dhanaṃjayam
a śatravo hatabhūyiṣṭhā jñātayaḥ paripālitāḥ
c gṛhītvā saṃjayaṃ cāsau nivṛttaḥ śinipuṃgavaḥ
a pariśrāntaś ca nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca bhārata
c yodhayitvā raṇe pāpān dhārtarāṣṭrapadānugān
a suyodhanam abhityajya traya ete vyavasthitāḥ
c kṛpaś ca kṛtavarmā ca drauṇiś caiva mahārathaḥ
a asau tiṣṭhati pāñcālyaḥ śriyā paramayā yutaḥ
c duryodhanabalaṃ hatvā saha sarvaiḥ prabhadrakaiḥ
a asau duryodhanaḥ pārtha vājimadhye vyavasthitaḥ
c chatreṇa dhriyamāṇena prekṣamāṇo muhur muhuḥ
a prativyūhya balaṃ sarvaṃ raṇamadhye vyavasthitaḥ
c enaṃ hatvā śitair bāṇaiḥ kṛtakṛtyo bhaviṣyasi
a gajānīkaṃ hataṃ dṛṣṭvā tvāṃ ca prāptam ariṃdama
c yāvan na vidravanty ete tāvaj jahi suyodhanam
a yātu kaś cit tu pāñcālyaṃ kṣipram āgamyatām iti
c pariśrāntabalas tāta naiṣa mucyeta kilbiṣī
a tava hatvā balaṃ sarvaṃ saṃgrāme dhṛtarāṣṭrajaḥ
c jitān pāṇḍusutān matvā rūpaṃ dhārayate mahat
d yathā daityacamūṃ hatvā purā śakro mahābalaḥ
a nihataṃ svabalaṃ dṛṣṭvā pīḍitaṃ cāpi pāṇḍavaiḥ
c dhruvam eṣyati saṃgrāme vadhāyaivātmano nṛpaḥ
a evam uktaḥ phalgunas tu kṛṣṇaṃ vacanam abravīt
c dhṛtarāṣṭrasutāḥ sarve hatā bhīmena mānada
e yāv etāv āsthitau kṛṣṇa tāv adya na bhaviṣyataḥ
a hato bhīṣmo hato droṇaḥ karṇo vaikartano hataḥ
c madrarājo hataḥ śalyo hataḥ kṛṣṇa jayadrathaḥ
a hayāḥ pañcaśatāḥ śiṣṭāḥ śakuneḥ saubalasya ca
c rathānāṃ tu śate śiṣṭe dve eva tu janārdana
e dantināṃ ca śataṃ sāgraṃ trisāhasrāḥ padātayaḥ
a aśvatthāmā kṛpaś caiva trigartādhipatis tathā
c ulūkaḥ śakuniś caiva kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥ
a etad balam abhūc cheṣaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya mādhava
c mokṣo na nūnaṃ kālād dhi vidyate bhuvi kasya cit
a tathā vinihate sainye paśya duryodhanaṃ sthitam
c adyāhnā hi mahārājo hatāmitro bhaviṣyati
a na hi me mokṣyate kaś cit pareṣām iti cintaye
c ye tv adya samaraṃ kṛṣṇa na hāsyanti raṇotkaṭāḥ
e tān vai sarvān haniṣyāmi yady api syur amānuṣāḥ
a adya yuddhe susaṃkruddho dīrghaṃ rājñaḥ prajāgaram
c apaneṣyāmi gāndhāraṃ pātayitvā śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a nikṛtyā vai durācāro yāni ratnāni saubalaḥ
c sabhāyām aharad dyūte punas tāny āharāmy aham
a adya tā api vetsyanti sarvā nāgapurastriyaḥ
c śrutvā patīṃś ca putrāṃś ca pāṇḍavair nihatān yudhi
a samāptam adya vai karma sarvaṃ kṛṣṇa bhaviṣyati
c adya duryodhano dīptāṃ śriyaṃ prāṇāṃś ca tyakṣyati
a nāpayāti bhayāt kṛṣṇa saṃgrāmād yadi cen mama
c nihataṃ viddhi vārṣṇeya dhārtarāṣṭraṃ subāliśam
a mama hy etad aśaktaṃ vai vājivṛndam ariṃdama
c soḍhuṃ jyātalanirghoṣaṃ yāhi yāvan nihanmy aham
a evam uktas tu dāśārhaḥ pāṇḍavena yaśasvinā
c acodayad dhayān rājan duryodhanabalaṃ prati
a tad anīkam abhiprekṣya trayaḥ sajjā mahārathāḥ
c bhīmaseno 'rjunaś caiva sahadevaś ca māriṣa
e prayayuḥ siṃhanādena duryodhanajighāṃsayā
a tān prekṣya sahitān sarvāñ javenodyatakārmukān
c saubalo 'bhyadravad yuddhe pāṇḍavān ātatāyinaḥ
a sudarśanas tava suto bhīmasenaṃ samabhyayāt
c suśarmā śakuniś caiva yuyudhāte kirīṭinā
e sahadevaṃ tava suto hayapṛṣṭhagato 'bhyayāt
a tato hy ayatnataḥ kṣipraṃ tava putro janādhipa
c prāsena sahadevasya śirasi prāharad bhṛśam
a sopāviśad rathopasthe tava putreṇa tāḍitaḥ
c rudhirāplutasarvāṅga āśīviṣa iva śvasan
a pratilabhya tataḥ saṃjñāṃ sahadevo viśāṃ pate
c duryodhanaṃ śarais tīkṣṇaiḥ saṃkruddhaḥ samavākirat
a pārtho 'pi yudhi vikramya kuntīputro dhanaṃjayaḥ
c śūrāṇām aśvapṛṣṭhebhyaḥ śirāṃsi nicakarta ha
a tad anīkaṃ tadā pārtho vyadhamad bahubhiḥ śaraiḥ
c pātayitvā hayān sarvāṃs trigartānāṃ rathān yayau
a tatas te sahitā bhūtvā trigartānāṃ mahārathāḥ
c arjunaṃ vāsudevaṃ ca śaravarṣair avākiran
a satyakarmāṇam ākṣipya kṣurapreṇa mahāyaśāḥ
c tato 'sya syandanasyeṣāṃ cicchide pāṇḍunandanaḥ
a śilāśitena ca vibho kṣurapreṇa mahāyaśāḥ
c śiraś ciccheda prahasaṃs taptakuṇḍalabhūṣaṇam
d hāhākāras tato jāto hate vīre suśarmaṇi
d tāvakānāṃ balaughānāṃ rājan durmantritāt tava
a satyeṣum atha cādatta yodhānāṃ miṣatāṃ tataḥ
c yathā siṃho vane rājan mṛgaṃ paribubhukṣitaḥ
a taṃ nihatya tataḥ pārthaḥ suśarmāṇaṃ tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
c viddhvā tān ahanat sarvān rathān rukmavibhūṣitān
a tatas tu pratvaran pārtho dīrghakālaṃ susaṃbhṛtam
c muñcan krodhaviṣaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ prasthalādhipatiṃ prati

c pūrayitvā tato vāhān nyahanat tasya dhanvinaḥ
a tataḥ śaraṃ samādāya yamadaṇḍopamaṃ śitam
c suśarmāṇaṃ samuddiśya cikṣepāśu hasann iva

c suśarmāṇaṃ samāsādya bibheda hṛdayaṃ raṇe
a sa gatāsur mahārāja papāta dharaṇītale
c nandayan pāṇḍavān sarvān vyathayaṃś cāpi tāvakān
a suśarmāṇaṃ raṇe hatvā putrān asya mahārathān
c sapta cāṣṭau ca triṃśac ca sāyakair anayat kṣayam
a tato 'sya niśitair bāṇaiḥ sarvān hatvā padānugān
c abhyagād bhāratīṃ senāṃ hataśeṣāṃ mahārathaḥ
a bhīmas tu samare kruddhaḥ putraṃ tava janādhipa
c sudarśanam adṛśyaṃ taṃ śaraiś cakre hasann iva
a tato 'sya prahasan kruddhaḥ śiraḥ kāyād apāharat
c kṣurapreṇa sutīkṣṇena sa hataḥ prāpatad bhuvi
a tasmiṃs tu nihate vīre tatas tasya padānugāḥ
a   tad anīkavanaṃ mahat
a adahad bhīmasenas tu helayā bāṇavahninā
c parivavrū raṇe bhīmaṃ kiranto viśikhāñ śitān
a tatas tu niśitair bāṇais tad anīkaṃ vṛkodaraḥ
c indrāśanisamasparśaiḥ samantāt paryavākirat
e tataḥ kṣaṇena tad bhīmo nyahanad bharatarṣabha
a teṣu tūtsādyamāneṣu senādhyakṣā mahābalāḥ
c bhīmasenaṃ samāsādya tato 'yudhyanta bhārata
e tāṃs tu sarvāñ śarair ghorair avākirata pāṇḍavaḥ
a tathaiva tāvakā rājan pāṇḍaveyān mahārathān
c śaravarṣeṇa mahatā samantāt paryavārayan
a vyākulaṃ tad abhūt sarvaṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ paraiḥ saha
c tāvakānāṃ ca samare pāṇḍaveyair yuyutsatām
a tatra yodhās tadā petuḥ parasparasamāhatāḥ
c ubhayoḥ senayo rājan saṃśocantaḥ sma bāndhavān
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tasmin pravṛtte saṃgrāme naravājigajakṣaye
c śakuniḥ saubalo rājan sahadevaṃ samabhyayāt
a tato 'syāpatatas tūrṇaṃ sahadevaḥ pratāpavān
c śaraughān preṣayām āsa pataṃgān iva śīghragān
e ulūkaś ca raṇe bhīmaṃ vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ
a śakunis tu mahārāja bhīmaṃ viddhvā tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
c sāyakānāṃ navatyā vai sahadevam avākirat
a te śūrāḥ samare rājan samāsādya parasparam
c vivyadhur niśitair bāṇaiḥ kaṅkabarhiṇavājitaiḥ
e svarṇapuṅkhaiḥ śilādhautair ā karṇāt prahitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a teṣāṃ cāpabhujotsṛṣṭā śaravṛṣṭir viśāṃ pate
c ācchādayad diśaḥ sarvā dhārābhir iva toyadaḥ
a tataḥ kruddho raṇe bhīmaḥ sahadevaś ca bhārata
c ceratuḥ kadanaṃ saṃkhye kurvantau sumahābalau
a tābhyāṃ śaraśataiś channaṃ tad balaṃ tava bhārata
c andhakāram ivākāśam abhavat tatra tatra ha
a aśvair viparidhāvadbhiḥ śaracchannair viśāṃ pate
c tatra tatra kṛto mārgo vikarṣadbhir hatān bahūn
a nihatānāṃ hayānāṃ ca sahaiva hayayodhibhiḥ
c varmabhir vinikṛttaiś ca prāsaiś chinnaiś ca māriṣa
d ṛṣṭibhiḥ śaktibhiś caiva tomaraiś ca paraṃtapa
e saṃchannā pṛthivī jajñe kusumaiḥ śabalā iva
a yodhās tatra mahārāja samāsādya parasparam
c vyacaranta raṇe kruddhā vinighnantaḥ parasparam
a udvṛttanayanai roṣāt saṃdaṣṭauṣṭhapuṭair mukhaiḥ
c sakuṇḍalair mahī channā padmakiñjalkasaṃnibhaiḥ
a bhujaiś chinnair mahārāja nāgarājakaropamaiḥ
c sāṅgadaiḥ satanutraiś ca sāsiprāsaparaśvadhaiḥ
a kabandhair utthitaiś chinnair nṛtyadbhiś cāparair yudhi
c kravyādagaṇasaṃkīrṇā ghorābhūt pṛthivī vibho
