b ṛṣīṇāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā jagāmāśramam uttamam
b tasyāśrame 'śvamedhasya phaḷam āpnoti mānavaḥ
c ṛṣīṃs tān abhivādyātha pārśve himavato 'cyutaḥ
e skandhāvārāṇi sarvāṇi nivartyāruruhe 'calam
a nātidūraṃ tato gatvā nagaṃ tāladhvajo balī
c puṇyaṃ tīrthavaraṃ dṛṣṭvā vismayaṃ paramaṃ gataḥ
a prabhavaṃ ca sarasvatyāḥ plakṣaprasravaṇaṃ balaḥ
c saṃprāptaḥ kārapacanaṃ tīrthapravaram uttamam
a halāyudhas tatra cāpi dattvā dānaṃ mahābalaḥ
c āplutaḥ salile śīte tasmāc cāpi jagāma ha
e āśramaṃ paramaprīto mitrasya varuṇasya ca
f āplutaḥ salile puṇye suśīte vimale śucau
f saṃtarpayām āsa pitṝn devāṃś ca raṇadurmadaḥ
f tatroṣyaikāṃ tu rajanīṃ yatibhir brāhmaṇaiḥ saha
f mitrāvaruṇayoḥ puṇyaṃ jagāmāśramam acyutaḥ
a indro 'gnir aryamā caiva yatra prāk prītim āpnuvan
c taṃ deśaṃ kārapacanād yamunāyāṃ jagāma ha
a snātvā tatrāpi dharmātmā parāṃ tuṣṭim avāpya ca
c ṛṣibhiś caiva siddhaiś ca sahito vai mahābalaḥ
e upaviṣṭaḥ kathāḥ śubhrāḥ śuśrāva yadupuṃgavaḥ
a tathā tu tiṣṭhatāṃ teṣāṃ nārado bhagavān ṛṣiḥ
c ājagāmātha taṃ deśaṃ yatra rāmo vyavasthitaḥ
d tatra saṃtiṣṭhataś cātha rāmasyāpratimadyuteḥ
d ājagāma mahātejā nārado bhagavān ṛṣiḥ
a jaṭāmaṇḍalasaṃvītaḥ svarṇacīrī mahātapāḥ
c hemadaṇḍadharo rājan kamaṇḍaludharas tathā
a kacchapīṃ sukhaśabdāṃ tāṃ gṛhya vīṇāṃ manoramām
c nṛtye gīte ca kuśalo devabrāhmaṇapūjitaḥ
a prakartā kalahānāṃ ca nityaṃ ca kalahapriyaḥ
c taṃ deśam agamad yatra śrīmān rāmo vyavasthitaḥ
a pratyutthāya tu te sarve pūjayitvā yatavratam
c devarṣiṃ paryapṛcchanta yathāvṛttaṃ kurūn prati
a tato 'syākathayad rājan nāradaḥ sarvadharmavit
c sarvam eva yathāvṛttam atītaṃ kurusaṃkṣayam
a tato 'bravīd rauhiṇeyo nāradaṃ dīnayā girā
c kim avasthaṃ tu tat kṣatraṃ ye ca tatrābhavan nṛpāḥ
a śrutam etan mayā pūrvaṃ sarvam eva tapodhana
c vistaraśravaṇe jātaṃ kautūhalam atīva me
 nārada uvāca
a pūrvam eva hato bhīṣmo droṇaḥ sindhupatis tathā
c hato vaikartanaḥ karṇaḥ putrāś cāsya mahārathāḥ
a bhūriśravā rauhiṇeya madrarājaś ca vīryavān
c ete cānye ca bahavas tatra tatra mahābalāḥ
a priyān prāṇān parityajya priyārthaṃ kauravasya vai
c rājāno rājaputrāś ca samareṣv anivartinaḥ
d nihatāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sarve gatāḥ svargagatiṃ prati
a ahatāṃs tu mahābāho śṛṇu me tatra mādhava
c dhārtarāṣṭrabale śeṣāḥ kṛpo bhojaś ca vīryavān
e aśvatthāmā ca vikrānto bhagnasainyā diśo gatāḥ
f   trayaḥ samitimardanāḥ
f kṛpaś ca kṛtavarmā ca droṇaputraś ca vīryavān
f te 'pi vai vidrutā rāma diśo daśa bhayāt tadā
a duryodhano hate sainye pradruteṣu kṛpādiṣu
c hradaṃ dvaipāyanaṃ nāma viveśa bhṛśaduḥkhitaḥ
a śayānaṃ dhārtarāṣṭraṃ tu stambhite salile tadā
c pāṇḍavāḥ saha kṛṣṇena vāgbhir ugrābhir ārdayan
a sa tudyamāno balavān vāgbhī rāma samantataḥ
c utthitaḥ prāg ghradād vīraḥ pragṛhya mahatīṃ gadām
a sa cāpy upagato yuddhaṃ bhīmena saha sāṃpratam
c bhaviṣyati ca tat sadyas tayo rāma sudāruṇam
a yadi kautūhalaṃ te 'sti vraja mādhava mā ciram
c paśya yuddhaṃ mahāghoraṃ śiṣyayor yadi manyase
c   adya rāmāhave dvayoḥ
c bhīmakauravayor vīra
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a nāradasya vacaḥ śrutvā tān abhyarcya dvijarṣabhān
c sarvān visarjayām āsa ye tenābhyāgatāḥ saha
e gamyatāṃ dvārakāṃ ceti so 'nvaśād anuyāyinaḥ
a so 'vatīryācalaśreṣṭhāt plakṣaprasravaṇāc chubhāt
c tataḥ prītamanā rāmaḥ śrutvā tīrthaphalaṃ mahat
e viprāṇāṃ saṃnidhau ślokam agāyad idam acyutaḥ
a sarasvatīvāsasamā kuto ratiḥ
sarasvatīvāsasamāḥ kuto guṇāḥ
c sarasvatīṃ prāpya divaṃ gatā janāḥ
sadā smariṣyanti nadīṃ sarasvatīm
a sarasvatī sarvanadīṣu puṇyā
sarasvatī lokasukhāvahā sadā
c sarasvatīṃ prāpya janāḥ suduṣkṛtāḥ
sadā na śocanti paratra ceha ca
a tato muhur muhuḥ prītyā prekṣamāṇaḥ sarasvatīm
c hayair yuktaṃ rathaṃ śubhram ātiṣṭhata paraṃtapaḥ
a sa śīghragāminā tena rathena yadupuṃgavaḥ
c didṛkṣur abhisaṃprāptaḥ śiṣyayuddham upasthitam
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evaṃ tad abhavad yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ janamejaya
c yatra duḥkhānvito rājā dhṛtarāṣṭro 'bravīd idam
a rāmaṃ saṃnihitaṃ dṛṣṭvā gadāyuddha upasthite
c mama putraḥ kathaṃ bhīmaṃ pratyayudhyata saṃjaya
 saṃjaya uvāca
a rāmasāṃnidhyam āsādya putro duryodhanas tava
c yuddhakāmo mahābāhuḥ samahṛṣyata vīryavān
a dṛṣṭvā lāṅgalinaṃ rājā pratyutthāya ca bhārata
c prītyā paramayā yukto yudhiṣṭhiram athābravīt
c   samabhyarcya yathāvidhi
c āsanaṃ ca dadau tasmai paryapṛcchad anāmayam
c tato yudhiṣṭhiraṃ rāmo vākyam etad uvāca ha
c madhuraṃ dharmasaṃyuktaṃ śūrāṇāṃ hitam eva ca
c mayā śrutaṃ kathayatām ṛṣīṇāṃ rājasattama
c kurukṣetraṃ paraṃ puṇyaṃ pāvanaṃ svargyam eva ca
c daivatair ṛṣibhir juṣṭaṃ brāhmaṇaiś ca mahātmabhiḥ
c tatra vai yotsyamānā ye dehaṃ tyakṣyanti mānavāḥ
c teṣāṃ svarge dhruvo vāsaḥ śakreṇa saha māriṣa
a samantapañcakaṃ kṣipram ito yāma viśāṃ pate
c prathitottaravedī sā devaloke prajāpateḥ
a tasmin mahāpuṇyatame trailokyasya sanātane
c saṃgrāme nidhanaṃ prāpya dhruvaṃ svargo bhaviṣyati
a tathety uktvā mahārāja kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c samantapañcakaṃ vīraḥ prāyād abhimukhaḥ prabhuḥ
a tato duryodhano rājā pragṛhya mahatīṃ gadām
c padbhyām amarṣād dyutimān agacchat pāṇḍavaiḥ saha
a tathā yāntaṃ gadāhastaṃ varmaṇā cāpi daṃśitam
c antarikṣagatā devāḥ sādhu sādhv ity apūjayan
e vātikāś ca narā ye 'tra dṛṣṭvā te harṣam āgatāḥ
a sa pāṇḍavaiḥ parivṛtaḥ kururājas tavātmajaḥ
c mattasyeva gajendrasya gatim āsthāya so 'vrajat
a tataḥ śaṅkhaninādena bherīṇāṃ ca mahāsvanaiḥ
c siṃhanādaiś ca śūrāṇāṃ diśaḥ sarvāḥ prapūritāḥ
d tatas te tu kurukṣetraṃ prāptā naravarottamāḥ
a pratīcyabhimukhaṃ deśaṃ yathoddiṣṭaṃ sutena te
c gatvā ca taiḥ parikṣiptaṃ samantāt sarvatodiśam
a dakṣiṇena sarasvatyāḥ svayanaṃ tīrtham uttamam
c tasmin deśe tv aniriṇe tatra yuddham arocayan
a tato bhīmo mahākoṭiṃ gadāṃ gṛhyātha varmabhṛt
c bibhrad rūpaṃ mahārāja sadṛśaṃ hi garutmataḥ
a avabaddhaśirastrāṇaḥ saṃkhye kāñcanavarmabhṛt
c rarāja rājan putras te kāñcanaḥ śailarāḍ iva
a varmabhyāṃ saṃvṛtau vīrau bhīmaduryodhanāv ubhau
c saṃyuge ca prakāśete saṃrabdhāv iva kuñjarau
a raṇamaṇḍalamadhyasthau bhrātarau tau nararṣabhau
c aśobhetāṃ mahārāja candrasūryāv ivoditau
a tāv anyonyaṃ nirīkṣetāṃ kruddhāv iva mahādvipau
c dahantau locanai rājan parasparavadhaiṣiṇau
a saṃprahṛṣṭamanā rājan gadām ādāya kauravaḥ
c sṛkkiṇī saṃlihan rājan krodharaktekṣaṇaḥ śvasan
a tato duryodhano rājā gadām ādāya vīryavān
c bhīmasenam abhiprekṣya gajo gajam ivāhvayat
a adrisāramayīṃ bhīmas tathaivādāya vīryavān
c āhvayām āsa nṛpatiṃ siṃhaḥ siṃhaṃ yathā vane
a tāv udyatagadāpāṇī duryodhanavṛkodarau
c saṃyuge sma prakāśete girī saśikharāv iva
a tāv ubhāv abhisaṃkruddhāv ubhau bhīmaparākramau
c ubhau śiṣyau gadāyuddhe rauhiṇeyasya dhīmataḥ
a ubhau sadṛśakarmāṇau yamavāsavayor iva
c tathā sadṛśakarmāṇau varuṇasya mahābalau
a vāsudevasya rāmasya tathā vaiśravaṇasya ca
c sadṛśau tau mahārāja madhukaiṭabhayor yudhi
a ubhau sadṛśakarmāṇau raṇe sundopasundayoḥ
b rāmarāvaṇayoś caiva vālisugrīvayos tathā
c tathaiva kālasya samau mṛtyoś caiva paraṃtapau
a anyonyam abhidhāvantau mattāv iva mahādvipau
c vāśitāsaṃgame dṛptau śaradīva madotkaṭau
a mattāv iva jigīṣantau mātaṅgau bharatarṣabhau
c ubhau krodhaviṣaṃ dīptaṃ vamantāv uragāv iva
a anyonyam abhisaṃrabdhau prekṣamāṇāv ariṃdamau
c ubhau bharataśārdūlau vikrameṇa samanvitau
a siṃhāv iva durādharṣau gadāyuddhe paraṃtapau
c nakhadaṃṣṭrāyudhau vīrau vyāghrāv iva durutsahau
a prajāsaṃharaṇe kṣubdhau samudrāv iva dustarau
c lohitāṅgāv iva kruddhau pratapantau mahārathau
d pūrvapaścimajau meghau vāyunā kṣubhitau yathā
d garjamānau suviṣamaṃ kṣarantau prāvṛṣīva hi
a raśmimantau mahātmānau dīptimantau mahābalau
c dadṛśāte kuruśreṣṭhau kālasūryāv ivoditau
a vyāghrāv iva susaṃrabdhau garjantāv iva toyadau
c jahṛṣāte mahābāhū siṃhau kesariṇāv iva
a gajāv iva susaṃrabdhau jvalitāv iva pāvakau
c dadṛśus tau mahātmānau saśṛṅgāv iva parvatau
a roṣāt prasphuramāṇoṣṭhau nirīkṣantau parasparam
c tau sametau mahātmānau gadāhastau narottamau
a ubhau paramasaṃhṛṣṭāv ubhau paramasaṃmatau
c sadaśvāv iva heṣantau bṛṃhantāv iva kuñjarau
a vṛṣabhāv iva garjantau duryodhanavṛkodarau
c daityāv iva balonmattau rejatus tau narottamau
a tato duryodhano rājann idam āha yudhiṣṭhiram
b bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitaṃ caiva kṛṣṇena ca mahātmanā
b rāmeṇāmitavīryeṇa vākyaṃ śauṇḍīryasaṃmatam
c sṛñjayaiḥ saha tiṣṭhantaṃ tapantam iva bhāskaram
d kekayaiḥ sṛñjayair guptaṃ pāñcālaiś ca mahātmabhiḥ
a idaṃ vyavasitaṃ yuddhaṃ mama bhīmasya cobhayoḥ
c upopaviṣṭāḥ paśyadhvaṃ vimardaṃ nṛpasattamāḥ
d śrutvā duryodhanavacaḥ pratyapadyanta tat tathā
a tataḥ samupaviṣṭaṃ tat sumahad rājamaṇḍalam
c virājamānaṃ dadṛśe divīvādityamaṇḍalam
a teṣāṃ madhye mahābāhuḥ śrīmān keśavapūrvajaḥ
c upaviṣṭo mahārāja pūjyamānaḥ samantataḥ
a śuśubhe rājamadhyastho nīlavāsāḥ sitaprabhaḥ
c nakṣatrair iva saṃpūrṇo vṛto niśi niśākaraḥ
a tau tathā tu mahārāja gadāhastau durāsadau
c anyonyaṃ vāgbhir ugrābhis takṣamāṇau vyavasthitau
a apriyāṇi tato 'nyonyam uktvā tau kurupuṃgavau
c udīkṣantau sthitau vīrau vṛtraśakrāv ivāhave
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tato vāgyuddham abhavat tumulaṃ janamejaya
a   tumulaṃ romaharṣaṇam
a krodhasaṃvardhanaṃ niṣṭhām sic
c yatra duḥkhānvito rājā dhṛtarāṣṭro 'bravīd idam
a dhig astu khalu mānuṣyaṃ yasya niṣṭheyam īdṛśī
c ekādaśacamūbhartā yatra putro mamābhibhūḥ
a ājñāpya sarvān nṛpatīn bhuktvā cemāṃ vasuṃdharām
c gadām ādāya vegena padātiḥ prasthito raṇam
a bhūtvā hi jagato nātho hy anātha iva me sutaḥ
c gadām udyamya yo yāti kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥ
a aho duḥkhaṃ mahat prāptaṃ putreṇa mama saṃjaya
c evam uktvā sa duḥkhārto virarāma janādhipaḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a sa meghaninado harṣād vinadann iva govṛṣaḥ
c ājuhāva tataḥ pārthaṃ yuddhāya yudhi vīryavān
a bhīmam āhvayamāne tu kururāje mahātmani
b ājuhāva tato bhīmo yuddhāya ca suyodhanam
b evam āhvayamāne tu bhīmasene mahātmani
c prādurāsan sughorāṇi rūpāṇi vividhāny uta
a vavur vātāḥ sanirghātāḥ pāṃsuvarṣaṃ papāta ca
c babhūvuś ca diśaḥ sarvās timireṇa samāvṛtāḥ
a mahāsvanāḥ sanirghātās tumulā romaharṣaṇāḥ
c petus tatholkāḥ śataśaḥ sphoṭayantyo nabhastalam
a rāhuś cāgrasad ādityam aparvaṇi viśāṃ pate
c cakampe ca mahākampaṃ pṛthivī savanadrumā
a rūkṣāś ca vātāḥ pravavur nīcaiḥ śarkaravarṣiṇaḥ
c girīṇāṃ śikharāṇy eva nyapatanta mahītale
a mṛgā bahuvidhākārāḥ saṃpatanti diśo daśa
c dīptāḥ śivāś cāpy anadan ghorarūpāḥ sudāruṇāḥ
a nirghātāś ca mahāghorā babhūvū romaharṣaṇāḥ
c dīptāyāṃ diśi rājendra mṛgāś cāśubhavādinaḥ
a udapānagatāś cāpo vyavardhanta samantataḥ
c aśarīrā mahānādāḥ śrūyante sma tadā nṛpa
a evamādīni dṛṣṭvātha nimittāni vṛkodaraḥ
c uvāca bhrātaraṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
a naiṣa śakto raṇe jetuṃ mandātmā māṃ suyodhanaḥ
c adya krodhaṃ vimokṣyāmi nigūḍhaṃ hṛdaye ciram
e suyodhane kauravendre khāṇḍave pāvako yathā
a śalyam adyoddhariṣyāmi tava pāṇḍava hṛcchayam
c nihatya gadayā pāpam imaṃ kurukulādhamam
a adya kīrtimayīṃ mālāṃ pratimokṣyāmy ahaṃ tvayi
c hatvemaṃ pāpakarmāṇaṃ gadayā raṇamūrdhani
a adyāsya śatadhā dehaṃ bhinadmi gadayānayā
c nāyaṃ praveṣṭā nagaraṃ punar vāraṇasāhvayam
a sarpotsargasya śayane viṣadānasya bhojane
c pramāṇakoṭyāṃ pātasya dāhasya jatuveśmani
a sabhāyām avahāsasya sarvasvaharaṇasya ca
c varṣam ajñātavāsasya vanavāsasya cānagha
d draupadyāḥ kleśadānasya vastrasaṃharaṇasya ca
a adyāntam eṣāṃ duḥkhānāṃ gantā bharatasattama
c ekāhnā vinihatyemaṃ bhaviṣyāmy ātmano 'nṛṇaḥ
a adyāyur dhārtarāṣṭrasya durmater akṛtātmanaḥ
c samāptaṃ bharataśreṣṭha mātāpitroś ca darśanam
d adya saukhyaṃ tu rājendra kururājasya durmateḥ
d samāptaṃ ca mahārāja nārīṇāṃ darśanaṃ punaḥ
a adyāyaṃ kururājasya śaṃtanoḥ kulapāṃsanaḥ
c prāṇāñ śriyaṃ ca rājyaṃ ca tyaktvā śeṣyati bhūtale
a rājā ca dhṛtarāṣṭro 'dya śrutvā putraṃ mayā hatam
c smariṣyaty aśubhaṃ karma yat tac chakunibuddhijam
a ity uktvā rājaśārdūla gadām ādāya vīryavān
c avātiṣṭhata yuddhāya śakro vṛtram ivāhvayan
a tam udyatagadaṃ dṛṣṭvā kailāsam iva śṛṅgiṇam
c bhīmasenaḥ punaḥ kruddho duryodhanam uvāca ha
a rājñaś ca dhṛtarāṣṭrasya tathā tvam api cātmanaḥ
a   tava hetor durātmanaḥ
a sarveṣām api cāsmākaṃ duḥkhaṃ prāptaṃ sudurmate
c smara tad duṣkṛtaṃ karma yad vṛttaṃ vāraṇāvate
a draupadī ca parikliṣṭā sabhāyāṃ yad rajasvalā
c dyūte ca vañcito rājā yat tvayā saubalena ca
a vane duḥkhaṃ ca yat prāptam asmābhis tvatkṛtaṃ mahat
c virāṭanagare caiva yonyantaragatair iva
e tat sarvaṃ yātayāmy adya diṣṭyā dṛṣṭo 'si durmate
a tvatkṛte 'sau hataḥ śete śaratalpe pratāpavān
c gāṅgeyo rathināṃ śreṣṭho nihato yājñaseninā
a hato droṇaś ca karṇaś ca tathā śalyaḥ pratāpavān
c vairāgner ādikartā ca śakuniḥ saubalo hataḥ
a prātikāmī tathā pāpo draupadyāḥ kleśakṛd dhataḥ
c bhrātaras te hatāḥ sarve śūrā vikrāntayodhinaḥ
a ete cānye ca bahavo nihatās tvatkṛte nṛpāḥ
c tvām adya nihaniṣyāmi gadayā nātra saṃśayaḥ
a ity evam uccai rājendra bhāṣamāṇaṃ vṛkodaram
c uvāca vītabhī rājan putras te satyavikramaḥ
a kiṃ katthitena bahudhā yudhyasva tvaṃ vṛkodara
c adya te 'haṃ vineṣyāmi yuddhaśraddhāṃ kulādhama
d iti duryodhanenoktaḥ pratyuvāca vṛkodaraḥ
a naiva duryodhanaḥ kṣudra kena cit tvadvidhena vai
c śakyas trāsayituṃ vācā yathānyaḥ prākṛto naraḥ
a cirakālepsitaṃ diṣṭyā hṛdayastham idaṃ mama
c tvayā saha gadāyuddhaṃ tridaśair upapāditam
a kiṃ vācā bahunoktena katthitena ca durmate
c vāṇī saṃpadyatām eṣā karmaṇā mā ciraṃ kṛthāḥ
a tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā sarva evābhyapūjayan
c rājānaḥ somakāś caiva ye tatrāsan samāgatāḥ
a tataḥ saṃpūjitaḥ sarvaiḥ saṃprahṛṣṭatanūruhaḥ
c bhūyo dhīraṃ manaś cakre yuddhāya kurunandanaḥ
a taṃ mattam iva mātaṅgaṃ talatālair narādhipāḥ
c bhūyaḥ saṃharṣayāṃ cakrur duryodhanam amarṣaṇam
a taṃ mahātmā mahātmānaṃ gadām udyamya pāṇḍavaḥ
c abhidudrāva vegena dhārtarāṣṭraṃ vṛkodaraḥ
a bṛṃhanti kuñjarās tatra hayā heṣanti cāsakṛt
c śastrāṇi cāpy adīpyanta pāṇḍavānāṃ jayaiṣiṇām
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tato duryodhano dṛṣṭvā bhīmasenaṃ tathāgatam
c pratyudyayāv adīnātmā vegena mahatā nadan
a samāpetatur ānadya śṛṅgiṇau vṛṣabhāv iva
c mahānirghātaghoṣaś ca saṃprahāras tayor abhūt
a abhavac ca tayor yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ romaharṣaṇam
c jigīṣator yudhānyonyam indraprahrādayor iva
d tau vṛṣāv iva garjantau maṇḍalāni viceratuḥ
d āvarjitagadāhastau duryodhanavṛkodarau
d maṇḍalāvartamārgeṣu gadāpraharaṇe 'pi ca
d nirviśeṣam abhūd yuddhaṃ tayoḥ puruṣasiṃhayoḥ
d taptahemamayī śubhrair babhūva bhayavardhanī
d agnijvālair ivāvidhya pade bhīmasya sā gadā
d tāḍitā dhārtarāṣṭreṇa bhīmasya gadayā gadā
d gadāyuddhe mahārāja sasṛje pāvakārciṣaḥ
d aṅgāravarṣaṃ mumuce tad adbhutam ivābhavat
d dantair iva mahānāgau śṛṅgair iva mahāvṛṣau
d tau tu rejatur anyonyaṃ gadābhyām aparikṣatau
d gadayābhihate gātre kṣaṇena rudhirokṣitau
d prekṣaṇīyatarāv āstāṃ puṣpitāv iva kiṃśukau
d gadayā dhārtarāṣṭreṇa savye pārśve bhṛśāhataḥ
d bhīmaseno mahābāhur na cacālācalo yathā
d tadā bhīmagadāvegais tāḍyamāno muhur muhuḥ
d kaṭitvān mocayām āsa duṣṭahastīva hastipam
d śuśruve dikṣu sarvāsu tayoḥ puruṣasiṃhayoḥ
d gadānipātasaṃhrādo vajrayor iva nisvanaḥ
d abhihṛtya mahāvīryau nivṛtya tu mahāgadau
d punar uttamamārgasthau maṇḍalāni viceratuḥ
d tadānyonyam abhidrutya sthitau vīrau mahāgadau
d udyamya lohadaṇḍābhyāṃ tāḍyamānau hi petatuḥ
d punar utpatya vegena maṇḍalāni viceratuḥ
d kriyāviśeṣabalinau darśayām āsatus tadā
d abhyudyatagadau vīrau saśṛṅgāv iva parvatau
d tāv ājaghnatur anyonyaṃ yathā bhūmicale 'calau
d tau parasparasaṃvegād gadābhyāṃ bhṛśam āhatau
d yugapat petatur vīrau tathālakṣya samutthitau
d bhṛśaṃ marmasv abhihatāv ubhāv āstāṃ suvihvalau
d tau parasparasaṃgharṣau prekṣatāṃ hi mahābalau
a rudhirokṣitasarvāṅgau gadāhastau manasvinau
c dadṛśāte mahātmānau puṣpitāv iva kiṃśukau
a tathā tasmin mahāyuddhe vartamāne sudāruṇe
c khadyotasaṃghair iva khaṃ darśanīyaṃ vyarocata
a tathā tasmin vartamāne saṃkule tumule bhṛśam
b saṃgrāme dāruṇe tāta subhṛśaṃ krodhasaṃyutau
c ubhāv api pariśrāntau yudhyamānāv ariṃdamau
a tau muhūrtaṃ samāśvasya punar eva paraṃtapau
c abhyahārayatāṃ tatra saṃpragṛhya gade śubhe
a tau tu dṛṣṭvā mahāvīryau samāśvastau nararṣabhau
c balinau vāraṇau yadvad vāśitārthe madotkaṭau
a apāravīryau saṃprekṣya pragṛhītagadāv ubhau
c vismayaṃ paramaṃ jagmur devagandharvadānavāḥ
a pragṛhītagadau dṛṣṭvā duryodhanavṛkodarau
c saṃśayaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ vijaye samapadyata
a samāgamya tato bhūyo bhrātarau balināṃ varau
c anyonyasyāntaraprepsū pracakrāte 'ntaraṃ prati
a yamadaṇḍopamāṃ gurvīm indrāśanim ivodyatām
c dadṛśuḥ prekṣakā rājan raudrīṃ viśasanīṃ gadām
a āvidhyato gadāṃ tasya bhīmasenasya saṃyuge
c śabdaḥ sutumulo ghoro muhūrtaṃ samapadyata
a āvidhyantam abhiprekṣya dhārtarāṣṭro 'tha pāṇḍavam
c gadām alaghuvegāṃ tāṃ vismitaḥ saṃbabhūva ha
a caraṃś ca vividhān mārgān maṇḍalāni ca bhārata
c aśobhata tadā vīro bhūya eva vṛkodaraḥ
a tau parasparam āsādya yat tāv anyonyarakṣaṇe
c mārjārāv iva bhakṣārthe tatakṣāte muhur muhuḥ
a acarad bhīmasenas tu mārgān bahuvidhāṃs tathā
c maṇḍalāni vicitrāṇi sthānāni vividhāni ca
a gomūtrikāṇi citrāṇi gatapratyāgatāni ca
c parimokṣaṃ prahārāṇāṃ varjanaṃ paridhāvanam
a abhidravaṇam ākṣepam avasthānaṃ savigraham
c parāvartanasaṃvartam avaplutam athāplutam
e upanyastam apanyastaṃ gadāyuddhaviśāradau
a evaṃ tau vicarantau tu nyaghnatāṃ vai parasparam
c vañcayantau punaś caiva ceratuḥ kurusattamau
a vikrīḍantau subalinau maṇḍalāni praceratuḥ
c gadāhastau tatas tau tu maṇḍalāvasthitau balī
a dakṣiṇaṃ maṇḍalaṃ rājan dhārtarāṣṭro 'bhyavartata
c savyaṃ tu maṇḍalaṃ tatra bhīmaseno 'bhyavartata
a tathā tu caratas tasya bhīmasya raṇamūrdhani
c duryodhano mahārāja pārśvadeśe 'bhyatāḍayat
a āhatas tu tadā bhīmas tava putreṇa bhārata
c āvidhyata gadāṃ gurvīṃ prahāraṃ tam acintayan
a indrāśanisamāṃ ghorāṃ yamadaṇḍam ivodyatām
c dadṛśus te mahārāja bhīmasenasya tāṃ gadām
a āvidhyantaṃ gadāṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīmasenaṃ tavātmajaḥ
c samudyamya gadāṃ ghorāṃ pratyavidhyad ariṃdamaḥ
d yamadaṇḍanibhāṃ rājan ghorāṃ prati ariṃdamaḥ
a gadāmārutavegena tava putrasya bhārata
c śabda āsīt sutumulas tejaś ca samajāyata
d śabda āsīn mahāṃs tatra tumulo lomaharṣaṇaḥ
a sa caran vividhān mārgān maṇḍalāni ca bhāgaśaḥ
c samaśobhata tejasvī bhūyo bhīmāt suyodhanaḥ
a āviddhā sarvavegena bhīmena mahatī gadā
c sadhūmaṃ sārciṣaṃ cāgniṃ mumocogrā mahāsvanā
d udvamac cārciṣo vahniṃ sasphuliṅgaṃ samantataḥ
a ādhūtāṃ bhīmasenena gadāṃ dṛṣṭvā suyodhanaḥ
c adrisāramayīṃ gurvīm āvidhyan bahv aśobhata
a gadāmārutavegaṃ hi dṛṣṭvā tasya mahātmanaḥ
c bhayaṃ viveśa pāṇḍūn vai sarvān eva sasomakān
a tau darśayantau samare yuddhakrīḍāṃ samantataḥ
c gadābhyāṃ sahasānyonyam ājaghnatur ariṃdamau
a tau parasparam āsādya daṃṣṭrābhyāṃ dviradau yathā
c aśobhetāṃ mahārāja śoṇitena pariplutau
a evaṃ tad abhavad yuddhaṃ ghorarūpam asaṃvṛtam
c parivṛtte 'hani krūraṃ vṛtravāsavayor iva
a dṛṣṭvā vyavasthitaṃ bhīmaṃ tava putro mahābalaḥ
c caraṃś citratarān mārgān kaunteyam abhidudruve
a tasya bhīmo mahāvegāṃ jāmbūnadapariṣkṛtām
c abhikruddhasya kruddhas tu tāḍayām āsa tāṃ gadām
a savisphuliṅgo nirhrādas tayos tatrābhighātajaḥ
c prādurāsīn mahārāja sṛṣṭayor vajrayor iva
a vegavatyā tayā tatra bhīmasenapramuktayā
c nipatantyā mahārāja pṛthivī samakampata
a tāṃ nāmṛṣyata kauravyo gadāṃ pratihatāṃ raṇe
c matto dvipa iva kruddhaḥ pratikuñjaradarśanāt
a sa savyaṃ maṇḍalaṃ rājann udbhrāmya kṛtaniścayaḥ
c ājaghne mūrdhni kaunteyaṃ gadayā bhīmavegayā
a tayā tv abhihato bhīmaḥ putreṇa tava pāṇḍavaḥ
c nākampata mahārāja tad adbhutam ivābhavat
a āścaryaṃ cāpi tad rājan sarvasainyāny apūjayan
c yad gadābhihato bhīmo nākampata padāt padam
a tato gurutarāṃ dīptāṃ gadāṃ hemapariṣkṛtām
c duryodhanāya vyasṛjad bhīmo bhīmaparākramaḥ
a taṃ prahāram asaṃbhrānto lāghavena mahābalaḥ
c moghaṃ duryodhanaś cakre tatrābhūd vismayo mahān
a sā tu moghā gadā rājan patantī bhīmacoditā
c cālayām āsa pṛthivīṃ mahānirghātanisvanā
a āsthāya kauśikān mārgān utpatan sa punaḥ punaḥ
b gadānipātaṃ kriyayā moghaṃ cakre sutas tava
b sa gadāvarjitaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīmasenam upādravat
b so 'gacchac calito rājan kaunteyas trirathāntaram
c gadānipātaṃ prajñāya bhīmasenam avañcayat
a vañcayitvā tathā bhīmaṃ gadayā kurusattamaḥ
c tāḍayām āsa saṃkruddho vakṣodeśe mahābalaḥ
a gadayābhihato bhīmo muhyamāno mahāraṇe
c nābhyamanyata kartavyaṃ putreṇābhyāhatas tava
a tasmiṃs tathā vartamāne rājan somakapāṇḍavāḥ
c bhṛśopahatasaṃkalpā nahṛṣṭamanaso 'bhavan
a sa tu tena prahāreṇa mātaṅga iva roṣitaḥ
c hastivad dhastisaṃkāśam abhidudrāva te sutam
a tatas tu rabhaso bhīmo gadayā tanayaṃ tava
c abhidudrāva vegena siṃho vanagajaṃ yathā
a upasṛtya tu rājānaṃ gadāmokṣaviśāradaḥ
c āvidhyata gadāṃ rājan samuddiśya sutaṃ tava
a atāḍayad bhīmasenaḥ pārśve duryodhanaṃ tadā
c sa vihvalaḥ prahāreṇa jānubhyām agaman mahīm
a tasmiṃs tu bharataśreṣṭhe jānubhyām avanīṃ gate
c udatiṣṭhat tato nādaḥ sṛñjayānāṃ jagatpate
a teṣāṃ tu ninadaṃ śrutvā sṛñjayānāṃ nararṣabhaḥ
c amarṣād bharataśreṣṭha putras te samakupyata
a utthāya tu mahābāhuḥ kruddho nāga iva śvasan
c didhakṣann iva netrābhyāṃ bhīmasenam avaikṣata
a tataḥ sa bharataśreṣṭho gadāpāṇir abhidravat
c pramathiṣyann iva śiro bhīmasenasya saṃyuge
a sa mahātmā mahātmānaṃ bhīmaṃ bhīmaparākramaḥ
c atāḍayac chaṅkhadeśe sa cacālācalopamaḥ
a sa bhūyaḥ śuśubhe pārthas tāḍito gadayā raṇe
c udbhinnarudhiro rājan prabhinna iva kuñjaraḥ
d sa saṃkruddho mahārāja bhīmo bhīmaparākramaḥ
a tato gadāṃ vīrahaṇīm ayasmayīṃ
pragṛhya vajrāśanitulyanisvanām
c atāḍayac chatrum amitrakarśano
balena vikramya dhanaṃjayāgrajaḥ
a sa bhīmasenābhihatas tavātmajaḥ
papāta saṃkampitadehabandhanaḥ
c supuṣpito mārutavegatāḍito
mahāvane sāla ivāvaghūrṇitaḥ
a tataḥ praṇedur jahṛṣuś ca pāṇḍavāḥ
samīkṣya putraṃ patitaṃ kṣitau tava
c tataḥ sutas te pratilabhya cetanāṃ
samutpapāta dvirado yathā hradāt
a sa pārthivo nityam amarṣitas tadā
mahārathaḥ śikṣitavat paribhraman
c atāḍayat pāṇḍavam agrataḥ sthitaṃ
sa vihvalāṅgo jagatīm upāspṛśat
a sa siṃhanādān vinanāda kauravo
nipātya bhūmau yudhi bhīmam ojasā
c bibheda caivāśanitulyatejasā
gadānipātena śarīrarakṣaṇam
a tato 'ntarikṣe ninado mahān abhūd
divaukasām apsarasāṃ ca neduṣām
c papāta coccair amarapraveritaṃ
vicitrapuṣpotkaravarṣam uttamam
a tataḥ parān āviśad uttamaṃ bhayaṃ
samīkṣya bhūmau patitaṃ narottamam
c ahīyamānaṃ ca balena kauravaṃ
niśamya bhedaṃ ca dṛḍhasya varmaṇaḥ
a tato muhūrtād upalabhya cetanāṃ
pramṛjya vaktraṃ rudhirārdram ātmanaḥ
c dhṛtiṃ samālambya vivṛttalocano
balena saṃstabhya vṛkodaraḥ sthitaḥ
d tato yamau yamasadṛśau parākrame
d sapārṣataḥ śinitanayaś ca vīryavān
d samāhvayann aham aham ity abhitvaraṃs
d tavātmajaṃ samabhiyayur vadhaiṣiṇaḥ
d nigṛhya tān punar api pāṇḍavo balī
d tavātmajaṃ svayam abhigamya kālavat
d cacāra ca vyapagatakhedavepathuḥ
d sureśvaro namucim ivottamaṃ raṇe
 saṃjaya uvāca
a samudīrṇaṃ tato dṛṣṭvā saṃgrāmaṃ kurumukhyayoḥ
c athābravīd arjunas tu vāsudevaṃ yaśasvinam
a anayor vīrayor yuddhe ko jyāyān bhavato mataḥ
c kasya vā ko guṇo bhūyān etad vada janārdana
 vāsudeva uvāca
a upadeśo 'nayos tulyo bhīmas tu balavattaraḥ
c kṛtayatnataras tv eṣa dhārtarāṣṭro vṛkodarāt
a bhīmasenas tu dharmeṇa yudhyamāno na jeṣyati
c anyāyena tu yudhyan vai hanyād eṣa suyodhanam
a māyayā nirjitā devair asurā iti naḥ śrutam
c virocanaś ca śakreṇa māyayā nirjitaḥ sakhe
e māyayā cākṣipat tejo vṛtrasya balasūdanaḥ
f tasmān māyāmayaṃ bhīma ātiṣṭhatu parākramam
f karotu bhīmaḥ samayaṃ balam āsthāya vīryavān
a pratijñātaṃ tu bhīmena dyūtakāle dhanaṃjaya
c ūrū bhetsyāmi te saṃkhye gadayeti suyodhanam
a so 'yaṃ pratijñāṃ tāṃ cāpi pārayitvārikarśanaḥ
c māyāvinaṃ ca rājānaṃ māyayaiva nikṛntatu
a yady eṣa balam āsthāya nyāyena prahariṣyati
c viṣamasthas tato rājā bhaviṣyati yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a punar eva ca vakṣyāmi pāṇḍavedaṃ nibodha me
c dharmarājāparādhena bhayaṃ naḥ punarāgatam
a kṛtvā hi sumahat karma hatvā bhīṣmamukhān kurūn
c jayaḥ prāpto yaśaś cāgryaṃ vairaṃ ca pratiyātitam
e tad evaṃ vijayaḥ prāptaḥ punaḥ saṃśayitaḥ kṛtaḥ
a abuddhir eṣā mahatī dharmarājasya pāṇḍava
c yad ekavijaye yuddhaṃ paṇitaṃ kṛtam īdṛśam
e suyodhanaḥ kṛtī vīra ekāyanagatas tathā
a api cośanasā gītaḥ śrūyate 'yaṃ purātanaḥ
c ślokas tattvārthasahitas tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇu
d asminn arthe purāṇo 'yaṃ śloko 'pi niyataḥ kila
d śrutaś cośanasā gītaḥ satāṃ nītividāṃ mataḥ
a punarāvartamānānāṃ bhagnānāṃ jīvitaiṣiṇām
c bhetavyam ariśeṣāṇām ekāyanagatā hi te
d sāhasotpatitānāṃ ca nirāśānāṃ ca jīvite
d na śakyam agrataḥ sthātuṃ śakreṇāpi dhanaṃjaya
a suyodhanam imaṃ bhagnaṃ hatasainyaṃ hradaṃ gatam
c parājitaṃ vanaprepsuṃ nirāśaṃ rājyalambhane
a ko nv eṣa saṃyuge prājñaḥ punar dvaṃdve samāhvayet
c api vo nirjitaṃ rājyaṃ na hareta suyodhanaḥ
a yas trayodaśavarṣāṇi gadayā kṛtaniśramaḥ
c caraty ūrdhvaṃ ca tiryak ca bhīmasenajighāṃsayā
a evaṃ cen na mahābāhur anyāyena haniṣyati
c eṣa vaḥ kauravo rājā dhārtarāṣṭro bhaviṣyati
a dhanaṃjayas tu śrutvaitat keśavasya mahātmanaḥ
c prekṣato bhīmasenasya hastenorum atāḍayat
a gṛhya saṃjñāṃ tato bhīmo gadayā vyacarad raṇe
c maṇḍalāni vicitrāṇi yamakānītarāṇi ca
a dakṣiṇaṃ maṇḍalaṃ savyaṃ gomūtrakam athāpi ca
c vyacarat pāṇḍavo rājann ariṃ saṃmohayann iva
a tathaiva tava putro 'pi gadāmārgaviśāradaḥ
c vyacaral laghu citraṃ ca bhīmasenajighāṃsayā
a ādhunvantau gade ghore candanāgarurūṣite
c vairasyāntaṃ parīpsantau raṇe kruddhāv ivāntakau
a anyonyaṃ tau jighāṃsantau pravīrau puruṣarṣabhau
c yuyudhāte garutmantau yathā nāgāmiṣaiṣiṇau
a maṇḍalāni vicitrāṇi carator nṛpabhīmayoḥ
c gadāsaṃpātajās tatra prajajñuḥ pāvakārciṣaḥ
a samaṃ praharatos tatra śūrayor balinor mṛdhe
c kṣubdhayor vāyunā rājan dvayor iva samudrayoḥ
a tayoḥ praharatos tulyaṃ mattakuñjarayor iva
c gadānirghātasaṃhrādaḥ prahārāṇām ajāyata
a tasmiṃs tadā saṃprahāre dāruṇe saṃkule bhṛśam
c ubhāv api pariśrāntau yudhyamānāv ariṃdamau
a tau muhūrtaṃ samāśvasya punar eva paraṃtapau
c abhyahārayatāṃ kruddhau pragṛhya mahatī gade
a tayoḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ ghorarūpam asaṃvṛtam
c gadānipātai rājendra takṣator vai parasparam
a vyāyāmapradrutau tau tu vṛṣabhākṣau tarasvinau
c anyonyaṃ jaghnatur vīrau paṅkasthau mahiṣāv iva
a jarjarīkṛtasarvāṅgau rudhireṇābhisaṃplutau
c dadṛśāte himavati puṣpitāv iva kiṃśukau
a duryodhanena pārthas tu vivare saṃpradarśite
c īṣad utsmayamānas tu sahasā prasasāra ha
a tam abhyāśagataṃ prājño raṇe prekṣya vṛkodaraḥ
c avākṣipad gadāṃ tasmai vegena mahatā balī
a avakṣepaṃ tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā putras tava viśāṃ pate
c apāsarpat tataḥ sthānāt sā moghā nyapatad bhuvi
a mokṣayitvā prahāraṃ taṃ sutas tava sa saṃbhramāt
c bhīmasenaṃ ca gadayā prāharat kurusattamaḥ
a tasya viṣyandamānena rudhireṇāmitaujasaḥ
b samāplutasya bhīmasya krodharaktekṣaṇasya ca
c prahāragurupātāc ca mūrcheva samajāyata
a duryodhanas taṃ ca veda pīḍitaṃ pāṇḍavaṃ raṇe
c dhārayām āsa bhīmo 'pi śarīram atipīḍitam
a amanyata sthitaṃ hy enaṃ prahariṣyantam āhave
c ato na prāharat tasmai punar eva tavātmajaḥ
a tato muhūrtam āśvasya duryodhanam avasthitam
c vegenābhyadravad rājan bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavān
a tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya saṃrabdham amitaujasam
c mogham asya prahāraṃ taṃ cikīrṣur bharatarṣabha
a avasthāne matiṃ kṛtvā putras tava mahāmanāḥ
c iyeṣotpatituṃ rājaṃś chalayiṣyan vṛkodaram
a abudhyad bhīmasenas tad rājñas tasya cikīrṣitam
c athāsya samabhidrutya samutkramya ca siṃhavat
a sṛtyā vañcayato rājan punar evotpatiṣyataḥ
c ūrubhyāṃ prāhiṇod rājan gadāṃ vegena pāṇḍavaḥ
a sā vajraniṣpeṣasamā prahitā bhīmakarmaṇā
c ūrū duryodhanasyātha babhañja priyadarśanau
a sa papāta naravyāghro vasudhām anunādayan
c bhagnorur bhīmasenena putras tava mahīpate
a vavur vātāḥ sanirghātāḥ pāṃsuvarṣaṃ papāta ca
c cacāla pṛthivī cāpi savṛkṣakṣupaparvatā
a tasmin nipatite vīre patyau sarvamahīkṣitām
c mahāsvanā punar dīptā sanirghātā bhayaṃkarī
e papāta colkā mahatī patite pṛthivīpatau
a tathā śoṇitavarṣaṃ ca pāṃsuvarṣaṃ ca bhārata
c vavarṣa maghavāṃs tatra tava putre nipātite
a yakṣāṇāṃ rākṣasānāṃ ca piśācānāṃ tathaiva ca
c antarikṣe mahānādaḥ śrūyate bharatarṣabha
a tena śabdena ghoreṇa mṛgāṇām atha pakṣiṇām
c jajñe ghoratamaḥ śabdo bahūnāṃ sarvatodiśam
a ye tatra vājinaḥ śeṣā gajāś ca manujaiḥ saha
c mumucus te mahānādaṃ tava putre nipātite
a bherīśaṅkhamṛdaṅgānām abhavac ca svano mahān
c antarbhūmigataś caiva tava putre nipātite
a bahupādair bahubhujaiḥ kabandhair ghoradarśanaiḥ
c nṛtyadbhir bhayadair vyāptā diśas tatrābhavan nṛpa
a dhvajavanto 'stravantaś ca śastravantas tathaiva ca
c prākampanta tato rājaṃs tava putre nipātite
a hradāḥ kūpāś ca rudhiram udvemur nṛpasattama
c nadyaś ca sumahāvegāḥ pratisrotovahābhavan
a pulliṅgā iva nāryas tu strīliṅgāḥ puruṣābhavan
c duryodhane tadā rājan patite tanaye tava
a dṛṣṭvā tān adbhutotpātān pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha
b sṛñjayāś ca mahārāja sarva eva mahārathāḥ
c āvignamanasaḥ sarve babhūvur bharatarṣabha
d prahṛṣṭamanasaś cāsan pāṇḍavāḥ sṛñjayaiḥ saha
a yayur devā yathākāmaṃ gandharvāpsarasas tathā
c kathayanto 'dbhutaṃ yuddhaṃ sutayos tava bhārata
a tathaiva siddhā rājendra tathā vātikacāraṇāḥ
c narasiṃhau praśaṃsantau viprajagmur yathāgatam
 saṃjaya uvāca
a taṃ pātitaṃ tato dṛṣṭvā mahāśālam ivodgatam
c prahṛṣṭamanasaḥ sarve babhūvus tatra pāṇḍavāḥ
a unmattam iva mātaṅgaṃ siṃhena vinipātitam
c dadṛśur hṛṣṭaromāṇaḥ sarve te cāpi somakāḥ
a tato duryodhanaṃ hatvā bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavān
c patitaṃ kauravendraṃ tam upagamyedam abravīt
d vṛkodaro mahārāja vākśalyam atiduḥsaham
a gaur gaur iti purā manda draupadīm ekavāsasam
c yat sabhāyāṃ hasann asmāṃs tadā vadasi durmate
e tasyāvahāsasya phalam adya tvaṃ samavāpnuhi
a evam uktvā sa vāmena padā maulim upāspṛśat
c śiraś ca rājasiṃhasya pādena samaloḍayat
a tathaiva krodhasaṃrakto bhīmaḥ parabalārdanaḥ
c punar evābravīd vākyaṃ yat tac chṛṇu narādhipa
a ye 'smān puro 'panṛtyanta punar gaur iti gaur iti
c tān vayaṃ pratinṛtyāmaḥ punar gaur iti gaur iti
a nāsmākaṃ nikṛtir vahnir nākṣadyūtaṃ na vañcanā
b na śāṭhyaṃ naiva no māyā yathāsya sudurātmanaḥ
c svabāhubalam āśritya prabādhāmo vayaṃ ripūn
a so 'vāpya vairasya parasya pāraṃ
vṛkodaraḥ prāha śanaiḥ prahasya
c yudhiṣṭhiraṃ keśavasṛñjayāṃś ca
dhanaṃjayaṃ mādravatīsutau ca
a rajasvalāṃ draupadīm ānayan ye
ye cāpy akurvanta sadasy avastrām
c tān paśyadhvaṃ pāṇḍavair dhārtarāṣṭrān
raṇe hatāṃs tapasā yājñasenyāḥ
a ye naḥ purā ṣaṇḍhatilān avocan
krūrā rājño dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putrāḥ
c te no hatāḥ sagaṇāḥ sānubandhāḥ
kāmaṃ svargaṃ narakaṃ vā vrajāmaḥ
a punaś ca rājñaḥ patitasya bhūmau
sa tāṃ gadāṃ skandhagatāṃ nirīkṣya
c vāmena pādena śiraḥ pramṛdya
duryodhanaṃ naikṛtikety avocat
a hṛṣṭena rājan kurupārthivasya
kṣudrātmanā bhīmasenena pādam
c dṛṣṭvā kṛtaṃ mūrdhani nābhyanandan
dharmātmānaḥ somakānāṃ prabarhāḥ
a tava putraṃ tathā hatvā katthamānaṃ vṛkodaram
c nṛtyamānaṃ ca bahuśo dharmarājo 'bravīd idam
d gato 'si vairasyānṛṇyaṃ pratijñā pūritā tvayā
d śubhenaivāśubhenātha karmaṇā viramādhunā
a mā śiro 'sya padā mardīr mā dharmas te 'tyagān mahān
a   ekādaśacamūpateḥ
a pañcānām api yo bhartā na sā prakṛtir mānuṣī
c rājā jñātir hataś cāyaṃ naitan nyāyyaṃ tavānagha
d āgacchet tvāṃ mahābāho vācyaṃ cādharmasaṃhitam
d mā śiro 'sya padā mṛdnā ekādaśacamūpateḥ
d na naśyetāṃ ca dharmasya tyāgāt kīrtir mahad yaśaḥ
d nihatasya padāghāto naitan nyāyyaṃ tavānagha
d ekādaśacamūnāthaṃ kurūṇām adhipaṃ tathā
d mā sprākṣīr bhīma pādena rājānaṃ jñātim eva ca
d hatabandhur hatāmātyo bhraṣṭasainyo hato mṛdhe
d sarvākāreṇa śocyo 'yaṃ nāvahāsyo 'yam īśvaraḥ
a vidhvasto 'yaṃ hatāmātyo hatabhrātā hataprajaḥ
c utsannapiṇḍo bhrātā ca naitan nyāyyaṃ kṛtaṃ tvayā
a dhārmiko bhīmaseno 'sāv ity āhus tvāṃ purā janāḥ
c sa kasmād bhīmasena tvaṃ rājānam adhitiṣṭhasi
a dṛṣṭvā duryodhanaṃ rājā kuntīputras tathāgatam
c netrābhyām aśrupūrṇābhyām idaṃ vacanam abravīt
d ity uktvā bhīmasenaṃ tu sāśrukaṇṭho yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d upasṛtyābravīd dīno duryodhanam ariṃdamam
d tāta manyur na te kāryo nātmā śocyas tvayā tathā
d nūnaṃ pūrvakṛtaṃ karma sughoram anubhūyate
a nūnam etad balavatā dhātrādiṣṭaṃ mahātmanā
c yad vayaṃ tvāṃ jighāṃsāmas tvaṃ cāsmān kurusattama
a ātmano hy aparādhena mahad vyasanam īdṛśam
c prāptavān asi yal lobhān madād bālyāc ca bhārata
a ghātayitvā vayasyāṃś ca bhrātṝn atha pitṝṃs tathā
c putrān pautrāṃs tathācāryāṃs tato 'si nidhanaṃ gataḥ
a tavāparādhād asmābhir bhrātaras te mahārathāḥ
b ātmā na śocanīyas te ślāghyo mṛtyus tavānagha
b vayam evādhunā śocyāḥ sarvāvasthāsu kaurava
b kṛpaṇaṃ vartayiṣyāmas tair hīnā bandhubhiḥ priyaiḥ
b bhrātṝṇāṃ caiva putrāṇāṃ tathā vai śokavihvalāḥ
b kathaṃ drakṣyāmi vidhavā vadhūḥ śokapariplutāḥ
b tvam ekaḥ susthito rājan svarge te nilayo dhruvaḥ
b vayaṃ narakasaṃjñā vai duḥkhaṃ bhokṣyāma dāruṇam
c nihatā jñātayaś cānye diṣṭaṃ manye duratyayam
a snuṣāś ca prasnuṣāś caiva dhṛtarāṣṭrasya vihvalāḥ
c garhayiṣyanti no nūnaṃ vidhavāḥ śokakarśitāḥ
a evam uktvā suduḥkhārto niśaśvāsa sa pārthivaḥ
c vilalāpa ciraṃ cāpi dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d vilalāpa mahīyān saḥ prakṛtyā karuṇāparaḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a adharmeṇa hataṃ dṛṣṭvā rājānaṃ mādhavottamaḥ
c kim abravīt tadā sūta baladevo mahābalaḥ
a gadāyuddhaviśeṣajño gadāyuddhaviśāradaḥ
c kṛtavān rauhiṇeyo yat tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya
 saṃjaya uvāca
a śirasy abhihataṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīmasenena te sutam
c rāmaḥ praharatāṃ śreṣṭhaś cukrodha balavad balī
a tato madhye narendrāṇām ūrdhvabāhur halāyudhaḥ
c kurvann ārtasvaraṃ ghoraṃ dhig dhig bhīmety uvāca ha
a aho dhig yad adho nābheḥ prahṛtaṃ śuddhavikrame
c naitad dṛṣṭaṃ gadāyuddhe kṛtavān yad vṛkodaraḥ
a adho nābhyā na hantavyam iti śāstrasya niścayaḥ
c ayaṃ tv aśāstravin mūḍhaḥ svacchandāt saṃpravartate
a tasya tat tad bruvāṇasya roṣaḥ samabhavan mahān
b tato rājānam ālokya roṣasaṃraktalocanaḥ
b baladevo mahārāja tato vacanam abravīt
b na caiṣa patitaḥ kṛṣṇa kevalaṃ matsamo 'samaḥ
b āśritasya tu daurbalyād āśrayaḥ paribhartsyate
c tato lāṅgalam udyamya bhīmam abhyadravad balī
a tasyordhvabāhoḥ sadṛśaṃ rūpam āsīn mahātmanaḥ
c bahudhātuvicitrasya śvetasyeva mahāgireḥ
d tam utpatantaṃ saṃkruddhaṃ vijñāya madhusūdanaḥ
d bhrātṛbhiḥ sahito bhīmaḥ sārjunair astrakovidaiḥ
d na vivyathe mahārāja dṛṣṭvā haladharaṃ balī
a tam utpatantaṃ jagrāha keśavo vinayānataḥ
c bāhubhyāṃ pīnavṛttābhyāṃ prayatnād balavad balī
a sitāsitau yaduvarau śuśubhāte 'dhikaṃ tataḥ
b saṃgatāv iva rājendra kailāsāñjanaparvatau
c nabhogatau yathā rājaṃś candrasūryau dinakṣaye
a uvāca cainaṃ saṃrabdhaṃ śamayann iva keśavaḥ
c ātmavṛddhir mitravṛddhir mitramitrodayas tathā
e viparītaṃ dviṣatsv etat ṣaḍvidhā vṛddhir ātmanaḥ
a ātmany api ca mitreṣu viparītaṃ yadā bhavet
c tadā vidyān manojyānim āśu śāntikaro bhavet
a asmākaṃ sahajaṃ mitraṃ pāṇḍavāḥ śuddhapauruṣāḥ
c svakāḥ pitṛṣvasuḥ putrās te parair nikṛtā bhṛśam
a pratijñāpāraṇaṃ dharmaḥ kṣatriyasyeti vettha ha
c suyodhanasya gadayā bhaṅktāsmy ūrū mahāhave
e iti pūrvaṃ pratijñātaṃ bhīmena hi sabhātale
a maitreyeṇābhiśaptaś ca pūrvam eva maharṣiṇā
c ūrū bhetsyati te bhīmo gadayeti paraṃtapa
e ato doṣaṃ na paśyāmi mā krudhas tvaṃ pralambahan
f ye jñātibāndhavebhyaś ca śreṣṭhā vai snehabāndhavāḥ
f pāṇḍavāś cābhavañ śreṣṭhāḥ snehāt saṃbandhatas tathā
a yaunair hārdaiś ca saṃbandhaiḥ saṃbaddhāḥ smeha pāṇḍavaiḥ
c teṣāṃ vṛddhyābhivṛddhir no mā krudhaḥ puruṣarṣabha
d vāsudevavacaḥ śrutvā sīrabhṛt prāha dharmavit
 rāma uvāca
a dharmaḥ sucaritaḥ sadbhiḥ saha dvābhyāṃ niyacchati
c arthaś cātyarthalubdhasya kāmaś cātiprasaṅginaḥ
a dharmārthau dharmakāmau ca kāmārthau cāpy apīḍayan
c dharmārthakāmān yo 'bhyeti so 'tyantaṃ sukham aśnute
a tad idaṃ vyākulaṃ sarvaṃ kṛtaṃ dharmasya pīḍanāt
c bhīmasenena govinda kāmaṃ tvaṃ tu yathāttha mām
 vāsudeva uvāca
a aroṣaṇo hi dharmātmā satataṃ dharmavatsalaḥ
c bhavān prakhyāyate loke tasmāt saṃśāmya mā krudhaḥ
a prāptaṃ kaliyugaṃ viddhi pratijñāṃ pāṇḍavasya ca
c ānṛṇyaṃ yātu vairasya pratijñāyāś ca pāṇḍavaḥ
d ataḥ puruṣaśārdūlo hatvā naikṛtikaṃ raṇe
d nikṛtyā nikṛtiprajñaṃ yo hanyād vairiṇaṃ raṇe
d adharmo vidyate nātra yad bhīmo hatavān ripum
d yudhyantaṃ samare vīraṃ kuruvṛṣṇiyaśaskaram
d anena karṇaḥ saṃdiṣṭaḥ pratīto dhanur acchinat
d tataḥ saṃchinnadhanvānaṃ virathaṃ pauruṣe sthitam
d vyāyudhīkṛtya hatavān saubhadram apalāyinam
d janmaprabhṛti lubdhaś ca pāpaś caiṣa durātmavān
d nihato bhīmasenena durbuddhiḥ kulapāṃsanaḥ
d pratijñāṃ bhīmasenasya trayodaśasamārjitām
d kimarthaṃ nābhijānāti yudhyamāno hi viśrutām
d ūrdhvam utkramya vegena jighāṃsantaṃ vṛkodaraḥ
d babhañja gadayā corū na ca sthāne ca maṇḍale
d gacchatv adya mahāprājño bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a dharmacchalam api śrutvā keśavāt sa viśāṃ pate
c naiva prītamanā rāmo vacanaṃ prāha saṃsadi
a hatvādharmeṇa rājānaṃ dharmātmānaṃ suyodhanam
c jihmayodhīti loke 'smin khyātiṃ yāsyati pāṇḍavaḥ
a duryodhano 'pi dharmātmā gatiṃ yāsyati śāśvatīm
c ṛjuyodhī hato rājā dhārtarāṣṭro narādhipaḥ
a yuddhadīkṣāṃ praviśyājau raṇayajñaṃ vitatya ca
c hutvātmānam amitrāgnau prāpa cāvabhṛthaṃ yaśaḥ
d svargaṃ gantā mahārājaḥ sasuhṛjjñātibāndhavaḥ
a ity uktvā ratham āsthāya rauhiṇeyaḥ pratāpavān
c śvetābhraśikharākāraḥ prayayau dvārakāṃ prati
a pāñcālāś ca savārṣṇeyāḥ pāṇḍavāś ca viśāṃ pate
c rāme dvāravatīṃ yāte nātipramanaso 'bhavan
a tato yudhiṣṭhiraṃ dīnaṃ cintāparam adhomukham
c śokopahatasaṃkalpaṃ vāsudevo 'bravīd idam
a dharmarāja kimarthaṃ tvam adharmam anumanyase
c hatabandhor yad etasya patitasya vicetasaḥ
a duryodhanasya bhīmena mṛdyamānaṃ śiraḥ padā
c upaprekṣasi kasmāt tvaṃ dharmajñaḥ san narādhipa
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a na mamaitat priyaṃ kṛṣṇa yad rājānaṃ vṛkodaraḥ
c padā mūrdhny aspṛśat krodhān na ca hṛṣye kulakṣaye
a nikṛtyā nikṛtā nityaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasutair vayam
c bahūni paruṣāṇy uktvā vanaṃ prasthāpitāḥ sma ha
a bhīmasenasya tad duḥkham atīva hṛdi vartate
c iti saṃcintya vārṣṇeya mayaitat samupekṣitam
a tasmād dhatvākṛtaprajñaṃ lubdhaṃ kāmavaśānugam
c labhatāṃ pāṇḍavaḥ kāmaṃ dharme 'dharme 'pi vā kṛte
 saṃjaya uvāca
a ity ukte dharmarājena vāsudevo 'bravīd idam
b ity uktavati kaunteye dharmarāje yudhiṣṭhire
b vāsudevo mahābāhur yudhiṣṭhiram abhāṣata
c kāmam astv evam iti vai kṛcchrād yadukulodvahaḥ
a ity ukto vāsudevena bhīmapriyahitaiṣiṇā
c anvamodata tat sarvaṃ yad bhīmena kṛtaṃ yudhi
d arjuno 'pi mahābāhur aprītenāntarātmanā
d novāca kiṃ cid vacanaṃ bhrātaraṃ sādhv asādhu vā
a bhīmaseno 'pi hatvājau tava putram amarṣaṇaḥ
c abhivādyāgrataḥ sthitvā saṃprahṛṣṭaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ
a provāca sumahātejā dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
c harṣād utphullanayano jitakāśī viśāṃ pate
a tavādya pṛthivī rājan kṣemā nihatakaṇṭakā
c tāṃ praśādhi mahārāja svadharmam anupālayan
a yas tu kartāsya vairasya nikṛtyā nikṛtipriyaḥ
c so 'yaṃ vinihataḥ śete pṛthivyāṃ pṛthivīpate
a duḥśāsanaprabhṛtayaḥ sarve te cogravādinaḥ
c rādheyaḥ śakuniś cāpi nihatās tava śatravaḥ
a seyaṃ ratnasamākīrṇā mahī savanaparvatā
c upāvṛttā mahārāja tvām adya nihatadviṣam
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a gataṃ vairasya nidhanaṃ hato rājā suyodhanaḥ
c kṛṣṇasya matam āsthāya vijiteyaṃ vasuṃdharā
a diṣṭyā gatas tvam ānṛṇyaṃ mātuḥ kopasya cobhayoḥ
c diṣṭyā jayasi durdharṣa diṣṭyā śatrur nipātitaḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a hataṃ duryodhanaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīmasenena saṃyuge
c pāṇḍavāḥ sṛñjayāś caiva kim akurvata saṃjaya
d aśvatthāmā kṛpaś caiva kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥ
d hataṃ duryodhanaṃ dṛṣṭvā pratyapadyanta saṃjaya
 saṃjaya uvāca
a hataṃ duryodhanaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīmasenena saṃyuge
c siṃheneva mahārāja mattaṃ vanagajaṃ vane
a prahṛṣṭamanasas tatra kṛṣṇena saha pāṇḍavāḥ
c pāñcālāḥ sṛñjayāś caiva nihate kurunandane
a āvidhyann uttarīyāṇi siṃhanādāṃś ca nedire
c naitān harṣasamāviṣṭān iyaṃ sehe vasuṃdharā
a dhanūṃṣy anye vyākṣipanta jyāś cāpy anye tathākṣipan
c dadhmur anye mahāśaṅkhān anye jaghnuś ca dundubhīḥ
a cikrīḍuś ca tathaivānye jahasuś ca tavāhitāḥ
c abruvaṃś cāsakṛd vīrā bhīmasenam idaṃ vacaḥ
a duṣkaraṃ bhavatā karma raṇe 'dya sumahat kṛtam
c kauravendraṃ raṇe hatvā gadayātikṛtaśramam
a indreṇeva hi vṛtrasya vadhaṃ paramasaṃyuge
c tvayā kṛtam amanyanta śatror vadham imaṃ janāḥ
a carantaṃ vividhān mārgān maṇḍalāni ca sarvaśaḥ
c duryodhanam imaṃ śūraṃ ko 'nyo hanyād vṛkodarāt
a vairasya ca gataḥ pāraṃ tvam ihānyaiḥ sudurgamam
c aśakyam etad anyena saṃpādayitum īdṛśam
a kuñjareṇeva mattena vīra saṃgrāmamūrdhani
c duryodhanaśiro diṣṭyā pādena mṛditaṃ tvayā
a siṃhena mahiṣasyeva kṛtvā saṃgaram adbhutam
c duḥśāsanasya rudhiraṃ diṣṭyā pītaṃ tvayānagha
a ye viprakurvan rājānaṃ dharmātmānaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
c mūrdhni teṣāṃ kṛtaḥ pādo diṣṭyā te svena karmaṇā
a amitrāṇām adhiṣṭhānād vadhād duryodhanasya ca
c bhīma diṣṭyā pṛthivyāṃ te prathitaṃ sumahad yaśaḥ
a evaṃ nūnaṃ hate vṛtre śakraṃ nandanti bandinaḥ
c tathā tvāṃ nihatāmitraṃ vayaṃ nandāma bhārata
a duryodhanavadhe yāni romāṇi hṛṣitāni naḥ
c adyāpi na vihṛṣyanti tāni tad viddhi bhārata
e ity abruvan bhīmasenaṃ vātikās tatra saṃgatāḥ
a tān hṛṣṭān puruṣavyāghrān pāñcālān pāṇḍavaiḥ saha
c bruvataḥ sadṛśaṃ tatra provāca madhusūdanaḥ
a na nyāyyaṃ nihataḥ śatrur bhūyo hantuṃ janādhipāḥ
c asakṛd vāgbhir ugrābhir nihato hy eṣa mandadhīḥ
a tadaivaiṣa hataḥ pāpo yadaiva nirapatrapaḥ
c lubdhaḥ pāpasahāyaś ca suhṛdāṃ śāsanātigaḥ
a bahuśo viduradroṇakṛpagāṅgeyasṛñjayaiḥ
b ity uktaḥ pāṇḍavebhyaś ca hy ardharājyaṃ dadasva vai
c pāṇḍubhyaḥ procyamāno 'pi pitryam aṃśaṃ na dattavān
d nānena kāryaṃ dṛṣṭena śrutenaiva kathāsv api
d īdṛśā bhinnamaryādā gatiṃ yāntīha tādṛśīm
d śrutvaivaṃ vacanaṃ tasya sāsūyavacanaṃ tadā
d jvalann iva ca roṣeṇa sphurann iva ca bhūpatiḥ
a naiṣa yogyo 'dya mitraṃ vā śatrur vā puruṣādhamaḥ
c kim anenātinunnena vāgbhiḥ kāṣṭhasadharmaṇā
a ratheṣv ārohata kṣipraṃ gacchāmo vasudhādhipāḥ
c diṣṭyā hato 'yaṃ pāpātmā sāmātyajñātibāndhavaḥ
a iti śrutvā tv adhikṣepaṃ kṛṣṇād duryodhano nṛpaḥ
c amarṣavaśam āpanna udatiṣṭhad viśāṃ pate
a sphigdeśenopaviṣṭaḥ sa dorbhyāṃ viṣṭabhya medinīm
c dṛṣṭiṃ bhrūsaṃkaṭāṃ kṛtvā vāsudeve nyapātayat
a ardhonnataśarīrasya rūpam āsīn nṛpasya tat
c kruddhasyāśīviṣasyeva cchinnapucchasya bhārata
a prāṇāntakaraṇīṃ ghorāṃ vedanām avicintayan
c duryodhano vāsudevaṃ vāgbhir ugrābhir ārdayat
a kaṃsadāsasya dāyāda na te lajjāsty anena vai
c adharmeṇa gadāyuddhe yad ahaṃ vinipātitaḥ
a ūrū bhindhīti bhīmasya smṛtiṃ mithyā prayacchatā
c kiṃ na vijñātam etan me yad arjunam avocathāḥ
a ghātayitvā mahīpālān ṛjuyuddhān sahasraśaḥ
c jihmair upāyair bahubhir na te lajjā na te ghṛṇā
a ahany ahani śūrāṇāṃ kurvāṇaḥ kadanaṃ mahat
c śikhaṇḍinaṃ puraskṛtya ghātitas te pitāmahaḥ
a aśvatthāmnaḥ sanāmānaṃ hatvā nāgaṃ sudurmate
c ācāryo nyāsitaḥ śastraṃ kiṃ tan na viditaṃ mama
a sa cānena nṛśaṃsena dhṛṣṭadyumnena vīryavān
c pātyamānas tvayā dṛṣṭo na cainaṃ tvam avārayaḥ
a vadhārthaṃ pāṇḍuputrasya yācitāṃ śaktim eva ca
c ghaṭotkace vyaṃsayathāḥ kas tvattaḥ pāpakṛttamaḥ
a chinnabāhuḥ prāyagatas tathā bhūriśravā balī
c tvayā nisṛṣṭena hataḥ śaineyena durātmanā
a kurvāṇaś cottamaṃ karma karṇaḥ pārthajigīṣayā
c vyaṃsanenāśvasenasya pannagendrasutasya vai
a punaś ca patite cakre vyasanārtaḥ parājitaḥ
c pātitaḥ samare karṇaś cakravyagro 'graṇīr nṛṇām
a yadi māṃ cāpi karṇaṃ ca bhīṣmadroṇau ca saṃyuge
c ṛjunā pratiyudhyethā na te syād vijayo dhruvam
a tvayā punar anāryeṇa jihmamārgeṇa pārthivāḥ
c svadharmam anutiṣṭhanto vayaṃ cānye ca ghātitāḥ
d tvayā māyāvinā kṛṣṇa māyām arkapramoṣiṇīm
d kṛtvā hataḥ sindhupatiḥ kiṃ tan na viditaṃ mama
 vāsudeva uvāca
a hatas tvam asi gāndhāre sabhrātṛsutabāndhavaḥ
c sagaṇaḥ sasuhṛc caiva pāpamārgam anuṣṭhitaḥ
a tavaiva duṣkṛtair vīrau bhīṣmadroṇau nipātitau
c karṇaś ca nihataḥ saṃkhye tava śīlānuvartakaḥ
a yācyamāno mayā mūḍha pitryam aṃśaṃ na ditsasi
c pāṇḍavebhyaḥ svarājyārdhaṃ lobhāc chakuniniścayāt
a viṣaṃ te bhīmasenāya dattaṃ sarve ca pāṇḍavāḥ
c pradīpitā jatugṛhe mātrā saha sudurmate
d pāṇḍavāḥ duḥkhitāś cāsan purā vai vāraṇāvate
a sabhāyāṃ yājñasenī ca kṛṣṭā dyūte rajasvalā
c tadaiva tāvad duṣṭātman vadhyas tvaṃ nirapatrapaḥ
a anakṣajñaṃ ca dharmajñaṃ saubalenākṣavedinā
c nikṛtyā yat parājaiṣīs tasmād asi hato raṇe
a jayadrathena pāpena yat kṛṣṇā kleśitā vane
c yāteṣu mṛgayāṃ teṣu tṛṇabindor athāśrame
d tasmāt so 'pi hataḥ krūras tava doṣeṇa cātmanaḥ
a abhimanyuś ca yad bāla eko bahubhir āhave
c tvaddoṣair nihataḥ pāpa tasmād asi hato raṇe
d yāny akāryāṇi cāsmākaṃ kṛtānīti prabhāṣase
d vaiguṇyena tavātyarthaṃ sarvaṃ hi tad anuṣṭhitam
d bṛhaspater uśanaso nopadeśaḥ śrutas tvayā
d vṛddhā nopāsitāś caiva hitaṃ vākyaṃ na te śrutam
d lobhenātibalena tvaṃ tṛṣṇayā ca vaśīkṛtaḥ
d kṛtavān asyakāryāṇi vipākas teṣu bhujyatām
d kurvāṇaṃ karma samare pāṇḍavān arthakāṅkṣiṇam
d yac chikhaṇḍy avadhīd bhīṣmaṃ mitrārthe na vyatikramaḥ
d svadharmaṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtvā ācāryas tvatpriyepsayā
d pārṣatena hataḥ saṃkhye vartamāno 'satāṃ pathi
d pratijñām ātmanaḥ satyāṃ cikīrṣan samare ripum
d hatavān sātvato vidvān saumadattiṃ mahāratham
d arjunaḥ samare rājan yudhyamānaḥ kadā cana
d ninditaṃ puruṣavyāghraḥ karoti na kathaṃ cana
d labdhvāpi bahuśaś chidraṃ vīravṛttam anusmaran
d na jaghāna raṇe karṇaṃ maivaṃ vocaḥ sudurmate
d devānāṃ matam ājñāya teṣāṃ priyahitepsayā
d nārjunasya mate nāgaṃ mayā vyaṃsitam asrajam
d tvaṃ ca bhīṣmaś ca karṇaś ca droṇo drauṇis tathā kṛpaḥ
d virāṭanagare tasya ānṛśaṃsyāc ca jīvitāḥ
d smara pārthasya vikrāntaṃ gandharveṣu kṛtaṃ tadā
d adharmaṃ nātra gāndhāre pāṇḍavair yat kṛtaṃ tvayi
d svabāhubalam āsthāya svadharmeṇa paraṃtapāḥ
d jitavanto raṇe vīrāḥ pāpo 'si nidhanaṃ gataḥ
 duryodhana uvāca
a adhītaṃ vidhivad dattaṃ bhūḥ praśāstā sasāgarā
c mūrdhni sthitam amitrāṇāṃ ko nu svantataro mayā
a yad iṣṭaṃ kṣatrabandhūnāṃ svadharmam anupaśyatām
c tad idaṃ nidhanaṃ prāptaṃ ko nu svantataro mayā
a devārhā mānuṣā bhogāḥ prāptā asulabhā nṛpaiḥ
c aiśvaryaṃ cottamaṃ prāptaṃ ko nu svantataro mayā
a sasuhṛt sānubandhaś ca svargaṃ gantāham acyuta
c yūyaṃ vihatasaṃkalpāḥ śocanto vartayiṣyatha
d na me viṣādo bhīmena pādena śira āhatam
d kāko vā kaṅkagṛdhro vā nidhāsyati padaṃ kṣaṇāt
 saṃjaya uvāca
a asya vākyasya nidhane kururājasya bhārata
c apatat sumahad varṣaṃ puṣpāṇāṃ puṇyagandhinām
a avādayanta gandharvā jaguś cāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ
a   vāditraṃ sumanoharam
a jaguś cāpsaraso rājño yaśaḥ saṃbaddham eva ca
c siddhāś ca mumucur vācaḥ sādhu sādhv iti bhārata
a vavau ca surabhir vāyuḥ puṇyagandho mṛduḥ sukhaḥ
c vyarājatāmalaṃ caiva nabho vaiḍūryasaṃnibham
a atyadbhutāni te dṛṣṭvā vāsudevapurogamāḥ
b āścaryaṃ paramaṃ jagmuḥ pāñcālāḥ somakaiḥ saha
c duryodhanasya pūjāṃ ca dṛṣṭvā vrīḍām upāgaman
a hatāṃś cādharmataḥ śrutvā śokārtāḥ śuśucur hi te
b hatāṃś ca kauravāñ śrutvādharmataś ca mahīpatīn
b śokārtāḥ śuśucuḥ sarve pāṇḍavā bharatarṣabha
c bhīṣmaṃ droṇaṃ tathā karṇaṃ bhūriśravasam eva ca
a tāṃs tu cintāparān dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavān dīnacetasaḥ
c provācedaṃ vacaḥ kṛṣṇo meghadundubhinisvanaḥ
a naiṣa śakyo 'tiśīghrāstras te ca sarve mahārathāḥ
c ṛjuyuddhena vikrāntā hantuṃ yuṣmābhir āhave
d naiṣa śakyaḥ kadā cit tu hantuṃ dharmeṇa pārthivaḥ
d te vā bhīṣmamukhāḥ sarve maheṣvāsā mahārathāḥ
d mayānekair upāyais tu māyāyogena cāsakṛt
d hatās te sarva evājau bhavatāṃ hitam icchatā
d yadi naivaṃvidhaṃ jātu kuryāṃ jihmam ahaṃ raṇe
d kuto vo vijayo bhūyaḥ kuto rājyaṃ kuto dhanam
a upāyā vihitā hy ete mayā tasmān narādhipāḥ
c anyathā pāṇḍaveyānāṃ nābhaviṣyaj jayaḥ kva cit
a te hi sarve mahātmānaś catvāro 'tirathā bhuvi
c na śakyā dharmato hantuṃ lokapālair api svayam
a tathaivāyaṃ gadāpāṇir dhārtarāṣṭro gataklamaḥ
c na śakyo dharmato hantuṃ kālenāpīha daṇḍinā
a na ca vo hṛdi kartavyaṃ yad ayaṃ ghātito nṛpaḥ
c mithyāvadhyās tathopāyair bahavaḥ śatravo 'dhikāḥ
a pūrvair anugato mārgo devair asuraghātibhiḥ
c sadbhiś cānugataḥ panthāḥ sa sarvair anugamyate
d evaṃ vidhātrā vihitaṃ vadham eṣāṃ mahātmanām
d daivaṃ puruṣakāreṇa na śakyam ativartitum
d bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyac ca nimeṣād yo haniṣyati
d kṛtāntam anyathākartuṃ necchet so 'yaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ
a kṛtakṛtyāḥ sma sāyāhne nivāsaṃ rocayāmahe
c sāśvanāgarathāḥ sarve viśramāmo narādhipāḥ
a vāsudevavacaḥ śrutvā tadānīṃ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha
c pāñcālā bhṛśasaṃhṛṣṭā vineduḥ siṃhasaṃghavat
a tataḥ prādhmāpayañ śaṅkhān pāñcajanyaṃ ca mādhavaḥ
b devadattaṃ prahṛṣṭātmā śaṅkhapravaram arjunaḥ
b anantavijayaṃ rājā kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
b pauṇḍraṃ dadhmau mahāśaṅkhaṃ bhīmakarmā vṛkodaraḥ
b nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca sughoṣamaṇipuṣpakau
b dhṛṣṭadyumnas tathā jaitraṃ sātyakir nandivardhanam
b teṣāṃ nādena mahatā śaṅkhānāṃ bharatarṣabha
b āpupūre nabhaḥ sarvaṃ pṛthivī ca cacāla ha
b tataḥ śaṅkhāś ca bheryaś ca paṇavānakagomukhāḥ
b pāṇḍusainyeṣv avādyanta sa śabdas tumulo 'bhavat
b astuvan pāṇḍavān anye gīrbhiś ca stutimaṅgalaiḥ
b gīrbhir maṅgalayuktābhir vandinaḥ stutipāṭhakāḥ
c hṛṣṭā duryodhanaṃ dṛṣṭvā nihataṃ puruṣarṣabhāḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tatas te prayayuḥ sarve nivāsāya mahīkṣitaḥ
c śaṅkhān pradhmāpayanto vai hṛṣṭāḥ parighabāhavaḥ
a pāṇḍavān gacchataś cāpi śibiraṃ no viśāṃ pate
c maheṣvāso 'nvagāt paścād yuyutsuḥ sātyakis tathā
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca draupadeyāś ca sarvaśaḥ
c sarve cānye maheṣvāsā yayuḥ svaśibirāṇy uta
a tatas te prāviśan pārthā hatatviṭkaṃ hateśvaram
c duryodhanasya śibiraṃ raṅgavad visṛte jane
a gatotsavaṃ puram iva hṛtanāgam iva hradam
c strīvarṣavarabhūyiṣṭhaṃ vṛddhāmātyair adhiṣṭhitam
a tatraitān paryupātiṣṭhan duryodhanapuraḥsarāḥ
c kṛtāñjalipuṭā rājan kāṣāyamalināmbarāḥ
a śibiraṃ samanuprāpya kururājasya pāṇḍavāḥ
c avaterur mahārāja rathebhyo rathasattamāḥ
a tato gāṇḍīvadhanvānam abhyabhāṣata keśavaḥ
c sthitaḥ priyahite nityam atīva bharatarṣabha
a avaropaya gāṇḍīvam akṣayyau ca maheṣudhī
c athāham avarokṣyāmi paścād bharatasattama
a svayaṃ caivāvaroha tvam etac chreyas tavānagha
c tac cākarot tathā vīraḥ pāṇḍuputro dhanaṃjayaḥ
a atha paścāt tataḥ kṛṣṇo raśmīn utsṛjya vājinām
c avārohata medhāvī rathād gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ
a athāvatīrṇe bhūtānām īśvare sumahātmani
c kapir antardadhe divyo dhvajo gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ
a sa dagdho droṇakarṇābhyāṃ divyair astrair mahārathaḥ
c atha dīpto 'gninā hy āśu prajajvāla mahīpate
a sopāsaṅgaḥ saraśmiś ca sāśvaḥ sayugabandhuraḥ
c bhasmībhūto 'patad bhūmau ratho gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ
a taṃ tathā bhasmabhūtaṃ tu dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍusutāḥ prabho
c abhavan vismitā rājann arjunaś cedam abravīt
a kṛtāñjaliḥ sapraṇayaṃ praṇipatyābhivādya ca
c govinda kasmād bhagavan ratho dagdho 'yam agninā
a kim etan mahad āścaryam abhavad yadunandana
c tan me brūhi mahābāho śrotavyaṃ yadi manyase
d arjunasya vacaḥ śrutvā punaḥ prāha janārdanaḥ
 vāsudeva uvāca
a astrair bahuvidhair dagdhaḥ pūrvam evāyam arjuna
c madadhiṣṭhitatvāt samare na viśīrṇaḥ paraṃtapa
a idānīṃ tu viśīrṇo 'yaṃ dagdho brahmāstratejasā
c mayā vimuktaḥ kaunteya tvayy adya kṛtakarmaṇi
 saṃjaya uvāca
a īṣad utsmayamānaś ca bhagavān keśavo 'rihā
c pariṣvajya ca rājānaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram abhāṣata
a diṣṭyā jayasi kaunteya diṣṭyā te śatravo jitāḥ
c diṣṭyā gāṇḍīvadhanvā ca bhīmasenaś ca pāṇḍavaḥ
a tvaṃ cāpi kuśalī rājan mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavau
c muktā vīrakṣayād asmāt saṃgrāmān nihatadviṣaḥ
e kṣipram uttarakālāni kuru kāryāṇi bhārata
a upayātam upaplavyaṃ saha gāṇḍīvadhanvanā
c ānīya madhuparkaṃ māṃ yat purā tvam avocathāḥ
a eṣa bhrātā sakhā caiva tava kṛṣṇa dhanaṃjayaḥ
c rakṣitavyo mahābāho sarvāsv āpatsv iti prabho
e tava caivaṃ bruvāṇasya tathety evāham abruvam
a sa savyasācī guptas te vijayī ca nareśvara
c bhrātṛbhiḥ saha rājendra śūraḥ satyaparākramaḥ
e mukto vīrakṣayād asmāt saṃgrāmād romaharṣaṇāt
a evam uktas tu kṛṣṇena dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c hṛṣṭaromā mahārāja pratyuvāca janārdanam
a pramuktaṃ droṇakarṇābhyāṃ brahmāstram arimardana
b bhīṣmadroṇakṛpadrauṇikarṇaśalyamukhān rathān
c kas tvad anyaḥ sahet sākṣād api vajrī puraṃdaraḥ
a bhavatas tu prasādena saṃgrāme bahavo jitāḥ
c mahāraṇagataḥ pārtho yac ca nāsīt parāṅmukhaḥ
a tathaiva ca mahābāho paryāyair bahubhir mayā
a   prasādād bahavo hatāḥ
a bhīmasenena ca mayā yamābhyāṃ yudhi mānada
a karmaṇā manasā vācā tvam asmākaṃ gatiḥ parā
c karmaṇām anusaṃtānaṃ tejasaś ca gatiḥ śubhā
a upaplavye maharṣir me kṛṣṇadvaipāyano 'bravīt
c yato dharmas tataḥ kṛṣṇo yataḥ kṛṣṇas tato jayaḥ
d evam uktas tataḥ kṛṣṇaḥ pratyuvāca yudhiṣṭhiram
d akṣauhiṇyo daśāṣṭau ca tava teṣāṃ ca bhārata
d na tulyaś cārjunasyeha balena kurunandana
d sa eva sarvāṇy astrāṇi divyāni prāpya śaṃkarāt
d matsamo madviśiṣṭo vā raṇe tvam iti pāṇḍava
d anujñātaḥ pāṇḍusutaḥ punaḥ pratyāgaman mahīm
d bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyac ca anujānāsi cet prabho
d nimeṣārdhān naravyāghro nayed iti matir mama
d droṇaṃ bhīṣmaṃ kṛpaṃ karṇaṃ droṇaputraṃ jayadratham
d nihantuṃ śaknuyāt kruddho nimeṣārdhād dhanaṃjayaḥ
d sadevāsuragandharvān sayakṣoragakiṃnarān
d trīn vā lokān vijetuṃ hi śaktaḥ kim iha mānuṣān
d vidhinā vihitaś cāsau mayā saṃcodito 'pi san
d na cakāra matiṃ hantuṃ kṛtānto balavattaraḥ
d atra gītā mayā suṣṭhu giraḥ satyā mahīpate
d darśitaṃ mayi sarvaṃ ca tenāsau jitavān ripūn
d arjuno 'pi mahābāhur mayā tulyo mahīpate
d sa maheśvaralabdhāstraḥ kiṃ na kuryād vibhuḥ prabho
a ity evam ukte te vīrāḥ śibiraṃ tava bhārata
c praviśya pratyapadyanta kośaratnarddhisaṃcayān
a rajataṃ jātarūpaṃ ca maṇīn atha ca mauktikān
c bhūṣaṇāny atha mukhyāni kambalāny ajināni ca
d gajān aśvān rathāṃś caiva mahānti śayanāni ca
e dāsīdāsam asaṃkhyeyaṃ rājyopakaraṇāni ca
a te prāpya dhanam akṣayyaṃ tvadīyaṃ bharatarṣabha
c udakrośan maheṣvāsā narendra vijitārayaḥ
a te tu vīrāḥ samāśvasya vāhanāny avamucya ca
c atiṣṭhanta muhuḥ sarve pāṇḍavāḥ sātyakis tathā
a athābravīn mahārāja vāsudevo mahāyaśāḥ
c asmābhir maṅgalārthāya vastavyaṃ śibirād bahiḥ
d jayantī yatra devī tu tatra vrajata mā ciram
d upayācitam etan me yuddhārambhopakalpitam
a tathety uktvā ca te sarve pāṇḍavāḥ sātyakis tathā
c vāsudevena sahitā maṅgalārthaṃ yayur bahiḥ
a te samāsādya saritaṃ puṇyāmoghavatīṃ nṛpa
c nyavasann atha tāṃ rātriṃ pāṇḍavā hataśatravaḥ
d yudhiṣṭhiras tato rājā prāptakālam acintayat
a tataḥ saṃpreṣayām āsur yādavaṃ nāgasāhvayam
c sa ca prāyāj javenāśu vāsudevaḥ pratāpavān
e dārukaṃ ratham āropya yena rājāmbikāsutaḥ
a tam ūcuḥ saṃprayāsyantaṃ sainyasugrīvavāhanam
c pratyāśvāsaya gāndhārīṃ hataputrāṃ yaśasvinīm
a sa prāyāt pāṇḍavair uktas tat puraṃ sātvatāṃ varaḥ
c āsasādayiṣuḥ kṣipraṃ gāndhārīṃ nihatātmajām
 janamejaya uvāca
a kimarthaṃ rājaśārdūlo dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c gāndhāryāḥ preṣayām āsa vāsudevaṃ paraṃtapam
a yadā pūrvaṃ gataḥ kṛṣṇaḥ śamārthaṃ kauravān prati
c na ca taṃ labdhavān kāmaṃ tato yuddham abhūd idam
a nihateṣu tu yodheṣu hate duryodhane tathā
c pṛthivyāṃ pāṇḍaveyasya niḥsapatne kṛte yudhi
a vidrute śibire śūnye prāpte yaśasi cottame
c kiṃ nu tat kāraṇaṃ brahman yena kṛṣṇo gataḥ punaḥ
a na caitat kāraṇaṃ brahmann alpaṃ vai pratibhāti me
c yatrāgamad ameyātmā svayam eva janārdanaḥ
a tattvato vai samācakṣva sarvam adhvaryusattama
c yac cātra kāraṇaṃ brahman kāryasyāsya viniścaye
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tvadyukto 'yam anupraśno yan māṃ pṛcchasi pārthiva
c tat te 'haṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi yathāvad bharatarṣabha
a hataṃ duryodhanaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīmasenena saṃyuge
c vyutkramya samayaṃ rājan dhārtarāṣṭraṃ mahābalam
a anyāyena hataṃ dṛṣṭvā gadāyuddhena bhārata
c yudhiṣṭhiraṃ mahārāja mahad bhayam athāviśat
a cintayāno mahābhāgāṃ gāndhārīṃ tapasānvitām
c ghoreṇa tapasā yuktāṃ trailokyam api sā dahet
a tasya cintayamānasya buddhiḥ samabhavat tadā
c gāndhāryāḥ krodhadīptāyāḥ pūrvaṃ praśamanaṃ bhavet
a sā hi putravadhaṃ śrutvā kṛtam asmābhir īdṛśam
c mānasenāgninā kruddhā bhasmasān naḥ kariṣyati
a kathaṃ duḥkham idaṃ tīvraṃ gāndhārī prasahiṣyati
c śrutvā vinihataṃ putraṃ chalenājihmayodhinam
a evaṃ vicintya bahudhā bhayaśokasamanvitaḥ
c vāsudevam idaṃ vākyaṃ dharmarājo 'bhyabhāṣata
a tava prasādād govinda rājyaṃ nihatakaṇṭakam
c aprāpyaṃ manasāpīha prāptam asmābhir acyuta
a pratyakṣaṃ me mahābāho saṃgrāme romaharṣaṇe
c vimardaḥ sumahān prāptas tvayā yādavanandana
a tvayā devāsure yuddhe vadhārtham amaradviṣām
c yathā sāhyaṃ purā dattaṃ hatāś ca vibudhadviṣaḥ
a sāhyaṃ tathā mahābāho dattam asmākam acyuta
c sārathyena ca vārṣṇeya bhavatā yad dhṛtā vayam
a yadi na tvaṃ bhaven nāthaḥ phalgunasya mahāraṇe
c kathaṃ śakyo raṇe jetuṃ bhaved eṣa balārṇavaḥ
d jetuṃ parān parivyūḍhān prāptāṃś caiva tvayācyuta
a gadāprahārā vipulāḥ parighaiś cāpi tāḍanam
c śaktibhir bhiṇḍipālaiś ca tomaraiḥ saparaśvadhaiḥ
a vācaś ca paruṣāḥ prāptās tvayā hy asmaddhitaiṣiṇā
b asmatkṛte tvayā kṛṣṇa vācaḥ suparuṣāḥ śrutāḥ
c tāś ca te saphalāḥ sarvā hate duryodhane 'cyuta
d śastrāṇāṃ ca nipātā vai vajrasparśopamā raṇe
d tat sarvaṃ na yathā naśyet punaḥ kṛṣṇa tathā kuru
d saṃdehadolāṃ prāptaṃ naś cetaḥ kṛṣṇa jaye sati
a gāndhāryā hi mahābāho krodhaṃ budhyasva mādhava
c sā hi nityaṃ mahābhāgā tapasogreṇa karśitā
a putrapautravadhaṃ śrutvā dhruvaṃ naḥ saṃpradhakṣyati
c tasyāḥ prasādanaṃ vīra prāptakālaṃ mataṃ mama
a kaś ca tāṃ krodhadīptākṣīṃ putravyasanakarśitām
c vīkṣituṃ puruṣaḥ śaktas tvām ṛte puruṣottama
a tatra me gamanaṃ prāptaṃ rocate tava mādhava
c gāndhāryāḥ krodhadīptāyāḥ praśamārtham ariṃdama
a tvaṃ hi kartā vikartā ca lokānāṃ prabhavāpyayaḥ
c hetukāraṇasaṃyuktair vākyaiḥ kālasamīritaiḥ
a kṣipram eva mahāprājña gāndhārīṃ śamayiṣyasi
c pitāmahaś ca bhagavān kṛṣṇas tatra bhaviṣyati
a sarvathā te mahābāho gāndhāryāḥ krodhanāśanam
c kartavyaṃ sātvataśreṣṭha pāṇḍavānāṃ hitaiṣiṇā
a dharmarājasya vacanaṃ śrutvā yadukulodvahaḥ
c āmantrya dārukaṃ prāha rathaḥ sajjo vidhīyatām
a keśavasya vacaḥ śrutvā tvaramāṇo 'tha dārukaḥ
c nyavedayad rathaṃ sajjaṃ keśavāya mahātmane
a taṃ rathaṃ yādavaśreṣṭhaḥ samāruhya paraṃtapaḥ
c jagāma hāstinapuraṃ tvaritaḥ keśavo vibhuḥ
a tataḥ prāyān mahārāja mādhavo bhagavān rathī
c nāgasāhvayam āsādya praviveśa ca vīryavān
a praviśya nagaraṃ vīro rathaghoṣeṇa nādayan
c vidito dhṛtarāṣṭrasya so 'vatīrya rathottamāt
a abhyagacchad adīnātmā dhṛtarāṣṭraniveśanam
c pūrvaṃ cābhigataṃ tatra so 'paśyad ṛṣisattamam
a pādau prapīḍya kṛṣṇasya rājñaś cāpi janārdanaḥ
c abhyavādayad avyagro gāndhārīṃ cāpi keśavaḥ
a tatas tu yādavaśreṣṭho dhṛtarāṣṭram adhokṣajaḥ
c pāṇim ālambya rājñaḥ sa sasvaraṃ praruroda ha
a sa muhūrtam ivotsṛjya bāṣpaṃ śokasamudbhavam
c prakṣālya vāriṇā netre ācamya ca yathāvidhi
e uvāca praśritaṃ vākyaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭram ariṃdamaḥ
a na te 'sty aviditaṃ kiṃ cid bhūtabhavyasya bhārata
c kālasya ca yathā vṛttaṃ tat te suviditaṃ prabho
a yad idaṃ pāṇḍavaiḥ sarvais tava cittānurodhibhiḥ
c kathaṃ kulakṣayo na syāt tathā kṣatrasya bhārata
a bhrātṛbhiḥ samayaṃ kṛtvā kṣāntavān dharmavatsalaḥ
c dyūtacchalajitaiḥ śaktair vanavāso 'bhyupāgataḥ
a ajñātavāsacaryā ca nānāveśasamāvṛtaiḥ
c anye ca bahavaḥ kleśās tv aśaktair iva nityadā
a mayā ca svayam āgamya yuddhakāla upasthite
c sarvalokasya sāṃnidhye grāmāṃs tvaṃ pañca yācitaḥ
a tvayā kālopasṛṣṭena lobhato nāpavarjitāḥ
c tavāparādhān nṛpate sarvaṃ kṣatraṃ kṣayaṃ gatam
a bhīṣmeṇa somadattena bāhlikena kṛpeṇa ca
c droṇena ca saputreṇa vidureṇa ca dhīmatā
e yācitas tvaṃ śamaṃ nityaṃ na ca tat kṛtavān asi
a kālopahatacitto hi sarvo muhyati bhārata
c yathā mūḍho bhavān pūrvam asminn arthe samudyate
a kim anyat kālayogād dhi diṣṭam eva parāyaṇam
c mā ca doṣaṃ mahārāja pāṇḍaveṣu niveśaya
a alpo 'py atikramo nāsti pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanām
c dharmato nyāyataś caiva snehataś ca paraṃtapa
a etat sarvaṃ tu vijñāya ātmadoṣakṛtaṃ phalam
c asūyāṃ pāṇḍuputreṣu na bhavān kartum arhati
a kulaṃ vaṃśaś ca piṇḍaś ca yac ca putrakṛtaṃ phalam
c gāndhāryās tava caivādya pāṇḍaveṣu pratiṣṭhitam
d tvaṃ caiva naraśārdūla gāndhārī ca yaśasvinī
d mā śuco naraśārdūla pāṇḍavān prati kilbiṣam
a etat sarvam anudhyātvā ātmanaś ca vyatikramam
c śivena pāṇḍavān dhyāhi namas te bharatarṣabha
a jānāsi ca mahābāho dharmarājasya yā tvayi
c bhaktir bharataśārdūla snehaś cāpi svabhāvataḥ
a etac ca kadanaṃ kṛtvā śatrūṇām apakāriṇām
c dahyate sma divārātraṃ na ca śarmādhigacchati
a tvāṃ caiva naraśārdūla gāndhārīṃ ca yaśasvinīm
c sa śocan bharataśreṣṭha na śāntim adhigacchati
a hriyā ca parayāviṣṭo bhavantaṃ nādhigacchati
c putraśokābhisaṃtaptaṃ buddhivyākulitendriyam
a evam uktvā mahārāja dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ yadūttamaḥ
c uvāca paramaṃ vākyaṃ gāndhārīṃ śokakarśitām
a saubaleyi nibodha tvaṃ yat tvāṃ vakṣyāmi suvrate
c tvatsamā nāsti loke 'sminn adya sīmantinī śubhe
a jānāmi ca yathā rājñi sabhāyāṃ mama saṃnidhau
c dharmārthasahitaṃ vākyam ubhayoḥ pakṣayor hitam
e uktavaty asi kalyāṇi na ca te tanayaiḥ śrutam
a duryodhanas tvayā cokto jayārthī paruṣaṃ vacaḥ
c śṛṇu mūḍha vaco mahyaṃ yato dharmas tato jayaḥ
a tad idaṃ samanuprāptaṃ tava vākyaṃ nṛpātmaje
c evaṃ viditvā kalyāṇi mā sma śoke manaḥ kṛthāḥ
e pāṇḍavānāṃ vināśāya mā te buddhiḥ kadā cana
a śaktā cāsi mahābhāge pṛthivīṃ sacarācarām
c cakṣuṣā krodhadīptena nirdagdhuṃ tapaso balāt
a vāsudevavacaḥ śrutvā gāndhārī vākyam abravīt
c evam etan mahābāho yathā vadasi keśava
a ādhibhir dahyamānāyā matiḥ saṃcalitā mama
c sā me vyavasthitā śrutvā tava vākyaṃ janārdana
a rājñas tv andhasya vṛddhasya hataputrasya keśava
c tvaṃ gatiḥ saha tair vīraiḥ pāṇḍavair dvipadāṃ vara
a etāvad uktvā vacanaṃ mukhaṃ pracchādya vāsasā
c putraśokābhisaṃtaptā gāndhārī praruroda ha
a tata enāṃ mahābāhuḥ keśavaḥ śokakarśitām
c hetukāraṇasaṃyuktair vākyair āśvāsayat prabhuḥ
a samāśvāsya ca gāndhārīṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ ca mādhavaḥ
c drauṇeḥ saṃkalpitaṃ bhāvam anvabudhyata keśavaḥ
a tatas tvarita utthāya pādau mūrdhnā praṇamya ca
c dvaipāyanasya rājendra tataḥ kauravam abravīt
a āpṛcche tvāṃ kuruśreṣṭha mā ca śoke manaḥ kṛthāḥ
c drauṇeḥ pāpo 'sty abhiprāyas tenāsmi sahasotthitaḥ
e pāṇḍavānāṃ vadhe rātrau buddhis tena pradarśitā
a etac chrutvā tu vacanaṃ gāndhāryā sahito 'bravīt
c dhṛtarāṣṭro mahābāhuḥ keśavaṃ keśisūdanam
a śīghraṃ gaccha mahābāho pāṇḍavān paripālaya
c bhūyas tvayā sameṣyāmi kṣipram eva janārdana
e prāyāt tatas tu tvarito dārukeṇa sahācyutaḥ
a vāsudeve gate rājan dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ janeśvaram
c āśvāsayad ameyātmā vyāso lokanamaskṛtaḥ
a vāsudevo 'pi dharmātmā kṛtakṛtyo jagāma ha
c śibiraṃ hāstinapurād didṛkṣuḥ pāṇḍavān nṛpa
a āgamya śibiraṃ rātrau so 'bhyagacchata pāṇḍavān
c tac ca tebhyaḥ samākhyāya sahitas taiḥ samāviśat
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a adhiṣṭhitaḥ padā mūrdhni bhagnasaktho mahīṃ gataḥ
c śauṭīramānī putro me kāny abhāṣata saṃjaya
a atyarthaṃ kopano rājā jātavairaś ca pāṇḍuṣu
c vyasanaṃ paramaṃ prāptaḥ kim āha paramāhave
 saṃjaya uvāca
a śṛṇu rājan pravakṣyāmi yathāvṛttaṃ narādhipa
c rājñā yad uktaṃ bhagnena tasmin vyasana āgate
a bhagnasaktho nṛpo rājan pāṃsunā so 'vaguṇṭhitaḥ
c yamayan mūrdhajāṃs tatra vīkṣya caiva diśo daśa
a keśān niyamya yatnena niḥśvasann urago yathā
c saṃrambhāśruparītābhyāṃ netrābhyām abhivīkṣya mām
a bāhū dharaṇyāṃ niṣpiṣya muhur matta iva dvipaḥ
c prakīrṇān mūrdhajān dhunvan dantair dantān upaspṛśan
e garhayan pāṇḍavaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ niḥśvasyedam athābravīt
a bhīṣme śāṃtanave nāthe karṇe cāstrabhṛtāṃ vare
c gautame śakunau cāpi droṇe cāstrabhṛtāṃ vare
a aśvatthāmni tathā śalye śūre ca kṛtavarmaṇi
b anyeṣv api ca śūreṣu nyastabhāro mahātmasu
c imām avasthāṃ prāpto 'smi kālo hi duratikramaḥ
a ekādaśacamūbhartā so 'ham etāṃ daśāṃ gataḥ
c kālaṃ prāpya mahābāho na kaś cid ativartate
a ākhyātavyaṃ madīyānāṃ ye 'smiñ jīvanti saṃgare
c yathāhaṃ bhīmasenena vyutkramya samayaṃ hataḥ
a bahūni sunṛśaṃsāni kṛtāni khalu pāṇḍavaiḥ
c bhūriśravasi karṇe ca bhīṣme droṇe ca śrīmati
a idaṃ cākīrtijaṃ karma nṛśaṃsaiḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ kṛtam
c yena te satsu nirvedaṃ gamiṣyantīti me matiḥ
a kā prītiḥ sattvayuktasya kṛtvopadhikṛtaṃ jayam
c ko vā samayabhettāraṃ budhaḥ saṃmantum arhati
a adharmeṇa jayaṃ labdhvā ko nu hṛṣyeta paṇḍitaḥ
c yathā saṃhṛṣyate pāpaḥ pāṇḍuputro vṛkodaraḥ
a kiṃ nu citram atas tv adya bhagnasakthasya yan mama
c kruddhena bhīmasenena pādena mṛditaṃ śiraḥ
a pratapantaṃ śriyā juṣṭaṃ vartamānaṃ ca bandhuṣu
c evaṃ kuryān naro yo hi sa vai saṃjaya pūjitaḥ
a abhijñau kṣatradharmasya mama mātā pitā ca me
c tau hi saṃjaya duḥkhārtau vijñāpyau vacanān mama
a iṣṭaṃ bhṛtyā bhṛtāḥ samyag bhūḥ praśāstā sasāgarā
c mūrdhni sthitam amitrāṇāṃ jīvatām eva saṃjaya
a dattā dāyā yathāśakti mitrāṇāṃ ca priyaṃ kṛtam
c amitrā bādhitāḥ sarve ko nu svantataro mayā
a yātāni pararāṣṭrāṇi nṛpā bhuktāś ca dāsavat
c priyebhyaḥ prakṛtaṃ sādhu ko nu svantataro mayā
a mānitā bāndhavāḥ sarve mānyaḥ saṃpūjito janaḥ
c tritayaṃ sevitaṃ sarvaṃ ko nu svantataro mayā
a ājñaptaṃ nṛpamukhyeṣu mānaḥ prāptaḥ sudurlabhaḥ
c ājāneyais tathā yātaṃ ko nu svantataro mayā
a adhītaṃ vidhivad dattaṃ prāptam āyur nirāmayam
c svadharmeṇa jitā lokāḥ ko nu svantataro mayā
a diṣṭyā nāhaṃ jitaḥ saṃkhye parān preṣyavad āśritaḥ
c diṣṭyā me vipulā lakṣmīr mṛte tv anyaṃ gatā vibho
a yad iṣṭaṃ kṣatrabandhūnāṃ svadharmam anutiṣṭhatām
c nidhanaṃ tan mayā prāptaṃ ko nu svantataro mayā
a diṣṭyā nāhaṃ parāvṛtto vairāt prākṛtavaj jitaḥ
c diṣṭyā na vimatiṃ kāṃ cid bhajitvā tu parājitaḥ
a suptaṃ vātha pramattaṃ vā yathā hanyād viṣeṇa vā
c evaṃ vyutkrāntadharmeṇa vyutkramya samayaṃ hataḥ
a aśvatthāmā mahābhāgaḥ kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥ
c kṛpaḥ śāradvataś caiva vaktavyā vacanān mama
a adharmeṇa pravṛttānāṃ pāṇḍavānām anekaśaḥ
c viśvāsaṃ samayaghnānāṃ na yūyaṃ gantum arhatha
a vātikāṃś cābravīd rājā putras te satyavikramaḥ
c adharmād bhīmasenena nihato 'haṃ yathā raṇe
a so 'haṃ droṇaṃ svargagataṃ śalyakarṇāv ubhau tathā
c vṛṣasenaṃ mahāvīryaṃ śakuniṃ cāpi saubalam
a jalasaṃdhaṃ mahāvīryaṃ bhagadattaṃ ca pārthivam
c saumadattiṃ maheṣvāsaṃ saindhavaṃ ca jayadratham
a duḥśāsanapurogāṃś ca bhrātṝn ātmasamāṃs tathā
c dauḥśāsaniṃ ca vikrāntaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ cātmajāv ubhau
a etāṃś cānyāṃś ca subahūn madīyāṃś ca sahasraśaḥ
c pṛṣṭhato 'nugamiṣyāmi sārthahīna ivādhvagaḥ
a kathaṃ bhrātṝn hatāñ śrutvā bhartāraṃ ca svasā mama
c rorūyamāṇā duḥkhārtā duḥśalā sā bhaviṣyati
a snuṣābhiḥ prasnuṣābhiś ca vṛddho rājā pitā mama
c gāndhārīsahitaḥ krośan kāṃ gatiṃ pratipatsyate
a nūnaṃ lakṣmaṇamātāpi hataputrā hateśvarā
c vināśaṃ yāsyati kṣipraṃ kalyāṇī pṛthulocanā
a yadi jānāti cārvākaḥ parivrāḍ vāgviśāradaḥ
c kariṣyati mahābhāgo dhruvaṃ so 'pacitiṃ mama
a samantapañcake puṇye triṣu lokeṣu viśrute
c ahaṃ nidhanam āsādya lokān prāpsyāmi śāśvatān
a tato janasahasrāṇi bāṣpapūrṇāni māriṣa
c pralāpaṃ nṛpateḥ śrutvā vidravanti diśo daśa
a sasāgaravanā ghorā pṛthivī sacarācarā
c cacālātha sanirhrādā diśaś caivāvilābhavan
a te droṇaputram āsādya yathāvṛttaṃ nyavedayan
c vyavahāraṃ gadāyuddhe pārthivasya ca ghātanam
a tad ākhyāya tataḥ sarve droṇaputrasya bhārata
b vādikā duḥkhasaṃtaptāḥ śokopahatacetasaḥ
c dhyātvā ca suciraṃ kālaṃ jagmur ārtā yathāgatam
 saṃjaya uvāca
a vātikānāṃ sakāśāt tu śrutvā duryodhanaṃ hatam
c hataśiṣṭās tato rājan kauravāṇāṃ mahārathāḥ
a vinirbhinnāḥ śitair bāṇair gadātomaraśaktibhiḥ
c aśvatthāmā kṛpaś caiva kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥ
e tvaritā javanair aśvair āyodhanam upāgaman
a tatrāpaśyan mahātmānaṃ dhārtarāṣṭraṃ nipātitam
c prabhagnaṃ vāyuvegena mahāśālaṃ yathā vane
a bhūmau viveṣṭamānaṃ taṃ rudhireṇa samukṣitam
c mahāgajam ivāraṇye vyādhena vinipātitam
a vivartamānaṃ bahuśo rudhiraughapariplutam
c yadṛcchayā nipatitaṃ cakram ādityagocaram
a mahāvātasamutthena saṃśuṣkam iva sāgaram
c pūrṇacandram iva vyomni tuṣārāvṛtamaṇḍalam
a reṇudhvastaṃ dīrghabhujaṃ mātaṅgasamavikramam
c vṛtaṃ bhūtagaṇair ghoraiḥ kravyādaiś ca samantataḥ
e yathā dhanaṃ lipsamānair bhṛtyair nṛpatisattamam
a bhrukuṭīkṛtavaktrāntaṃ krodhād udvṛttacakṣuṣam
c sāmarṣaṃ taṃ naravyāghraṃ vyāghraṃ nipatitaṃ yathā
a te tu dṛṣṭvā maheṣvāsā bhūtale patitaṃ nṛpam
c moham abhyāgaman sarve kṛpaprabhṛtayo rathāḥ
a avatīrya rathebhyas tu prādravan rājasaṃnidhau
c duryodhanaṃ ca saṃprekṣya sarve bhūmāv upāviśan
a tato drauṇir mahārāja bāṣpapūrṇekṣaṇaḥ śvasan
c uvāca bharataśreṣṭhaṃ sarvalokeśvareśvaram
a na nūnaṃ vidyate 'sahyaṃ mānuṣye kiṃ cid eva hi
c yatra tvaṃ puruṣavyāghra śeṣe pāṃsuṣu rūṣitaḥ
a bhūtvā hi nṛpatiḥ pūrvaṃ samājñāpya ca medinīm
c katham eko 'dya rājendra tiṣṭhase nirjane vane
a duḥśāsanaṃ na paśyāmi nāpi karṇaṃ mahāratham
c nāpi tān suhṛdaḥ sarvān kim idaṃ bharatarṣabha
a duḥkhaṃ nūnaṃ kṛtāntasya gatiṃ jñātuṃ kathaṃ cana
c lokānāṃ ca bhavān yatra śete pāṃsuṣu rūṣitaḥ
a eṣa mūrdhāvasiktānām agre gatvā paraṃtapaḥ
c satṛṇaṃ grasate pāṃsuṃ paśya kālasya paryayam
a kva te tad amalaṃ chatraṃ vyajanaṃ kva ca pārthiva
c sā ca te mahatī senā kva gatā pārthivottama
c   gajāśvarathasaṃkulā
c sāmantarājasaṃyuktā
d bhrātaras te mahārāja vīryaśakrasamā yudhi
d śatrūṇāṃ ca nihantāro mahābalaparākramāḥ
d kva gatāḥ pārthivendrādya saubhrātraṃ ca samāśritam
d tava putrā mahābhāga lakṣmaṇādyā mahārathāḥ
d pūrṇendusadṛśā vīrāḥ śāntisaundaryakāntibhiḥ
d kṛtavān nṛpaśārdūla jayantasamavikramam
a durvijñeyā gatir nūnaṃ kāryāṇāṃ kāraṇāntare
c yad vai lokagurur bhūtvā bhavān etāṃ daśāṃ gataḥ
a adhruvā sarvamartyeṣu dhruvaṃ śrīr upalakṣyate
b dhruveva bhāti sarvatra nityaṃ mohakarī nṛṇām
b vivekibhir nṛbhir nityaṃ cintyamānā viśeṣataḥ
b na tu viśvasen nityāṃ vai hy adhruvā vai svabhāvataḥ
c bhavato vyasanaṃ dṛṣṭvā śakravispardhino bhṛśam
d imaṃ lokam anityaṃ vā hy adyāhaṃ samacintaye
a tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā duḥkhitasya viśeṣataḥ
c uvāca rājan putras te prāptakālam idaṃ vacaḥ
a vimṛjya netre pāṇibhyāṃ śokajaṃ bāṣpam utsṛjan
c kṛpādīn sa tadā vīrān sarvān eva narādhipaḥ
a īdṛśo martyadharmo 'yaṃ dhātrā nirdiṣṭa ucyate
c vināśaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ kālaparyāyakāritaḥ
a so 'yaṃ māṃ samanuprāptaḥ pratyakṣaṃ bhavatāṃ hi yaḥ
c pṛthivīṃ pālayitvāham etāṃ niṣṭhām upāgataḥ
a diṣṭyā nāhaṃ parāvṛtto yuddhe kasyāṃ cid āpadi
b diṣṭyāhaṃ no nṛpatibhir nirjito na kadā cana
b diṣṭyā mayā nirjitās te rājāno bahuśo yudhi
c diṣṭyāhaṃ nihataḥ pāpaiś chalenaiva viśeṣataḥ
c   pāṇḍuputrair durātmabhiḥ
c adharmato gadāyuddhe
a utsāhaś ca kṛto nityaṃ mayā diṣṭyā yuyutsatā
b diṣṭyā hatā gajā yuddhe sagajārohakā bhṛśam
b diṣṭyāśvā deśajāḥ sarve kṛtino vegaśālinaḥ
b kuśalaiḥ sādibhiḥ sārdhaṃ nihatā raṇamūrdhani
b diṣṭyā raṇe vinihatā rathā hemapariṣkṛtāḥ
b rathibhir yuddhakuśalaiḥ sārdhaṃ vidalitaiḥ śaraiḥ
b diṣṭyā yodhā dhanuṣmantaḥ sarve yuddhaviśāradāḥ
b śaranirbhinnasarvāṅgāḥ samare patitābhavan
b diṣṭyā mamāyudhāny āśu nāśam āyānti vai kṣaṇāt
c diṣṭyā cāsmi hato yuddhe nihatajñātibāndhavaḥ
a diṣṭyā ca vo 'haṃ paśyāmi muktān asmāj janakṣayāt
b svasti haṃto tv ahaṃ yuddhe nihatajñātibāndhavaḥ
c svastiyuktāṃś ca kalyāṃś ca tan me priyam anuttamam
a mā bhavanto 'nutapyantāṃ sauhṛdān nidhanena me
c yadi vedāḥ pramāṇaṃ vo jitā lokā mayākṣayāḥ
a manyamānaḥ prabhāvaṃ ca kṛṣṇasyāmitatejasaḥ
c tena na cyāvitaś cāhaṃ kṣatradharmāt svanuṣṭhitāt
a sa mayā samanuprāpto nāsmi śocyaḥ kathaṃ cana
b tathā tu dṛṣṭvā rājendra vartate vijayo mama
c kṛtaṃ bhavadbhiḥ sadṛśam anurūpam ivātmanaḥ
e yatitaṃ vijaye nityaṃ daivaṃ tu duratikramam
a etāvad uktvā vacanaṃ bāṣpavyākulalocanaḥ
c tūṣṇīṃ babhūva rājendra rujāsau vihvalo bhṛśam
a tathā tu dṛṣṭvā rājānaṃ bāṣpaśokasamanvitam
c drauṇiḥ krodhena jajvāla yathā vahnir jagatkṣaye
a sa tu krodhasamāviṣṭaḥ pāṇau pāṇiṃ nipīḍya ca
c bāṣpavihvalayā vācā rājānam idam abravīt
a pitā me nihataḥ kṣudraiḥ sunṛśaṃsena karmaṇā
c na tathā tena tapyāmi yathā rājaṃs tvayādya vai
a śṛṇu cedaṃ vaco mahyaṃ satyena vadataḥ prabho
b anṛṇo 'haṃ bhaviṣyāmi tavādya nṛpasattama
b tava priyaṃ kariṣyāmi kṛtvā kāryam anuttamam
b īpsitaṃ manasā rājan yathecchasi tathā vada
c iṣṭāpūrtena dānena dharmeṇa sukṛtena ca
d śapeyaṃ rājaśārdūla pādābhyāṃ mama vai pituḥ
a adyāhaṃ sarvapāñcālān vāsudevasya paśyataḥ
a   sṛñjayāṃś caiva sarvaśaḥ
a sarvāṃś ca nṛpatīn rājan dhṛṣṭadyumnapurogamān
a sasainyān yudhiśeṣāṃś ca
c sarvopāyair hi neṣyāmi pretarājaniveśanam
d adya rātrau mahārāja nihaniṣyāmi pāṇḍavān
e anujñāṃ tu mahārāja bhavān me dātum arhati
a iti śrutvā tu vacanaṃ droṇaputrasya kauravaḥ
b tac chrutvā vacanaṃ drauṇer dhṛtarāṣṭra tavātmajaḥ
c manasaḥ prītijananaṃ kṛpaṃ vacanam abravīt
e ācārya śīghraṃ kalaśaṃ jalapūrṇaṃ samānaya
a sa tad vacanam ājñāya rājño brāhmaṇasattamaḥ
c kalaśaṃ pūrṇam ādāya rājño 'ntikam upāgamat
a tam abravīn mahārāja putras tava viśāṃ pate
c mamājñayā dvijaśreṣṭha droṇaputro 'bhiṣicyatām
e senāpatyena bhadraṃ te mama ced icchasi priyam
a rājño niyogād yoddhavyaṃ brāhmaṇena viśeṣataḥ
c vartatā kṣatradharmeṇa hy evaṃ dharmavido viduḥ
a rājñas tu vacanaṃ śrutvā kṛpaḥ śāradvatas tataḥ
c drauṇiṃ rājño niyogena senāpatye 'bhyaṣecayat
a so 'bhiṣikto mahārāja pariṣvajya nṛpottamam
c prayayau siṃhanādena diśaḥ sarvā vinādayan
a duryodhano 'pi rājendra śoṇitaughapariplutaḥ
c tāṃ niśāṃ pratipede 'tha sarvabhūtabhayāvahām
a apakramya tu te tūrṇaṃ tasmād āyodhanān nṛpa
c śokasaṃvignamanasaś cintādhyānaparābhavan
d kṛtavarmakṛpābhyāṃ ca aśvatthāme 'pi gacchati
d āste rājā cintayānas teṣām āgamanaṃ prati
d gadāparvaṇi rājendra samāpte 'bhīṣṭade nṛṇām
d brāhmaṇān bhojayet paścād vaktāraṃ ca supūjayet
